Zhang,J. Y. Zhang,J. Z. Zhang,Jianyu Zhang,L. M. Zhang,Lei Zhang,N. Zhang,P. Zhang,Q. Zhang,Q. Y. Zhang,R. Y. Zhang,S. H. Zhang,Shulei Zhang,X. M. Zhang,X. Y. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Y. T. Zhang,Y. H. Zhang,Y. P. Zhang,Z. D. Zhang,Z. H. Zhang,Z. L. Zhang,Z. L. Zhang,Z. X. Zhang,Z. Y. Zhang,Z. Y. Zhang,Z. Y. Zhang,Zh. Zh. Zhang,G. Zhao,J. Y. Zhao,J. Z. Zhao,L. Zhao,L. Zhao,M. G. Zhao,S. J. Zhao,Y. B. Zhao,Y. L. Zhao,Y. P. Zhao,Y. X. Zhao,Z. G. Zhao,A. Zhemchugov,B. Zheng,B. M. Zheng,J. P. Zheng,W. J. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次利用能量扫描方法测量了$e^{+}e^{-}\to K^{+}K^{-}$过程在$ψ(2S)$共振峰附近的截面，并提取了$ψ(2S)$共振强振幅与电磁振幅的相对相位$Φ$，获得了$ψ(2S)\to K^{+}K^{-}$分支比的两个解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在测量$e^{+}e^{-}\to K^{+}K^{-}$过程在$ψ(2S)$共振峰附近的截面，以提取粲偶素物理中的一个基本参数——$ψ(2S)$共振强振幅与电磁振幅的相对相位$Φ$。该测量对于理解$ψ(2S)$衰变中的干涉效应至关重要。

Method: 采用能量扫描方法（energy scan method），基于BESIII探测器在BEPCII上收集的495 pb$^{-1}$积分亮度$e^{+}e^{-}$对撞数据。通过分析截面线形（cross section line-shape），在假设$ψ(2S)$共振电磁振幅与连续谱相对相位为零的前提下，提取相对相位$Φ$。

Result: 观测到$ψ(2S)\to K^{+}K^{-}$分支比$\mathcal{B}$的两个解：相长干涉解$\mathcal{B}=(7.49\pm0.41)\times10^{-5}$、$Φ=(110.1\pm6.7)^\circ$，相消干涉解$\mathcal{B}=(10.94\pm0.48)\times10^{-5}$、$Φ=(-106.8\pm5.7)^\circ$。首次报告了$ψ(2S)$强形状因子和带电kaon能量依赖电磁形状因子。

Conclusion: 研究建立了$Φ$与$\mathcal{B}$之间的显著相关性，证明在$ψ(2S)$分支比测量中必须考虑干涉效应。该工作为粲偶素物理提供了重要参数，并首次报告了相关形状因子结果。

Abstract: We report the first measurement of the $e^{+}e^{-}\to K^{+}K^{-}$ cross sections around the $ψ(2S)$ resonance using the energy scan method. The analysis is based on $e^{+}e^{-}$ collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 495~pb$^{-1}$ collected with the BESIII detector at BEPCII. By analyzing the cross section line-shape, we extract the relative phase $Φ$ between the strong and electromagnetic amplitudes of the $ψ(2S)$ resonance, a fundamental parameter in charmonium physics, based on the assumption that the relative phase between the electromagnetic amplitude of the $ψ(2S)$ resonance and the continuum is zero. Two distinct solutions for the branching fraction $\mathcal{B}$ of $ψ(2S)\to K^{+}K^{-}$ are observed: a constructive interference solution with $\mathcal{B}=(7.49\pm0.41)\times10^{-5}$ and $Φ=(110.1 \pm6.7)^\circ$, and a destructive interference solution with $\mathcal{B}=(10.94\pm0.48)\times10^{-5}$ and $Φ=(-106.8\pm5.7)^\circ$. A significant correlation between $Φ$ and $\mathcal{B}$ is established, demonstrating that interference effects must be taken into account in the $ψ(2S)$ branching fraction measurements. Additionally, the first results for both the $ψ(2S)$ strong form factor, which characterizes the strong coupling between $ψ(2S)$ and $K^{+}K^{-}$, and the energy-dependent electromagnetic form factor of the charged kaon in this energy region are here reported.

</details>


<div id='physics.chem-ph'></div>

# physics.chem-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Quantum coherence governs macroscopic polymorphism in organic semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28834)
*Hai Wang,Tianhong Huang,Jiawei Chang*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了有机半导体中晶体多晶型（polymorphism）的量子调控机制，发现室温下分子物质波的量子相干性（quantum coherence）和多体量子纠缠（multipartite quantum entanglement）是决定铜酞菁（CuPc）晶体组装的关键因素，并基于此设计出新型多晶型ω-CuPc。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机半导体中的晶体多晶型（crystal polymorphism）从根本上决定光电器件性能，但经典热力学模型无法解释相选择（phase selection）的微观起源，特别是无法解释在相同热力学参数下不同反应器规模中出现的多晶型差异这一长期异常现象。

Method: 研究建立了耗散结构场诱导多体纠缠（Dissipative structure field-Induced Multipartite Entanglement, DIME）框架，该框架整合了环境黑体辐射（ambient blackbody radiation）、分子德布罗意波长（molecular de Broglie wavelengths）和前线轨道方向性（frontier orbital directionality）来模拟场驱动的量子纠缠（field-driven quantum entanglement）。通过常压有机气相沉积（atmospheric-pressure organic vapor phase deposition, OVPD）技术，利用DIME框架调控环境退相干（environmental decoherence）。

Result: 研究发现室温下极弱的环境退相干保持了分子物质波（molecular matter waves）的相干性，实现了超长（>1 cm）单晶η-CuPc纳米线的自组装。通过操纵环境退相干，理性设计OVPD反应器成功合成了先前未知的多晶型ω-CuPc。

Conclusion: 多体量子纠缠（multipartite quantum entanglement）是有机晶体组装的决定性调控因子，这为有机半导体多晶型工程开辟了一条确定性的量子水平（quantum-level）路径。

Abstract: The wave-particle duality of massive macromolecules -- such as the fullerene C$_{60}$ -- is a well-established quantum phenomenon. However, whether the quantum behavior of large organic molecules actively dictates the macroscopic structure and function of synthetic materials remains unknown. In organic semiconductors, crystal polymorphism fundamentally determines optoelectronic performance, yet classical thermodynamic models consistently fail to resolve the microscopic origins of phase selection. This includes the long-standing anomaly of divergent polymorph formation under identical thermodynamic parameters across different reactor scales. Here we show that the polymorphism of copper phthalocyanine (CuPc, 576 Da) -- a planar macromolecule comparable in mass to C$_{60}$ -- is governed by quantum coherence during atmospheric-pressure organic vapor phase deposition (OVPD). We establish the Dissipative structure field-Induced Multipartite Entanglement (DIME) framework, which integrates ambient blackbody radiation, molecular de Broglie wavelengths, and frontier orbital directionality to model field-driven quantum entanglement. We demonstrate that exceptionally weak environmental decoherence at room temperature preserves the coherence of molecular matter waves, enabling the self-assembly of ultralong ($>1$ cm) single-crystalline $η$-CuPc nanowires. By leveraging the DIME framework to manipulate environmental decoherence, we rationally designed an OVPD reactor to synthesize a previously undiscovered polymorph, designated $ω$-CuPc. Our findings reveal that multipartite quantum entanglement acts as the decisive regulator of organic crystal assembly, opening a deterministic, quantum-level pathway for engineering organic semiconductor polymorphism.

</details>


### [3] [Short-lived memory in multidimensional spectra encodes full signal evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29814)
*Thomas Sayer,Ethan H. Fink,Zachary R. Wiethorn,Devin R. Williams,Anthony J. Dominic,Luke Guerrieri,Yi Ji,Veronica Policht,Jennifer Ogilvie,Gabriela Schlau-Cohen,Amber Krummel,Andrés Montoya-Castillo*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种名为"谱广义主方程（spectral GME）"的新技术，能够利用短等待时间的二维光谱来预测任意等待时间下的完整二维光谱演化，大幅降低实验成本并提高时间分辨率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前超快多维光谱技术面临复杂装置、长平均时间等限制，导致其应用局限于少数样品的详细机理研究，无法广泛表征分子系统或优化材料性能。特别是二维光谱的统计噪声收敛成本随等待时间增加呈指数增长，且长时间激光照射会增加样品降解风险。

Method: 本研究开发了谱广义主方程（spectral generalized master equation, GME）技术，该方法能够利用短等待时间的二维光谱数据，通过理论框架预测任意等待时间下的完整光谱演化。该方法在理论生成和实验测量的二维电子光谱及二维红外光谱上进行了验证。

Result: 谱广义主方程技术将实验成本降低了多个数量级，同时能够准确去除统计噪声，减少时间平均需求，并规避了随等待时间增加而增长的收敛成本。该方法提供了高时间分辨率的光谱演化预测能力。

Conclusion: 这一进展有望使研究者能够研究那些对当前多维光谱技术过于脆弱的系统，并加速基于二维光谱的显微技术发展，从而在异质环境中提供具有空间分辨率的高分辨率激发动力学信息。

Abstract: Ultrafast multidimensional spectroscopies are powerful tools that can access charge and energy flow in complex materials, shifting chemical kinetics, and even many-body interactions in correlated matter. However, current implementations typically involve complex apparatuses and long averaging times. As a result, these methods have been limited to detailed mechanistic investigations of a few samples, precluding the broad characterization of molecular systems and/or the optimization of material ones. For example, converging the statistical noise in 2D spectra becomes exponentially expensive with increasing waiting times, and extended laser exposure heightens the probability of sample degradation. We address this fundamental challenge by developing a new technique, the spectral generalized master equation (GME), that enables one to employ short-waiting time 2D spectra to determine the full evolution of 2D spectra over arbitrary waiting times with high temporal resolution. In addition to reducing the cost of experiments by multiple orders of magnitude, our approach accurately removes statistical noise, reducing the need for time averaging, while circumventing the increasing convergence costs with longer waiting times. We provide a rigorous theoretical footing for the spectral GME and demonstrate its applicability on theoretically generated and experimentally measured 2D electronic and 2D infrared spectra. We anticipate that this advance has the potential to enable the investigation of systems that are too delicate for study with current multidimensional spectroscopies and accelerate the progress of 2D spectroscopy-based microscopies that can offer highly resolved excitation dynamics with spatial resolution over heterogeneous environments.

</details>


### [4] [Gap edge eigenpairs from density matrix purification using moments of the Dirac distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29849)
*Lionel Alexandre Truflandier*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种基于准纯化单粒子密度矩阵（quasi-purified one-particle density matrix）的简单方法，用于解析电子本征谱带隙边缘的本征态，通过幂窄化迭代（power narrowing iterations）实现高效计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要一种简单有效的方法来解析电子本征谱带隙边缘的本征态，仅使用准纯化单粒子密度矩阵作为输入，避免复杂的计算过程。

Method: 方法基于将占据数方差（occupation number variance）分解为粒子矩和空穴矩（particle and hole moment），通过幂窄化迭代纯化这些矩，从而分离出最高占据和最低未占据单态投影算子（higher occupied and lower unoccupied single state projectors），获得相应的本征对。

Result: 该方法在选定分子的基准测试中表现出鲁棒性和高效性，在最坏情况下仅需约十几次矩阵-矩阵乘法；当遇到简并时，幂窄化仍能提供相关的混合态；讨论了使用Lanczos子空间方法降低计算成本的可能性。

Conclusion: 幂窄化算法的极低计算复杂度使其易于在已具备费米算符展开或密度矩阵纯化功能的电子结构代码或库中实现，为解析带隙边缘本征态提供了简洁有效的解决方案。

Abstract: In this work, we propose a simple method to resolve the eigenstates located at the band gap edges of an electronic eigenspectrum using only the quasi-purified one-particle density matrix as input. The theoretical framework relies on the decomposition of the occupation number variance into a particle and hole moment. These moments, when purified using power narrowing iterations, allow to isolate the higher occupied and lower unoccupied single state projectors, giving readily access to the corresponding eigenpairs. We demonstrate that when degeneracy is encountered, power narrowing remains able to deliver relevant mixed states. From a benchmark of selected molecules, we show that the method is robust and efficient since it requires no more that a dozen of matrix-matrix multiplications at worst. The possibility of reducing the computational cost using Lanczos subspace approach is discussed. The very low algorithmic complexity of power narrowing makes it very easy to implement in electronic structure codes or libraries already featuring Fermi operator expansion or density matrix purifications.

</details>

### [5] [Enhanced nanocomposite susceptibility by field-alignment of superparamagnetic particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29983)
*Mathias Zambach,Miriam Varón,Thomas Veile,Matti Knaapila,László Almásy,Tomás S. Plivelic,Christer Johansson,Ziwei Ouyang,Marco Beleggia,Cathrine Frandsen*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过磁场对齐纳米颗粒，显著提高了纳米复合材料的磁化率（从21提升至50），并降低了磁损耗，为高频电感器核心材料提供了有前景的候选方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绝缘磁性单畴颗粒纳米复合材料（nanocomposites）作为高频、无涡流软磁材料具有潜力，但通常面临磁化率低（<20）的问题。颗粒对齐（particle alignment）被提出可提高磁化率并降低磁损耗，但缺乏实验验证。

Method: 研究采用含3-57 vol%磁场对齐（field-aligned）的11±3 nm磁赤铁矿（maghemite）颗粒的聚乙烯基体纳米复合材料。通过均匀静态对齐场（alignment field）在复合材料干燥过程中对齐颗粒，利用小角散射（small-angle scattering）排除颗粒聚集，并通过振动样品磁强计（vibrating sample magnetometry）、交流磁化率（AC-susceptibility）和高频磁滞测量（high-frequency hysteresis measurements）从直流至922 kHz研究对齐场强度和颗粒浓度对磁化率和磁滞损耗的影响。

Result: 纳米复合材料磁化率随颗粒分数超线性增加，源于弱颗粒相互作用（weak particle interactions）。颗粒对齐使57 vol%样品的磁化率从21提升至50。磁损耗在颗粒对齐后降低，测量得到的50磁化率是纳米复合材料中最高值之一。测量结果可通过包含平均场相互作用效应（mean-field interaction effects）和部分颗粒对齐的方向依赖德拜模型（directional dependent Debye-models）组合进行建模。

Conclusion: 颗粒对齐与相互作用的协同效应使纳米复合材料获得高于预期的磁化率。使用良好分散的单畴超顺磁纳米颗粒（single-domain superparamagnetic nanoparticles）进行磁性对齐可降低磁损耗，使其成为电力电子（power electronics）应用中相关的高频电感器核心材料候选方案。

Abstract: Nanocomposites comprised of insulated magnetic single-domain particles are promising candidates for high-frequency, eddy current free, soft magnetic materials, but tend to suffer from low magnetic susceptibility ($<20$). Particle alignment has been proposed to increase nanocomposite susceptibility and reduce magnetic losses but experimental verification has been lacking. Here, magnetic nanocomposites containing 3-57 vol\% field-aligned 11$\pm$3 nm maghemite particles in a poly-vinyl matrix were investigated for potential use as high-frequency inductor core materials. The particles were aligned by a homogenous static alignment field during nanocomposite drying, fixating the particle orientation. Particle aggregation was disproved by small-angle scattering. The dependence of the alignment field strength and particle concentration on the nanocomposite's susceptibility and hysteresis losses were investigated from DC up to 922 kHz by vibrating sample magnetometry, AC-susceptibility and high-frequency hysteresis measurements. Nanocomposite susceptibility increased super-linearly with particle fraction due to weak particle interactions. Alignment of the particles increased the nanocomposite susceptibility from 21 to 50 for samples with a particle content of 57 vol\%. Hence, the synergy between particle alignment and interaction allows for a higher than expected susceptibility of nanocomposites. The results show that magnetically aligning particles in a nanocomposite reduces magnetic losses when using well-dispersed single-domain superparamagnetic nanoparticles. Measured nanocomposite susceptibility could be modelled by a combination of directional dependent Debye-models including mean-field interaction effects and partial particle alignment. Measured susceptibility of 50 is among the highest obtained for nanocomposites, making it a relevant candidate for applications in power electronics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微观分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟方法，研究接触侧向粒子库的二元流体混合物系统。通过在不同粒子库中施加不同粒子浓度，使系统维持在受控非平衡条件下。

Conclusion: 分子动力学模拟为先前随机分析的理论预测提供了有力验证，确认了二元流体混合物在非平衡条件下的时间可逆性这一意外性质。

In the absence of relevant experimental evidence, we employ microscopic molecular dynamics simulations to assess the validity of this surprising result. Remarkably, the simulation results unambiguously confirm the prediction of the stochastic analysis.

### [7] [Non-Hermitian Causal Memory Generates Observable Temporal Correlations Invisible to Spectral Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29035)
*Mario J. Pinheiro*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文发现了一类新的非厄米因果过程，能产生传统谱方法无法检测的显著时间相关性。通过严格因果记忆核的生成模型，揭示了时间不对称随机过程在特征尺度上产生尖锐转变，这些转变在相似性空间中表现为局域结构，但在功率谱中无迹可寻。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统谱分析方法对非厄米（non-Hermitian）、非平稳过程的因果记忆效应存在根本性局限。研究旨在识别传统谱方法无法检测的时间相关性，为开放量子系统中的因果记忆提供实验可检验的特征。

Method: 采用具有严格因果记忆核（strictly causal memory kernel）的生成模型，分析时间不对称随机过程（time-asymmetric stochastic processes）。通过高精度计数实验验证模型预测，包括不对称转变轮廓和方向依赖的不对称参数。

Result: 模型预测的不对称转变轮廓符合$A(θ)=A_0\cos(θ+δ)$形式，与高精度计数实验达到定量一致（$χ^2/\mathrm{dof}=0.50$, $p=0.86$）。实验显示出极高显著性（$p<10^{-15}$），证实了相似性空间中的局域结构在功率谱中无迹可寻的现象。

Conclusion: 研究确立了谱分析对非厄米、非平稳过程的根本性局限，为开放量子系统中的因果记忆提供了实验可检验的特征。这些发现揭示了传统谱方法无法检测的新型时间相关性模式。

Abstract: We identify a new class of non-Hermitian causal processes that produce statistically significant temporal correlations invisible to conventional spectral methods. Using a generative model with a strictly causal memory kernel, we demonstrate that time-asymmetric stochastic processes naturally yield sharp transitions at characteristic scales that appear as localized structures in similarity space but leave no trace in power spectra. The model predicts an asymmetric transition profile with orientation-dependent asymmetry parameter $A(θ)=A_0\cos(θ+δ)$ and achieves quantitative agreement ($χ^2/\mathrm{dof}=0.50$, $p=0.86$) with high-precision counting experiments exhibiting $p<10^{-15}$ significance. These results establish a fundamental limitation of spectral analysis for non-Hermitian, non-stationary processes and provide experimentally testable signatures of causal memory in open quantum systems.

### [8] [Longest weakly increasing subsequences of discrete random walks on the integers with heavy tailed distribution of increments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29047)
*José Ricardo G. Mendonça,Marcelo V. Freire*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了具有重尾增量分布的随机游走中弱最长递增子序列（weak LIS）长度的渐近行为，发现当增量方差有限时平均长度按√n log n缩放，方差无限时按n^θ缩放（θ>0.5），且分布主体可由对数正态模型良好近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有重尾增量分布的随机游走中弱最长递增子序列（weak LIS）长度的渐近行为，特别是当增量分布具有零均值、对称重尾质量分布时，该分布与参数α>0相关。

Method: 研究方法包括探索性拟合、加权非线性最小二乘法和ANOVA模型比较，分析样本平均长度⟨L_n⟩的缩放行为，并对L_n分布进行诊断性检验。

Result: 研究结果显示：当增量分布方差有限（α>2）时，⟨L_n⟩ ∼ √n log n；当方差无限（α≤2）时，⟨L_n⟩ ∼ n^θ（θ>0.5）。分布诊断表明L_n分布主体可由对数正态模型良好近似，但尾部存在系统性偏差。

Conclusion: 结论证实并扩展了先前关于其他类型重尾随机游走LIS的结果，并提出了关于L_n分布是否可由对数正态分布有效描述的猜想。

Abstract: We investigate the behavior of the length of the longest weakly increasing subsequences (weak LIS) of $n$-step random walks with nonzero integer increments $k = \pm 1, \pm 2, \dots$ given by a zero-mean, symmetric heavy tailed mass distribution proportional to $|k|^{-1-α}$ for several values of the real parameter $α> 0$ together with that of the simple random walk ($k=\pm 1$), to which the $n$-step heavy tailed random walks tends when $α> (1+o(1))\log_{2}{n}$.
  By means of exploratory fits, weighted nonlinear least squares, and ANOVA model comparison, we found that the sample average length $\langle{L_{n}}\rangle$ scales like $\langle{L_{n}}\rangle \sim \sqrt{n}\log{n}$ when the distribution of increments has finite variance ($α> 2$) and $\langle{L_{n}}\rangle \sim n^θ$ with a varying exponent $θ> 0.5$ when the variance is infinite ($α\leq 2$). Distributional diagnostics indicate that the bulk of the $L_{n}$ distribution is very well-approximated by a lognormal model, though systematic deviations are observed in the tails.
  Our results corroborate and expand upon previous results for the LIS of other types of heavy-tailed random walks and raise a conjecture as to whether the distribution of $L_{n}$ is given, or can be effectively described, by a lognormal distribution.

### [9] [How much of persistent homology is topology? A quantitative decomposition for spin model phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29072)
*Matthew Loftus*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究量化分析了点云持久同调（PH）在检测经典自旋模型相变时，信号中真正拓扑成分的比例。通过引入密度匹配的洗牌零模型，发现H_0统计量主要（94-100%）由密度驱动，而H_1统计量则包含显著的拓扑成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 点云持久同调（point-cloud persistent homology）已被广泛应用于检测经典自旋模型的相变，但先前研究未明确区分信号中的密度驱动成分与真正拓扑成分。本研究旨在量化分析持久同调信号中真正拓扑贡献的比例。

Method: 引入f_topo定量分解方法，通过比较真实自旋构型与密度匹配的洗牌零模型（density-matched shuffled null models），分离持久同调统计量中的密度驱动贡献和拓扑贡献。在2D Ising模型（系统尺寸L=16-128，十个温度）和Potts模型（q=3,5）上进行验证。

Result: H_0统计量（总持久性、持久熵、特征计数）94-100%为密度驱动（f_topo < 0.07），仅密度信息即可检测相变。H_1统计量则包含部分拓扑成分：拓扑分数随系统尺寸增长（δ(TP_H1) ~ L^0.53），并遵循有限尺寸标度塌缩。最长持久性条带具有强拓扑性（f_topo > 1）并与关联长度标度相关。

Conclusion: 建议相变检测的拓扑数据分析（TDA）社区采用洗牌零模型作为标准实践，并在寻求真正拓扑信息时使用H_1而非H_0统计量。尺度分辨分析显示拓扑超额随系统尺寸增大从大尺度特征向小尺度特征转移。

Abstract: Point-cloud persistent homology (PH) -- computing alpha or Rips complexes on spin-position point clouds -- has been widely applied to detect phase transitions in classical spin models since Donato et al. (2016), with subsequent studies attributing the detection to the topological content of the persistence diagram. We ask a simple question that has not been posed: what fraction of the PH signal is genuinely topological? We introduce f_topo, a quantitative decomposition that separates the density-driven and topological contributions to any PH statistic by comparing real spin configurations against density-matched shuffled null models. Across the 2D Ising model (system sizes L = 16-128, ten temperatures) and Potts models (q = 3, 5), we find that H_0 statistics -- total persistence, persistence entropy, feature count -- are 94-100% density-driven (f_topo < 0.07). The density-matched shuffled null detects T_c at the identical location and with comparable peak height as real configurations, showing that density alone is sufficient for phase transition detection. However, H_1 statistics are partially topological: the topological fraction grows with system size as delta(TP_{H_1}) ~ L^{0.53} and follows a finite-size scaling collapse delta(T, L) = L^{0.53} g(tL^{1/nu}) with collapse quality CV = 0.27. The longest persistence bar is strongly topological (f_topo > 1) and scales with the correlation length. A scale-resolved analysis reveals that the topological excess shifts from large-scale to small-scale features as L increases. We propose that the TDA-for-phase-transitions community adopt shuffled null models as standard practice, and that H_1 rather than H_0 statistics be used when genuine topological information is sought.

</details>


### [10] [The geometric origin of criticality: a universal mechanism in mean-field rotor Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29074)
*Loris Di Cairano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于恒定能量壳（constant-energy shell）几何结构的平均场转子哈密顿量临界性普适判据，将相变重构为能量壳固有的几何不稳定性现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统相变表征主要依赖热力学奇异性，本文旨在建立一种基于能量壳几何重组的普适临界性判据，揭示相变背后的几何不稳定性本质。

Method: 针对有限维三角平均场相互作用（trigonometric mean-field interactions）的广泛类别，利用魏因加滕算子（Weingarten operator）的迹展开，构建能量依赖的二次型，通过其本征模识别系统的几何不稳定通道。

Result: 临界性与相应曲率系数的消失相关联，为相变时的不稳定模式提供了直接的几何选择原理。该框架在所考虑的类别内具有几何普适性，仅依赖于有限的集体耦合参数。

Conclusion: 平均场系统中的相变可重构为能量壳固有的几何不稳定性现象，临界行为可理解为由底层能量壳几何结构的集体重组所触发的几何重组。

Abstract: We introduce a universal criterion for criticality in mean-field rotor Hamiltonians based on the geometric structure of the constant-energy shell. Rather than characterizing the onset of a phase transition through the conventional thermodynamic singularities alone, we show that the relevant information is already encoded in the way the geometry of the shell reorganizes along distinguished collective directions.
  For a broad class of finite-dimensional trigonometric mean-field interactions, the trace of the Weingarten operator (representing the principal curvatures) admits a universal collective expansion in terms of the order-parameter amplitudes. This expansion defines an energy-dependent quadratic form whose eigenmodes identify the geometrically unstable channels of the system. Criticality is then associated with the vanishing of the corresponding curvature coefficients, yielding a direct geometric selection principle for the modes that become unstable at the transition.
  In this way, the phase transition in mean-field systems (usually of first- or second-order) is reformulated as a geometric instability phenomenon intrinsic to the microcanonical energy shell. The resulting framework is geometrically universal within the class considered, independent of model-specific details except for a finite set of collective couplings. Moreover, our approach recovers the known critical channels in standard mean-field rotor models while extending naturally to multimode and spectrally coupled cases. These results support a view in which critical behavior can be understood as reorganizations of energy-shell geometry triggered by a collective restructuring of the underlying energy-shell geometry.

</details>


### [11] [Mean first passage times of velocity jump processes in higher dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29241)
*Maria R. D'Orsogna,Alan E. Lindsay,Thomas Hillen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个通用框架，用于估计固定速度速度跳跃过程（velocity jump processes）的平均首次通过时间（MFPT）和生存概率的高阶矩，涵盖了从强对齐到完全角度各向异性的可能重定向情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 首次通过现象（first passage phenomena）在物理、生物和金融领域普遍存在，但速度跳跃过程在更高维度下的首次通过特性研究不足，特别是在存在方向偏置（directional bias）的情况下。许多随机过程更适合用速度跳跃过程来描述，其特征是持续运动被随机的速度变化打断。

Method: 提出了一个通用框架来估计固定速度速度跳跃过程的平均首次通过时间和生存概率高阶矩。对于低克努森数（low Knudsen numbers）情况，推导了平均首次通过时间的通用形式，其中两个偏置函数（bias functions）编码了广泛的角分布类别。在窄捕获极限（narrow capture limit）下，分析了方向持续性（directional persistence）引起的反常标度行为。

Result: 获得了平均首次通过时间的通用形式，能够编码包括冯·米塞斯-费舍尔分布（von Mises-Fisher）、环绕柯西分布（wrapped Cauchy）和椭圆族（elliptical families）在内的广泛角分布类别。在窄捕获极限下，方向持续性诱导了反常标度，包括平均首次通过时间保持有限而标准扩散预测发散的区域。获得了能够准确再现首次通过统计的朗之万表示（Langevin representation）。

Conclusion: 该框架为速度跳跃过程的首次通过特性提供了全面的理论分析，揭示了方向持续性在窄捕获极限下引起的反常行为。解析预测通过数值模拟得到了验证，表明朗之万表示能够准确再现首次通过统计。

Abstract: First passage phenomena arise across physics, biology, and finance when stochastic processes first reach a threshold, triggering downstream events. Examples include the irreversible exit from a domain, a biochemical reaction, a financial selloff. While typical formulations involve diffusive motion, many stochastic processes are better described as velocity jump processes, characterized by persistent motion interrupted by stochastic velocity changes. Despite their ubiquity, first-passage properties of velocity jump processes remain underdeveloped in higher dimensions, especially under directional bias. We present a general framework to estimate the mean first passage time (MFPT) and higher moments of the survival probability for fixed-speed velocity jump processes where possible reorientations range from strong alignment to full angular anisotropy. For low Knudsen numbers, when the mean free path is small compared to the distance to the target, we derive a universal form for the MFPT in which two bias functions encode broad classes of angular distributions, including von Mises-Fisher, wrapped Cauchy, and elliptical families. In the narrow capture limit of a vanishingly small target, directional persistence induces anomalous scaling, including regimes where the MFPT remains finite whereas standard diffusion would predict divergence. Finally, we obtain a Langevin representation that accurately reproduces first-passage statistics. Analytical predictions are confirmed by numerical simulations.

</details>


### [12] [Bethe Ansatz with a Large Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29932)
*Balázs Pozsgay,István Vona*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索大型语言模型（Large Language Model, LLM）在数学物理特定计算任务中的能力，特别是求解可积自旋链模型的坐标Bethe Ansatz解。研究者选择了三个未发表解的可积哈密顿量，其中两个是全新的模型。

Method: 研究方法采用ChatGPT 5.2 Pro和5.4 Pro进行半自主计算任务。LLM负责求解坐标Bethe Ansatz解，研究人员发现错误后进行人工修正。结果通过精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和作者验证进行检验。

Result: LLM在所有案例中半自主地完成了任务，过程中出现少量错误但经人工修正。第二个模型明显破坏左右不变性但保持PT对称性，其解在广义流体动力学中可能有应用价值。第三个模型通过特殊形式的嵌套Bethe Ansatz求解，具有独特的自由费米子结构且缺乏U(1)不变性。

Conclusion: 研究表明LLM能够有效辅助数学物理计算任务，成功求解了包括新模型在内的可积自旋链Bethe Ansatz解。LLM发现的第三个模型的独特结构具有研究价值，展示了AI在理论物理研究中的潜力。

Abstract: We explore the capability of a Large Language Model (LLM) to perform specific computations in mathematical physics: the task is to compute the coordinate Bethe Ansatz solution of selected integrable spin chain models. We select three integrable Hamiltonians for which the solutions were unpublished; two of the Hamiltonians are actually new. We observed that the LLM semi-autonomously solved the task in all cases, with a few mistakes along the way. These were corrected after the human researchers spotted them. The results of the LLM were checked against exact diagonalization (performed by separate programs), and the derivations were also checked by the authors. The Bethe Ansatz solutions are interesting in themselves. Our second model manifestly breaks left-right invariance, but it is PT-symmetric, therefore its solution could be interesting for applications in Generalized Hydrodynamics. And our third model is solved by a special form of the nested Bethe Ansatz, where the model is interacting, but the nesting level has a free fermionic structure lacking $U(1)$-invariance. This structure appears to be unique and it was found by the LLM. We used ChatGPT 5.2 Pro and 5.4 Pro by OpenAI.

### [13] [Force Geometry and Irreversibility in Nonequilibrium Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29416)
*Erez Aghion,Swetamber Das*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出力几何（force geometry）作为非平衡热力学的组织原则，通过力对齐（force alignment）概念解释空间耗散异质性，建立了熵产生与驱动力-熵梯度相对取向的几何关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验观察到光阱系统中耗散的空间异质性常与局域位置涨落反相关，这暴露了标量随机热力学描述的结构性缺陷。传统标量框架虽能通过流和熵产生率量化耗散，但无法揭示塑造空间耗散模式的底层矢量力几何。

Method: 研究通过识别力几何作为非平衡热力学的组织原则，引入力对齐作为不可逆性的几何决定因素。形式化地通过时间依赖的力相关系数量化驱动力与熵梯度之间的相对取向，建立了熵产生的瞬时几何下界。

Result: 熵产生不仅取决于力的大小，还取决于确定性驱动力与熵梯度之间的相对取向，仅在精确反对齐且幅度匹配时消失。在过阻尼动力学中，完美反对齐定义了热力学停滞点，此时净输运消失且熵产生下界达到饱和。

Conclusion: 力几何视角为实验观测到的涨落-耗散反相关和非均匀耗散提供了结构性解释。研究构建了恒定拖曳和正弦驱动协议的几何控制图，将力几何定位为跨越活性生物系统、微流变学并自然扩展到欠阻尼动力学的不可逆性统一结构视角。

Abstract: Recent experiments have revealed heterogeneous dissipation in optically trapped systems, often anticorrelated with local positional fluctuations, exposing a structural gap in the scalar stochastic thermodynamic description. While the conventional scalar framework successfully quantifies dissipation through currents and entropy production rates, it does not reveal the underlying vectorial force geometry that shapes spatial dissipation patterns. Here, we bridge this gap by identifying force geometry as an organizing principle for nonequilibrium thermodynamics and introducing force alignment as a geometric determinant of irreversibility. We show that entropy production depends not only on force magnitudes but also on the relative orientation between deterministic driving forces and entropic gradients, vanishing only under exact anti-alignment with matched magnitudes. We formalize this geometric alignment through a time-dependent force-correlation coefficient, quantifying the relative orientation between the forces. This yields an instantaneous geometric lower bound on entropy production that remains valid even when force magnitudes are matched. For overdamped dynamics, perfect anti-alignment defines a thermodynamic stall where net transport vanishes and the lower bound on entropy production is saturated. This force-level perspective provides a structural explanation for the experimentally observed fluctuation-dissipation anticorrelation and nonuniform dissipation. We construct geometric control charts for both constant dragging and sinusoidal driving protocols, explicitly locating experimental operating points within this force-space representation. Together, these results position force geometry as a unifying structural perspective on irreversibility, spanning active biological systems, microrheology, and naturally extending to underdamped dynamics.

</details>

*Thomas Franosch*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在弥合物理学与数学文献之间的知识鸿沟。尽管相关函数的表征定理（如Bochner定理）在数学领域已确立，但这些重要工具未在物理学家中广泛认知，部分原因是它们超出了标准课程范畴。

Method: 采用双部分结构：第一部分以物理学家语言介绍（自）相关函数（(auto-)correlation functions）和线性响应函数（linear-response functions），重点阐述经典涨落耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem）；第二部分转向严格数学视角，陈述相关函数的关键结构特性并提供选择性推导。

Result: 论文系统介绍了相关函数和响应函数的数学表征理论，包括Bochner定理（Bochner's theorem）用于相关函数表征，以及Herglotz-Nevanlinna表示（Herglotz-Nevanlinna representations）用于响应函数表征，这些结果为物理应用提供了严格数学基础。

Conclusion: 论文强调相关函数在物理系统中的核心地位，并通过引入数学文献中的表征定理，为物理学家提供了理解和应用这些函数的更严格框架，最终回归到线性响应函数的一般表征结果讨论。

Abstract: In the first part of these short lecture notes, we will present an introduction on (auto-)correlation functions and linear-response functions in the language of a physicist. In particular, the fluctuation-dissipation theorem in classical physics is presented underlining the central role of correlation functions. The fundamental importance of (auto-)correlation functions raises the natural question on how they are characterized in general without referring to the concrete underlying dynamical laws. Perhaps unexpectedly -- despite being elegant and long established in the mathematical literature (Bochner's theorem for correlations; Herglotz-Nevanlinna representations for response) -- this answer is not widely appreciated in physics, partly because the requisite tools lie outside the standard curriculum.
  In the second part we adopt a more rigorous viewpoint: we state the key structural properties of correlation functions and provide selected derivations of these results. Finally, we return to linear response and discuss general characterization results for response functions.

### [15] [Thermalization in high-dimensional systems: the (weak) role of chaos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29614)
*Marco Baldovin,Marco Cattaneo,Dario Lucente,Paolo Muratore-Ginanneschi,Angelo Vulpiani*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了统计力学有效性的核心要素，认为大量自由度（degrees of freedom）和广延可观测量（extensive observables）的选择比动力学细节更为关键。通过研究可积（harmonic）与混沌（nonharmonic）振子链在非平衡条件下的热化（thermalization）行为，发现可积系统中热化与否取决于可观测量，而混沌系统中所有可观测量最终都会热化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于Fermi-Pasta-Ulam-Tsingou（FPUT）问题引发的关于统计力学与动力学性质（如混沌和遍历性（ergodicity））关系的长期探讨。尽管统计力学结果通常需要遍历性假设来严格证明，但许多迹象表明这些预测在缺乏严格遍历性的情况下依然成立。本研究旨在重新审视Khinchin的观点，即统计力学的有效性主要依赖于大量自由度和广延可观测量，而非动力学细节。

Method: 研究方法是将Khinchin关于平衡态宏观观测量典型性（typicality）的证明扩展到非平衡（non equilibrium）情境。具体通过研究谐波（可积）和非谐波（混沌）振子链在初始非平衡条件下的热化特性来实现。分析重点在于比较不同系统（可积vs混沌）中各种观测量的热化行为。

Result: 研究结果显示，在可积（integrable）系统中，热化（thermalization）是否发生取决于所选择的观测量。而在混沌（chaotic）系统中，所有观测量最终都会达到热化，尽管其弛豫时间尺度（relaxation timescale）可能超过观测时间。这一发现支持了统计力学预测的有效性可能不严格依赖于遍历性假设的观点。

Conclusion: 结论指出，统计力学的有效性可能更依赖于系统拥有大量自由度和选择适当的广延可观测量，而非动力学的具体细节（如是否严格满足遍历性）。该研究将Khinchin的平衡态典型性观点成功扩展到非平衡情境，为理解非平衡统计力学提供了新视角。

Abstract: In their seminal work, Fermi, Pasta, Ulam and Tsingou explored the connection between statistical mechanics and dynamical properties, such as chaos and ergodicity. Even today, seventy years later, the topic is not fully understood: while most results of statistical mechanics require the ergodic hypothesis to be rigorously proved, there are many indications that these predictions, both in and out of equilibrium, hold even in the absence of a rigorous form of ergodicity.
  Motivated by the above considerations, in this work we reconsider the point of view that the relevant ingredients for the validity of statistical mechanics are the large number of degrees of freedom and the choice of extensive observables, while the details of the dynamics do not play an essential role. This is the idea behind Khinchin's famous proof of the typicality of macroscopic observables at equilibrium. We extend this perspective to the context of non equilibrium, by investigating the thermalization properties of both harmonic (integrable) and nonharmonic (chaotic) oscillator chains initially prepared in out-of-equilibrium conditions. In integrable systems, thermalization occurs, or not, depending on the observable. In the chaotic regime, instead, thermalization is reached by any observable, although the relaxation timescale might be larger than the observation time.

</details>

Method: 提出了一种新颖的耦合方案（coupling scheme），通过根据振子频率失谐（frequency detuning）缩放相互作用强度来增强同步。该方法允许通过改变单个参数来调控系统的临界行为。

Result: 该耦合方案显著增强了网络同步，并诱导了临界性变化（change in criticality），将系统从连续相变（continuous phase transition）驱动到爆炸性相变（explosive transition）。

Conclusion: 这项工作为工程网络中的高效同步提供了一条通用路径，并为Kuramoto模型的临界行为提供了新的见解。频率依赖的耦合策略是优化同步性能的有效方法。

Abstract: We introduce a novel coupling scheme for maximizing the synchronization of Kuramoto oscillator networks under a fixed coupling budget. We show that by scaling the interaction strength between oscillators according to their frequency detuning, synchronization is enhanced. The coupling scheme induces a change in criticality, driving the system from a continuous phase transition to an explosive transition by changing a single parameter. Our work offers a general route to efficient synchronization in engineered networks and provides insight into the critical behavior of the Kuramoto model.

*Emanuele Panizon*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究解析求解了在昂贵测量条件下通过光镊驱动过阻尼粒子的有限时间控制问题，建立了介观信息引擎的最优测量与驱动协议，并推导了热涨落可提取的最大功率物理界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于解决在昂贵测量条件下驱动过阻尼粒子的有限时间控制问题，将介观信息引擎（mesoscopic information engine）置于部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）框架中进行分析。

Method: 采用部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）框架，利用线性二次高斯（LQG）动力学将最优测量和驱动协议简化为一维代数Riccati递推关系，从而推导出陷阱位置的最优反馈控制律。

Result: 研究结果包括：推导出陷阱位置的最优反馈控制律，在连续时间开环极限下恢复了Schmiedl-Seiferd驱动协议；绘制了引擎的操作相空间，推导了热涨落可提取最大功率的显式物理界限；发现了截止时间诱导的盲视现象（deadline-induced blindness）。

Conclusion: 该研究为介观信息引擎提供了完整的解析解决方案，建立了最优控制协议与物理界限，并将结果推广到可变精度传感器（variable-precision sensor）的情况。

Abstract: We analytically solve the finite-time control problem of driving an overdamped particle via an optical trap under costly measurement. By formulating this mesoscopic information engine within the Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) framework, we demonstrate that the underlying Linear-Quadratic-Gaussian (LQG) dynamics reduce the optimal measurement and driving protocols to a one-dimensional algebraic Riccati recurrence. From this reduction, we derive the optimal feedback control law for the trap placement, which recovers the discontinuous Schmiedl-Seifert driving protocol in the continuous-time, open-loop limit. We map the operational phase space of the engine, deriving explicit physical bounds on the maximum power that can be extracted from thermal fluctuations. Taking the infinite-horizon limit, we find the exact periodic measurement schedules for the steady-state and derive the macroscopic velocity envelopes beyond which viscous drag forces the engine into a net-dissipative regime. We prove the emergence of deadline-induced blindness, a phenomenon where all measurement ceases as the deadline approaches regardless of their cost. Finally, we generalize the results to a variable-precision sensor.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于对环境的可求和混合假设，以及相关非选择性通道余环（non-selective channel cocycle）的退火迹范数遗忘性质。首先在动态平稳状态确定的退火律下建立中心极限定理，然后引入基于耦合的初始状态可容许性概念。

Abstract: We prove annealed central limit theorems for finite pattern counts in the measurement record of discrete-time quantum trajectories generated by repeated measurements in a disordered environment. Under summable mixing assumptions on the environment and an annealed trace-norm forgetting property for the associated non-selective channel cocycle, we first establish the CLT under the annealed law determined by the dynamically stationary state. This part applies to general disordered quantum instruments and, in particular, is not restricted to the perfect-measurement regime; it complements both the corresponding law of large numbers for disordered measurement records and the homogeneous central limit theorem. We then introduce a coupling-based notion of admissibility for initial states and show that the same Gaussian limit extends to every admissible initial law, with unchanged centering and asymptotic variance. In the perfect-measurement setting, we further identify a general condition ensuring admissibility for every initial state, and hence obtain a universal annealed central limit theorem. We also provide practical sufficient criteria for this condition and verify the assumptions across a broad family of examples, including disordered walk-type models generated by finite group actions

### [21] [The Contextual Modal Logic of a Wigner's Friend Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29028)
*Felipe Dilho Alves,João Carlos Alves Barata*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入量子系统的语境性（contextuality）概念，特别是基于Kochen-Specker定理，论证了Frauchiger-Renner思想实验中的所谓矛盾在逻辑上是不可达的，从而维护了量子力学的逻辑一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子力学自诞生以来一直受到逻辑审视，其与经典系统的根本差异常被认为暗示逻辑不一致性。Frauchiger-Renner思想实验是近期质疑量子力学逻辑完备性的典型例子，声称证明了量子力学的逻辑不一致性。

Method: 本文通过考虑量子系统的语境性（contextuality）属性，特别是基于Kochen-Specker定理的预测，重新分析Frauchiger-Renner思想实验的逻辑结构。

Result: 分析表明，当考虑量子系统的语境性时，Frauchiger和Renner提出的所谓矛盾在逻辑上变得不可达（logically inaccessible），从而消除了该思想实验对量子力学逻辑一致性的挑战。

Conclusion: 通过引入语境性概念，本文解决了Frauchiger-Renner思想实验提出的逻辑挑战，维护了量子力学的逻辑一致性，表明该思想实验中的矛盾实际上在量子力学的逻辑框架内是不可达的。

Abstract: Quantum mechanics has been subject to logical scrutiny since its inception. The behavior of quantum systems, which are fundamentally dissimilar from classical systems, often appears to point to a logical inconsistency in quantum mechanics, allegedly leading to contradictions in the prediction of experimental measurements--though such contradictions have never materialized. A recent example of this type of inquiry into the logical well-posedness of quantum mechanics is the Frauchiger-Renner Gedankenexperiment, which purports to demonstrate that quantum mechanics is logically inconsistent. In this article, we show that by considering the property of contextuality in quantum systems--as predicted by the Kochen-Specker theorem--the supposed contradiction proposed by Frauchiger and Renner becomes logically inaccessible.

</details>


### [22] [The Moyal cohomology of the spinning particle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29046)
*Ezra Getzler*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了在Batalin-Fradkin-Vilkovisky模型的微分分级辛超流形中，用Moyal括号（Moyal bracket）替代泊松括号（Poisson bracket）可以消除负度数中的虚假上同调类（spurious cohomology classes）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Felder和Kazhdan猜想经典Batalin-Vilkovisky形式主义中的局部上同调（local cohomology）在足够负的度数中消失，但这一假设被N=1自旋粒子（spinning particle）违反。Barnich-Grigoriev证明该上同调与相关Batalin-Fradkin-Vilkovisky模型的微分分级辛超流形（differential graded symplectic supermanifold）上函数代数的上同调同构，而后者在所有负度数中都是非平凡的。

Method: 通过在该辛超流形中用Moyal括号替代泊松括号，研究其对上同调结构的影响。这种方法旨在消除由传统泊松代数结构产生的虚假上同调类。

Result: 使用Moyal括号替代泊松括号成功消除了所有负度数中的虚假上同调类，从而解决了Felder-Kazhdan猜想在N=1自旋粒子情况下的违反问题。

Conclusion: 在Batalin-Fradkin-Vilkovisky模型的微分分级辛超流形框架下，Moyal括号的引入能够修正传统泊松代数结构产生的上同调异常，为处理量子场论中的规范固定问题提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: Felder and Kazhdan conjecture that the local cohomology in the classical Batalin-Vilkovisky formalism vanishes in sufficiently negative degrees. This hypothesis is violated by the $N=1$ spinning particle. By Barnich-Grigoriev, this cohomology is isomorphic to the cohomology of the algebra of functions on the differential graded symplectic supermanifold of the associated Batalin-Fradkin-Vilkovisky model. This cohomology is nontrivial in all negative degrees. We show in this article that replacement in this symplectic supermanifold of the Poisson bracket by the Moyal bracket eliminates these spurious cohomology classes.

</details>


### [23] [Derivative relations for determinants, Pfaffians and characteristic polynomials in random matrix theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29510)
*Gernot Akemann,Georg Angermann,Mario Kieburg,Adrian Padellaro*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了行列式或Pfaffian行列式与Vandermonde行列式之比的导数显式表达式。这些比值出现在Harish-Chandra-Itzykson-Zuber型一般群积分和随机矩阵理论中特征多项式乘积的期望值中。研究推广了先前关于随机矩阵特定系综中混合矩的结果，并展示了在复Ginibre系综和圆酉系综等实例中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在推导行列式或Pfaffian行列式与Vandermonde行列式之比的导数显式表达式。这类比值在数学物理中具有重要应用，例如出现在Harish-Chandra-Itzykson-Zuber型一般群积分和随机矩阵理论中特征多项式乘积的期望值计算中。

Method: 研究方法基于已知的有限矩阵尺寸下无导数期望值结果，这些结果以行列式或Pfaffian形式给出相应核（kernel）的表达式。从一阶导数开始，包含相应矩阵或核的Borel变换，证明了行列式一般比值的若干等价表达式。高阶导数通过包含这些导数行列式的分区求和表示，系数由组合表达式给出。

Result: 获得了最一般的结果：多变量行列式比值的混合高阶导数显式表达式。这推广了先前关于随机矩阵特定系综中混合矩的发现，特别是在黎曼ζ函数应用中相关的系综。研究结果在多个实例中得到应用，包括复Ginibre系综（complex Ginibre ensemble）和圆酉系综（circular unitary ensemble）。

Conclusion: 本文成功证明了行列式或Pfaffian行列式与Vandermonde行列式之比的导数显式表达式，推广了随机矩阵理论中相关结果。研究提供了适用于多变量混合高阶导数的通用表达式，并在具体系综中展示了应用价值，为数学物理中的相关计算提供了新工具。

Abstract: Explicit expressions are proven for derivatives of the ratio of a determinant or Pfaffian determinant and a Vandermonde determinant. Such ratios appear for example in general group integrals of Harish-Chandra--Itzykson--Zuber type and in expectation values of products of characteristic polynomials in random matrix theory. In the latter case we start from known results for general non-Hermitian and Hermitian ensembles for expectation values without derivatives, at finite matrix size. They are given in terms of the determinant or Pfaffian of the corresponding kernel, for unitary or orthogonal and symplectic ensembles, respectively. Several equivalent expressions are proven for general ratios of determinants, starting from first order derivatives containing the Borel transform of the corresponding matrix or kernel. Higher order derivatives are expressed as sums over partitions containing determinants of derivatives of these, with coefficients given in terms of combinatorial expressions. Our most general result is valid for mixed higher order derivatives of ratios of determinants in several variables. This generalises previous findings, e.g. for mixed moments in specific ensembles of random matrices, relevant in applications to the Riemann $ζ$-function. Applications of our results to several examples are presented, including the complex Ginibre ensemble and the circular unitary ensemble.

</details>


### [24] [Ground state energy of the Bose--Hubbard model with large coordination number with a polaron-type quantum de Finetti theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29562)
*Shahnaz Farhat,Denis Périce,Sören Petrat*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了在具有大配位数（large coordination number）的图上，玻色-哈伯德模型（Bose-Hubbard model）的基态能量收敛于平均场能量泛函（mean-field energy functional）的最小值。该结果通过发展一种新型的极化子型量子德菲内蒂定理（polaron-type quantum de Finetti theorem）实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究玻色-哈伯德模型在具有大且均匀配位数的图上的基态能量行为。在无限配位数极限下，期望证明基态能量收敛于平均场能量泛函的最小值，从而为大配位数情况下的相图提供定性正确的描述。

Method: 发展了新型的极化子型量子德菲内蒂定理，该定理适用于希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）为某个希尔伯特空间与玻色福克空间（bosonic Fock space）张量积的情况。将该定理应用于玻色-哈伯德模型，将其约化为极化子型模型后证明基态能量的收敛性。

Result: 在无限配位数极限下，证明了玻色-哈伯德模型的基态能量收敛于平均场能量泛函的最小值。该平均场描述处于强耦合区域（strong coupling regime），其中跳跃项（hopping term）通过对大量连接位点平均获得，而相互作用能（interaction energy）未被平均。

Conclusion: 所发展的极化子型量子德菲内蒂定理是现有量子德菲内蒂结果的更广泛有用的扩展。该平均场描述预期能为足够大配位数下的玻色-哈伯德模型相图提供定性正确的图像。

Abstract: We consider the ground state energy of the Bose--Hubbard model on a graph with large and homogeneous coordination number. In the limit of infinite coordination number, we prove convergence of the ground state energy to the minimizer of a mean-field energy functional. This functional is obtained by averaging the hopping term over the large number of connected sites, while the interaction energy is not averaged. Hence, the resulting mean-field description is in the strong coupling regime, and is expected to provide a qualitatively correct picture of the phase diagram of the Bose--Hubbard model for large enough coordination number. For our proof, we develop a new version of a de Finetti-type theorem, which we call the polaron-type quantum de Finetti theorem, and which we expect to be a more broadly useful extension of existing quantum de Finetti results. Our theorem covers the case where the Hilbert space is a tensor product of some Hilbert space with a bosonic Fock space. This theorem is applied to the convergence of the ground state energy of the Bose--Hubbard model after reducing it to a polaron-type model.

</details>


### [25] [Functional models and self-modeling property of minimal Dirac operators on the half-line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30001)
*M. I. Belishev,S. A. Simonov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 证明了半直线上最小狄拉克算子是自建模的，即任意酉等价副本在形状等价变换下唯一确定原算子。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用半直线上最小矩阵薛定谔算子（minimal matrix Schrödinger operator）的波函数模型（wave functional model）进行分析和证明。

Result: 证明了半直线上最小狄拉克算子是自建模的（self-modeling），即任意酉等价副本通过形状等价变换（shape equivalence）唯一确定原算子，该变换仅改变势能（potential）的模为1的常数因子。

Conclusion: 最小狄拉克算子具有自建模性质，其酉等价副本在形状等价变换下能唯一确定原算子，这一结果通过波函数模型方法得以证明。

Abstract: We prove that minimal Dirac operators on the half-line are self-modeling, which means that such an operator is determined by its arbitrary unitary copy uniquely up to a transformation (shape equivalence) which changes its potential by a constant factor of modulus one. This result is obtained using the wave functional model of the minimal matrix Schrödinger operator on the half-line.

### [26] [Disorder-Driven Enhancement of Coulomb Repulsion Governs The Superconducting Dome in Ionic-Liquid-Gated Quasi-2D Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28920)
*Giovanni Marini,Pierluigi Cudazzo,Matteo Calandra*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜酸盐、镍酸盐、扭曲双层石墨烯和过渡金属二硫化物等材料中普遍存在的超导转变温度随掺杂变化的穹顶相图常被视为非常规配对的标志。理解这些相图的物理机制并建立可靠的理论框架是当前的重要挑战。

Method: 研究采用结合无序效应的多体方法与第一性原理计算相结合的方法，分析离子液体门控的少层过渡金属二硫化物。重点考察冻结离子液体产生的无序离子势驱动系统接近安德森转变（Anderson transition）的机制。

Result: 无序驱动的库仑排斥增强显著抑制超导转变温度，自然形成超导穹顶相图。计算获得的相图和隧穿谱与实验结果在定量上高度吻合，验证了理论模型的可靠性。

Conclusion: 无序驱动的库仑排斥增强是离子液体门控准二维材料在高偏压下的基本特征，为理解这类材料中超导穹顶的形成机制提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: The superconducting dome in the Tc versus doping phase diagram, found in cuprates, nickelates, twisted bilayer graphene, and transition metal dichalcogenides, is often considered a signature of unconventional pairing. Identifying the underlying mechanisms of any of these phase diagrams and developing a reliable theoretical understanding of it remains a critical challenge. Here we demonstrate that, in ionic-liquid-gated quasi-2D materials, the disordered ionic potential from the frozen ionic liquid drives the system close to Anderson transition. In this regime, quenched charge fluctuations and reduced screening markedly enhance repulsive Coulomb interactions, suppressing Tc and naturally leading to the formation of a superconducting dome. By integrating a many-body approach including disorder with first-principles calculations, we obtain the phase diagrams and tunneling spectra of gated few-layers transition metal dichalchogenides in robust quantitative agreement with experiments. Our findings establish that disorder-driven enhancement of Coulomb repulsion is a fundamental feature of ionic-liquid-gated quasi-2D materials at high bias.

### [27] [Altermagnetic-doping interplay as a route to enhanced d-wave pairing in the Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29377)
*Ji Liu,Jianyu Li,Peng Zhang,Xiaosen Yang,Ho-Kin Tang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了交变磁体（altermagnets）中通过自旋各向异性调控超导配对对称性的机制，发现弱自旋各向异性增强d波配对，强各向异性则导致d+p混合配对态，为理解铜氧化物超导体和设计新型超导材料提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）作为具有动量奇自旋分裂的零净矩磁体，提供了一种可调控的途径来抑制长程反铁磁性同时保留强短程自旋涨落。研究旨在探索这种环境如何稳定非常规超导性并产生混合对称性配对。

Method: 通过自旋各向异性哈伯德模型（spin-anisotropic Hubbard model）的强耦合分析，推导出各向异性t-J模型，其中交换相互作用协同增强单重态d波配对并促进三重态p波配对。采用平均场分析和约束路径量子蒙特卡洛模拟（constrained-path quantum Monte Carlo simulations）进行研究。

Result: 平均场分析显示配对演化由交变磁各向异性驱动：弱自旋各向异性增强d波通道，类似于铜氧化物超导体中的主导配对对称性；强各向异性则激活三重态通道，导致稳定的d+p混合配对态。量子蒙特卡洛模拟证实了在最佳掺杂附近主导d波关联与涌现p波分量共存。

Conclusion: 交变磁体中的自旋各向异性能够调控超导配对对称性，弱各向异性增强d波配对，强各向异性产生协同的d+p混合配对态，这种协同态表现出显著增强的整体配对强度，暗示了实现更高超导转变温度的可能性。

Abstract: Altermagnets - collinear, zero-net-moment magnets with momentum-odd spin splitting protected by crystalline symmetries - offer a tunable route to suppress long-range antiferromagnetism while preserving strong short-range spin fluctuations. We show that this environment robustly stabilizes unconventional superconductivity and naturally produces mixed-symmetry pairing. Through a strong-coupling analysis of a spin-anisotropic Hubbard model, we derive an anisotropic t-J model where exchange interactions cooperatively enhance singlet d-wave pairing and promote triplet p-wave pairing. Our mean-field analysis reveals a pairing evolution driven by altermagnetic anisotropy: for small spin anisotropy, the d-wave channel is enhanced, closely resembling the dominant pairing symmetry in cuprate superconductors, which suggests that weak spin anisotropy may be an essential ingredient in realistic models of these materials. Constrained-path quantum Monte Carlo simulations confirm this picture, showing a regime where dominant d-wave correlations coexist with an emergent p-wave component near optimal doping. As spin anisotropy increases, strong C2 anisotropy and spin splitting activate the triplet channel, leading to a stable d+p mixed-pairing state. This synergistic state exhibits significantly enhanced overall pairing strength, suggesting the possibility of a higher superconducting transition temperature.

### [28] [Pressure-enhanced superconductivity and its correlation with suppressed resistance dip in (La,Pr)3Ni2O7 films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29531)
*Jinyu Zhao,Guangdi Zhou,Shu Cai,Shuaihang Sun,Yaqi Chen,Jing Guo,Yazhou Zhou,Haoliang Huang,Jin-Feng Jia,Yang Ding,Qi Wu,Zhuoyu Chen,Qi-Kun Xue,Liling Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究报道了(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇超导薄膜在静水压下的系统研究，发现压力能普遍增强薄膜的超导转变温度（T_c），最高可达68.5 K（2.0 GPa），并揭示了电阻下降特征与氧空位浓度相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: La₃Ni₂O₇和(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇薄膜在常压下超过40 K的超导转变温度（T_c）为常压条件下的实验提供了平台。确定T_c能否进一步提升并揭示控制这些常压超导薄膜T_c的物理机制至关重要。

Method: 研究对(La,Pr)₃Ni₂O₇薄膜的超导性质进行了静水压（hydrostatic pressure）效应的系统研究，通过施加外部压力（最高2.0 GPa）观察超导转变温度的变化和电阻行为特征。

Result: 外部压力普遍增强了薄膜样品的T_c，起始T_c从0.3 GPa时的62 K显著增加到2.0 GPa时的68.5 K。未达到零电阻的样品在超导转变上方出现电阻下降（resistance dip），而达到零电阻的样品则无此特征。压力可抑制该下降特征并驱动系统趋向零电阻状态。

Conclusion: 电阻下降特征与氧空位（oxygen vacancies）相关，其深度可作为空位浓度的指标。该特征可能由移动电子在空位处的局域化（localization）引起，施加压力可使这些电子退局域化（delocalize），从而可能促进T_c的增加。

Abstract: The discovery of superconductivity with a transition temperature (Tc) exceeding 40 K in La3Ni2O7 and (La,Pr)3Ni2O7 thin films at ambient pressure provides a viable platform for the experiments that can only be conducted under ambient-pressure conditions, and for the theoretical investigations aimed at understanding the commonalities and peculiarities of the behaviors related to the superconductivity between the film and the compressed bulk systems - including the effects of oxygen vacancies and strain. Consequently, it is crucial to determine whether Tc can be further enhanced and to uncover the underlying physics that controls the Tc value in these ambient-pressure superconducting thin films. Here, we report a systematic study of hydrostatic pressure effects on the superconducting properties of (La,Pr)3Ni2O7 thin films. We find that external pressure universally enhances Tc of the film samples regardless of their initial Tc value. The onset Tc of 68.5 K at 2.0 GPa demonstrates a notable increase from 62 K at 0.3 GPa. Furthermore, we observe that the samples without zero resistance show a resistance dip just above the superconducting transition, whereas the samples that exhibit zero resistance do not display this dip. Applying pressure can suppress the dips and drive the system toward zero resistance. Based on our results, we propose that this feature is associated with oxygen vacancies and that the depth of the dip can serve as an indicator of the concentration of the vacancies. It is plausible that the dip is caused by the localization of mobile electrons at the vacancy sites. Applying pressure can delocalize these electrons, which in turn may contribute to the increase in Tc.

</details>


### [29] [Ultrafast Two-Dimensional Spectroscopy Uncovers Ubiquitous Electron-Paramagnon Coupling in Cuprate Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29713)
*Francesco Proietto,Alessandra Milloch,Paolo Franceschini,Mohammadjavad Azarm,Niccolò Sellati,Rishabh Mishra,Peter C. Gorovikov,Pinder Dosanjh,Stefania Pagliara,Gabriele Ferrini,Fabio Boschini,Lara Benfatto,Giacomo Ghiringhelli,Fulvio Parmigiani,Jeffrey A. Davis,Andrea Damascelli,Claudio Giannetti*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子激发与集体玻色模式（bosonic modes）的耦合是铜酸盐高温超导性的关键机制。然而，传统平衡态和泵浦-探测光学光谱难以区分能量尺度重叠的不同玻色模式耦合，需要新的实验方法来克服这一限制。

Method: 研究采用超快二维电子光谱（2DES）技术，该技术以飞秒时间分辨率关联相干激发和探测光子能量。通过将测量光谱与包含电荷转移和磁激发相互作用的理论框架进行比较，识别出特定的玻色模式。

Result: 2DES揭示了由能量约200 meV的非热玻色子超快产生引起的显著非对角共振。这些玻色子被识别为动量中心在(π/2,π/2)并向(0,π)和(π,0)延伸的顺磁子。该共振在宽温度和掺杂范围内持续存在，表明高能顺磁子在整个铜酸盐相图中普遍且强耦合于电子激发。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了2DES作为解耦模式选择性电子-玻色子相互作用和解决退相干动力学的强大方法，为研究强关联量子材料开辟了新途径。同时为未来时间分辨共振非弹性X射线散射实验提供了直接框架，以追踪磁激发的超快动力学。

Abstract: The coupling between electronic excitations and collective bosonic modes is fundamental to the emergence of high-temperature superconductivity in cuprates. Despite extensive effort, conventional equilibrium and pump-probe optical spectroscopies still struggle to disentangle couplings to different bosonic modes when their energy scales overlap. Here we overcome this limitation using ultrafast two-dimensional electronic spectroscopy (2DES), which correlates coherent excitation and detection photon energies with femtosecond time resolution. Applied to optimally doped Bi$_2$Sr$_2$Ca$_{0.92}$Y$_{0.08}$Cu$_2$O$_{8+δ}$, 2DES reveals a pronounced off-diagonal resonance arising from the ultrafast generation of non-thermal bosons with energy $\hbarΩ_\mathbf{q}\simeq200$ meV. By comparing the measured spectra with a theoretical framework that explicitly includes the interaction between charge-transfer and magnetic excitations, we identify these bosons as paramagnons with momenta centered near $(π/2,π/2)$ and extending toward $(0,π)$ and $(π,0)$. The resonance persists across a large range of temperatures and doping concentrations, demonstrating that high-energy paramagnons are ubiquitously and strongly coupled to electronic excitations throughout the cuprate phase diagram. Time-domain analysis constrains the build-up of the paramagnon population to $\lesssim 10$ fs, placing a lower bound $λ\gtrsim 0.7$ on the coupling strength. More broadly, our results establish 2DES as a powerful approach for disentangling mode-selective electron-boson interactions and addressing decoherence dynamics, thereby establishing a new avenue for investigating strongly correlated quantum materials. These findings also provide a direct framework for future time-resolved resonant inelastic X-ray scattering experiments aimed at tracking the ultrafast dynamics of magnetic excitations.

</details>

### [30] [Dark radiation from Kerr primordial black holes: the role of superradiance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29790)
*Nayun Jia,Chen Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了超辐射（superradiance）对原初黑洞（PBHs）蒸发产生的暗辐射（DR）的影响，发现超辐射通常抑制有效相对论粒子数ΔN_eff，需要重新评估不考虑超辐射时对PBH质量和自旋的现有约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解超辐射不稳定性（superradiant instability）如何影响原初黑洞（primordial black holes）蒸发产生的暗辐射（dark radiation）。当粒子谱包含超出标准模型（beyond-the-Standard-Model）的玻色子时，超辐射会从黑洞中提取角动量形成玻色子云，从而改变暗辐射的产生机制。

Method: 方法包括在膨胀的早期宇宙背景下，同时演化黑洞质量和自旋、超辐射模式占据数、共动熵和宇宙学能量密度。通过比较超辐射时间尺度与黑洞蒸发时间尺度，分析其对暗辐射产生的影响。

Result: 研究发现超辐射通常抑制ΔN_eff：通过提取角动量阻止霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）将其转化为引力子，超辐射"饿死"了主要的暗辐射通道。超辐射云发射的引力波（gravitational waves）只能部分补偿这种损失，且仅当超辐射与黑洞蒸发时间尺度相当时有效。

Conclusion: 结论表明，如果粒子谱中存在超出标准模型的玻色子，则不考虑超辐射时对原初黑洞质量和自旋的现有ΔN_eff约束必须重新评估，因为超辐射会显著改变暗辐射的产生机制。

Abstract: Light primordial black holes (PBHs) that fully evaporate before Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) produce dark radiation (DR) via Hawking radiation of gravitons, contributing to the effective number of relativistic species $ΔN_{\rm eff}$. If the particle spectrum contains a beyond-the-Standard-Model (BSM) boson with Compton wavelength comparable to the black hole (BH) gravitational radius, superradiant instability extracts angular momentum from the BH into a bosonic cloud, whose gravitational wave (GW) emission contributes an additional source of DR. By simultaneously evolving the BH mass and spin, superradiant mode occupation numbers, comoving entropy and cosmological energy densities in an expanding early-universe background, we find that superradiance generically suppresses $ΔN_{\rm eff}$: by extracting angular momentum before Hawking radiation can convert it into gravitons, superradiance starves the dominant dark-radiation channel. The GWs emitted by the superradiant cloud can partially compensate this loss, but only when the superradiant and BH evaporation timescales are comparable; otherwise the cloud GWs are emitted too early and diluted by cosmological expansion. The results imply that existing $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ bounds on PBH mass and spin derived without superradiance must be revisited if BSM bosons are present in the particle spectrum.

</details>

### [31] [On the Meaning of Urban Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30021)
*Ulysse Marquis,Marc Barthelemy*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了城市标度律（urban scaling laws）中横向比较（transversal scaling）与纵向动态（longitudinal scaling）的根本差异，指出横向标度指数主要反映城市群体的统计异质性而非个体城市的动态演化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市标度律通常通过横向比较不同城市在特定时间点的数据获得，但其与单个城市时间演化动态之间的联系尚不明确。本研究旨在探讨横向标度指数如何从城市纵向动态中产生，并阐明其实际意义。

Method: 研究从城市纵向动态出发推导横向标度指数的显式表达式，分析城市群体异质性对测量结果的影响。通过城市面积-人口关系等具体案例，验证理论推导的结论。

Result: 研究发现横向标度指数并不直接反映个体城市动态，而是城市群体异质性的统计产物。即使所有城市都遵循线性纵向动态，横向比较仍可能产生表观的亚线性或超线性标度关系。横向标度指数所描述的行为通常在任何单个城市的演化轨迹中都观察不到。

Conclusion: 横向标度律（cross-sectional scaling laws）通常不能用于推断个体城市的动态演化规律。横向标度指数只有在严格条件下（城市表现为彼此的缩放版本且路径依赖性较弱）才具有明确的动态意义，否则它主要反映城市群体的统计异质性而非增长规律。

Abstract: Urban scaling laws describe how an urban quantity $Y$ varies with city population $P$, typically as $Y \sim P^β$. These relations are usually obtained from cross-sectional comparisons across cities at a given time (transversal scaling), but their link to the temporal evolution of individual cities (longitudinal scaling) remains unclear. Here we derive explicit expressions for the transversal exponent from the longitudinal dynamics of cities. We show that the measured exponent does not directly reflect individual city dynamics, but instead arises from a snapshot of a heterogeneous ensemble of cities with distinct growth trajectories. As a result, transversal scaling combines intrinsic dynamics with statistical effects due to the distribution of city sizes and correlations between population and city-specific parameters. Consequently, cross-sectional scaling laws cannot, in general, be used to infer the dynamics of individual cities. In particular, apparent sub- or superlinear scaling can emerge even when all cities follow linear longitudinal dynamics, as we demonstrate for the area-population relation. Strikingly, the behavior associated with the transversal exponent is in general not observed in the trajectory of any individual city, underscoring its collective, rather than dynamical, nature. More broadly, the transversal exponent has a clear dynamical meaning only under restrictive conditions-when cities behave as scaled versions of one another and path dependence is weak. Outside of these limits, it is not a law of urban growth, but a statistical artefact of heterogeneity.

</details>

### [32] [A non-local constitutive model for the Mullins effect in filled elastomers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28911)
*Keven Alkhoury*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过两种非局部方法扩展了填充橡胶材料的局部本构模型，以解决网格依赖性（mesh dependence）问题，并提供了在Abaqus中的数值实现细节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 填充橡胶材料（filled rubber-like materials）在工程应用中广泛使用，且已知表现出穆林斯效应（Mullins effect）。现有的局部本构模型存在固有的网格依赖性，需要扩展至非局部设置来解决这一问题。

Method: 采用两种非局部方法扩展局部模型：(i) 基于亥姆霍兹型方程（Helmholtz-type equation）控制非局部软体积分数（non-local soft volume fraction）；(ii) 在软体积分数局部演化定律中直接引入拉普拉斯项（Laplacian term）。两种方法均产生额外的偏微分方程，通过类比热传导方程在Abaqus中进行数值求解。

Result: 两种非局部方法得到了不同的结果，选择哪种方法需要由实验发现来指导。研究提供了详细的实现细节和开发的代码。

Conclusion: 通过引入非局部效应成功解决了局部本构模型的网格依赖性问题，但两种非局部方法的结果差异表明需要实验验证来确定最合适的建模方法。

Abstract: Filled rubber-like materials are widely used in engineering applications and are well known to exhibit the Mullins effect. In this work, an established local constitutive model from the literature is extended to a non-local setting to resolve the mesh dependence inherent to the local approach. Non-local effects are incorporated using two separate approaches: (i) a Helmholtz-type equation governing a non-local soft volume fraction, and (ii) a Laplacian term introduced directly into the soft volume fraction local evolution law. In both formulations, an additional governing partial differential equation arises and is solved numerically in Abaqus using an analogy with the heat equation. The two approaches yield different results, leaving the choice between them to be guided by experimental findings. The details of the implementation, along with the code developed in this work are also provided.

</details>


### [33] [Emergent charge crystallization and frustration in a particle anti-spin Ice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29389)
*Renaud Baillou,Matthew Terkel,Cristiano Nisoli,Pietro Tierno*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究首次实现了"反自旋冰（anti-spin ice）"系统，其中系统寻求最大化而非最小化自旋冰电荷，颠覆了传统自旋冰的冰规则（ice rule）。通过在快速旋转面内磁场中利用胶体粒子间的各向同性吸引力，实现了与传统胶体自旋冰排斥相互作用的范式反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工自旋冰（artificial spin ice）已成为设计奇异物态的多功能平台，但其核心冰规则（ice rule）始终要求最小化局部拓扑电荷。本研究旨在探索冰规则不成立甚至其对立情况，即系统寻求最大化自旋冰电荷的新物理体系。

Method: 采用快速旋转的面内磁场（fast-rotating, in-plane magnetic fields）在胶体粒子间产生各向同性吸引力，从而反转传统胶体自旋冰的排斥相互作用范式。通过实验和模拟相结合的方法，在标准方形和蜂窝状晶格以及新型五七边形（pentaheptite）几何结构中进行研究。

Result: 建立了反自旋冰中的有序和无序规则，并在五七边形晶格中展示了该系统也能表现出新的挫败（frustration）类型。这种拓扑电荷挫败（topological charge frustration）源于晶格连通性，其中不等边奇数多边形网络在高相互作用强度下抑制电荷结晶。

Conclusion: 本研究首次实现了反自旋冰系统，不仅打破了传统冰规则，还实现了其对立面。通过反转胶体自旋冰的相互作用范式，揭示了新型拓扑电荷挫败机制，为工程化奇异物态提供了新平台。

Abstract: Artificial spin ices have transcended their origins in frustrated rare-earth pyrochlores to become a versatile platform for engineering exotic states of matter. Across diverse implementations, from nanomagnets and superconducting vortices to colloids, quantum annealers, liquid crystals, and metamaterials, they are unified by the ice rule, which often leads to degeneracy and constrained disorder by enforcing minimization of the local topological charge. Here, we report the first realization of an "anti-spin ice" in which not only the ice rule does not hold, but its opposite is true as the system seeks to maximize, rather than minimize, spin ice charges. Using fast-rotating, in-plane magnetic fields to generate isotropic attraction between colloidal particles, we invert the conventional paradigm of repulsive interactions in colloidal spin ices. Combining experiments and simulations across standard square and honeycomb lattices as well as novel pentaheptite geometries, we establish rules for order and disorder in the anti-spin ice. With the pentaheptite lattice, we demonstrate that the anti-spin ice system can also exhibit frustration, but of a new kind. This topological charge frustration arises from the lattice connectivity, where networks of unequal, odd-sided polygons suppress charge crystallization at high interaction strength.

</details>


### [34] [Concentration-Dependent Restructuring of Ionic Liquid Micelles Induced by an Anionic Surfactant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29413)
*Devansh Kaushik,Sajal K. Ghosh,Syed M. Kamil*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了亚临界胶束浓度（sub-CMC）的阴离子表面活性剂十二烷基硫酸钠（SDS）如何影响离子液体（IL）1-甲基-3-辛基咪唑氯化物的胶束化行为，揭示了SDS作为IL聚集有效调节剂的作用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然离子液体对表面活性剂胶束化的影响已被广泛研究，但关于表面活性剂（特别是低于其临界胶束浓度时）如何影响离子液体聚集的研究相对较少。理解这种相互作用对于阐明离子液体-表面活性剂体系的物理化学性质及其工业应用至关重要。

Method: 研究采用表面张力测量、理论分析和粗粒度分子动力学模拟（coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations）相结合的方法。实验在离子液体浓度高于其CMC、SDS浓度低于其CMC的条件下进行，考察SDS对IL胶束化的影响。

Result: 研究发现：低浓度SDS（约2 mM）可平滑插入预存IL胶束，形成稳定的混合胶束；当SDS浓度接近约4 mM时，胶束内部动力学发生显著变化，热力学参数出现偏差；超过此浓度后，体系重组形成SDS比例更高但仍富含IL的稳定混合胶束。Clint和Rubingh模型量化了协同效应，模拟结果支持结构转变，显示胶束尺寸、聚集数和径向分布函数的变化。

Conclusion: 该工作证明SDS可作为离子液体聚集的有效调节剂，为理解离子液体-表面活性剂共组装机制提供了机理性见解。研究揭示了亚CMC表面活性剂对IL胶束化的复杂调制作用，对相关工业应用具有指导意义。

Abstract: The self-assembling behaviour of ionic liquids in aqueous solution is important for understanding their physicochemical properties and for their industrial applications. While the influence of ionic liquids on surfactant micellization has been widely studied, much less attention has been given to how surfactants affect the aggregation of ionic liquids, particularly when the surfactant concentration is below its critical micelle concentration (CMC). In this work, we examine the effect of the anionic surfactant sodium dodecyl sulfate (SDS), introduced at sub-CMC concentration, on the micellization of 1-methyl-3-octylimidazolium chloride in aqueous solution maintained above the IL CMC, using surface tension measurements, theoretical analysis, and coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations. We find that at low SDS concentrations (approx 2 mM), SDS inserts smoothly into the pre-existing IL micelles, producing stable mixed micelles with favourable IL-SDS interactions. When the SDS concentration approaches (approx 4 mM), the micelles exhibit distinct changes in their internal dynamics, reflected in deviations in the thermodynamic parameters. Beyond this point, as more SDS is added, the system reorganizes and forms stable mixed micelles again, now containing a higher fraction of SDS but still enriched in IL. The synergistic behaviour is quantified using Clint and Rubingh's models, and simulations supports the structural transitions, showing variations in micelle size, aggregation number, and radial distribution functions. This work demonstrates that SDS acts as an effective modulator of IL aggregation, providing mechanistic insight into IL-surfactant co-assembly.

</details>


### [35] [The continuum limit of the Poland-Scheraga DNA denaturation model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29637)
*Richard Dengler*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过场论方法推导了长DNA分子的相图，发现排除体积效应导致两个稳定不动点，分别对应连续相变和一阶相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解长DNA分子的相图特性，特别是排除体积相互作用对相变性质的影响，这有助于揭示DNA结构转变的物理机制。

Method: 采用与Poland-Scheraga（PS）模型晶格版本等价的场论方法，对包含排除体积相互作用的广义PS模型进行单圈重整化群计算。

Result: 计算显示存在两个稳定不动点：当原始排除体积效应较弱时达到的不动点对应连续相变；另一个不动点则对应一阶相变，排除体积效应在两个不动点均发挥作用。

Conclusion: 长DNA分子的相图可以通过封闭形式推导，排除体积相互作用导致相变性质的多样性，为理解DNA结构转变提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Using a field theory equivalent to a lattice version of the Poland-Scheraga (PS) model, the phase diagram for a long DNA molecule is derived in closed form. A one-loop renormalization group calculation for the generalized PS model with excluded volume interactions shows that there are two stable fixed points. At both fixed points, the excluded volume effect plays a role. At the fixed point reached when the original excluded volume effect is weak, the phase transition is continuous. At the other fixed point, the phase transition is first order.

### [36] [Numerical calculations of neutron star mountains supported by crustal lattice pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28857)
*T. J. Hutchins,D. I. Jones*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过自洽计算磁化吸积中子星中的温度不对称性、晶格压力扰动和质量不对称性，发现由热梯度驱动的弹性应变形成的"山脉"过小，无法主导低质量X射线双星的自旋平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波可能决定低质量X射线双星（LMXBs）中中子星的自旋频率，其中一个机制是通过热梯度驱动的弹性应变形成质量不对称性（即"山脉"）。先前研究多孤立探讨弹性应变或温度不对称性的起源，未考虑整个形成过程。

Method: 在统一框架内自洽计算温度不对称性、地壳晶格压力扰动和质量不对称性；首次采用布鲁塞尔-蒙特利尔核能密度泛函BSk19、BSk20和BSk21等现实状态方程，以热力学一致的方式统一描述吸积中子星所有区域。

Result: 研究发现这些"山脉"过小，无法主导低质量X射线双星的自旋平衡；同时估算了它们产生的引力波辐射水平。

Conclusion: 通过详细计算验证了热梯度驱动的弹性应变形成的质量不对称性不足以解释低质量X射线双星的自旋平衡机制，为理解中子星引力波辐射提供了重要约束。

Abstract: Gravitational waves may set the spin frequencies of neutron stars in low-mass X-ray binaries (LMXBs). One mechanism for facilitating such emission is the formation of a mass asymmetry - or 'mountain' - supported by elastic strains driven by thermal gradients. Most studies have focused either on the origin of the elastic strains or the temperature asymmetry in isolation, and have not considered the entire formation process. In previous work, we showed that anisotropic heat transport in magnetised accreting neutron stars can source a significant temperature asymmetry, and made rough estimates that suggested temperature-induced perturbations in the pressure supplied by the crustal lattice may be competitive with the widely known model of temperature-induced capture-layer shifts. In this paper we carry out detailed calculations to properly explore this scenario. We self-consistently calculate both the temperature asymmetries, the perturbations in crustal lattice pressure, and the mass asymmetries within a single framework. For the first time, we make use of the set of realistic equations of state from the Brussels-Montreal nuclear energy-density functionals BSk19, BSk20, and BSk21 which describe all regions of accreting neutron stars in a thermodynamically consistent, unified way. We find these mountains are too small to be dictating the spin-equilibrium of LMXBs, and estimate the level of gravitational wave emission they produce.

</details>


### [37] [Eccentricity constraints disfavor single-single capture in nuclear star clusters as the origin of all LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA binary black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29019)
*Nihar Gupte,M. Coleman Miller,Rhiannon Udall,Sophie Bini,Alessandra Buonanno,Jonathan Gair,Aldo Gamboa,Lorenzo Pompili,Antoni Ramos-Buades,Maximilian Dax,Stephen R. Green,Annalena Kofler,Jakob Macke,Bernhard Schölkopf*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究利用LVK O4a观测到的85个双黑洞并合事件，通过多极、偏心、自旋对齐的有效单体波形模型分析轨道偏心率分布，未发现显著的偏心信号，并据此排除了核星团中单-单引力波捕获作为主要形成机制的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双黑洞（BBHs）的形成机制多样，包括孤立双星演化和致密星团中的动力学组装，但各通道的相对贡献仍不确定。通过分析LVK探测到的黑洞并合轨道偏心率分布，可以约束不同形成通道的比例。

Method: 研究分析了LVK第四轮观测前半段（O4a）的85个双黑洞事件，采用多极、偏心、自旋对齐的有效单体（effective-one-body）波形模型。参数推断结合了神经后验估计和嵌套采样方法，并纳入了天体物理先验概率。

Result: 未发现任何候选事件达到足够高的统计显著性以确认偏心率的可靠探测。基于这些上限约束，在假设所有O4a双黑洞均来自单-单引力波捕获（single-single GW captures）的特定模型下，推断宿主环境的速度弥散上限为σ < 24.3 km/s（95%置信上限）。

Conclusion: 该结果排除了核星团（速度弥散约20-200 km/s）中单-单捕获作为所有观测双黑洞并合主要来源的可能性。偏心率测量对于在现有和未来引力波探测器中区分致密双星形成通道具有重要价值。

Abstract: Multiple formation pathways have been proposed for the origin of binary black holes (BBHs). These include isolated binary evolution and dynamical assembly in dense stellar environments such as nuclear or globular star clusters. Yet, the fraction of BBHs originating from each channel still remains uncertain. One way to constrain this fraction is by investigating the distribution of the orbital eccentricities of the BH coalescences detected by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) Collaboration. In this work, we analyze 85 BBHs from the first part of the fourth LVK observing run (O4a) using a multipolar, eccentric, aligned-spin effective-one-body waveform model. We perform parameter inference with neural posterior estimation and nested sampling. After incorporating astrophysical prior odds and comparing to the quasicircular precessing-spin hypothesis, we find that no candidates reach a high enough statistical significance to claim a confident detection of eccentricity. We use these upper limits to explore a particular model, in which all O4a BBHs originate from single-single gravitational wave (GW) captures. We perform hierarchical inference on the velocity dispersion of the host environment and find $σ< 24.3\,\mathrm{km/s}$ (95% credible upper bound). This disfavors single-single capture in nuclear star clusters (~20-200 km/s) as the dominant source of all observed BBH mergers. We verify that this dispersion bound does not increase by repeating the inference on a synthetic catalog augmented with eccentric events motivated by analyses of the third observing run of the LVK (O3). Our results place improved constraints on the number of eccentric BBHs and highlight the importance of eccentricity measurements in disentangling compact-binary formation channels in current and future GW detectors.

</details>

### [38] [A Determination of the Top Mass from a Global PDF Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28865)
*Richard D. Ball,Jaco ter Hoeve,Roy Stegeman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在部分子分布函数（PDF）的全局分析框架内，通过结合多种高精度测量数据，间接确定了顶夸克（top-quark）的极点质量（pole mass）$m_t$，结果为$172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过结合部分子分布函数（PDF）的全局分析，利用多种高精度实验数据对顶夸克极点质量进行更精确的间接测定。该方法旨在克服传统直接测量中的局限性，通过综合不同来源的约束提高测量精度。

Method: 采用基于NNPDF框架的全局PDF分析方法，考虑了广泛的测量数据，包括单微分和双微分可观测量。计算达到次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD精度并包含电弱（EW）修正，同时PDF演化达到近似三阶（N³LO）QCD精度并包含QED修正。分析独特之处包括：包含$t\bar{t}$阈值附近的顶偶素（toponium）贡献、来自格点（lattice）的先进$α_s$约束，以及对ATLAS和CMS在8和13 TeV能量下微分截面测量的详细灵敏度研究。

Result: 研究确定了顶夸克极点质量$m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV，该结果是在近似N³LO QCD精度下，包含NLO QED、电弱（EW）和顶偶素（toponium）修正后得到的。分析表明，联合确定需要重新拟合PDF以正确关联不确定性。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了在PDF全局分析框架内结合多种高精度测量数据对顶夸克极点质量进行间接测定的有效性。通过包含顶偶素贡献、格点$α_s$约束和详细的微分截面灵敏度分析，获得了高精度的$m_t$测量结果，为粒子物理标准模型参数确定提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We present an indirect determination of the top-quark pole mass $m_t$ within a global analysis of parton distribution functions (PDFs), based on the public NNPDF framework. We consider a wide range of measurements, including both single- and double-differential observables, computed at NNLO QCD accuracy with EW corrections, and analyse their individual as well as combined impact on the joint $(α_s, m_t)$ parameter space, while accounting for PDF evolution up to approximate ${\rm N^3LO}$ QCD accuracy with QED corrections. We account for missing higher order QCD uncertainties by default. Unique to our analysis are the inclusion of, first, toponium contributions around the $t\bar{t}$ threshold, second, state-of-the-art constraints on $α_s$ from the lattice, and finally, a detailed sensitivity study of the various ATLAS and CMS differential cross-section measurements at 8 and 13 TeV. We demonstrate explicitly how a combined determination requires the refitting of the PDFs in order to correctly correlate uncertainties. We find $m_t = 172.80 \pm 0.26$ GeV at approximate N$^3$LO QCD including NLO QED, EW and toponium corrections.

</details>


### [39] [Higgs Boson Spookiness: Probing Quantum Nonlocality with Spacetime-Resolved $H\rightarrowτ^+τ^-$ Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28868)
*Lawrence Lee,John Lawless,Caroline Riggall*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出在未来电子-正电子对撞机（Higgs工厂）中，通过测量Higgs玻色子衰变产生的τ轻子自旋关联随时空间隔的变化，实现对量子非定域性（quantum nonlocality）的时空分辨检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在利用未来Higgs工厂的精确测量能力，首次在粒子对撞机中实现电弱量子纠缠（electroweak quantum entanglement）的时空分辨测量，直接检验量子非定域性并排除超光速纠缠信号传播理论。

Method: 通过模拟在质心能量240 GeV的电子-正电子对撞中产生的ZH→(μμ)(ττ)事件，重建τ轻子衰变顶点并测量其自旋关联（spin correlations）随两个τ衰变间时空间隔（spacetime interval）的函数变化。

Result: 在0.75 ab⁻¹积分亮度下，该测量能以95%置信水平排除低于约2倍光速的纠缠信号传播速度，对于任何自旋关联信号，可排除低于约9倍光速的传播速度。

Conclusion: 该研究首次提出在粒子对撞机中进行电弱量子纠缠的时空分辨测量，展示了未来Higgs工厂在检验量子非定域性和排除超光速有限速度纠缠信号理论方面的独特能力。

Abstract: We demonstrate that a future precision $ee$ Higgs factory would be able to perform a spacetime-resolved test of quantum nonlocality in Higgs boson decays. In simulated $ee\rightarrow ZH \rightarrow (μμ)(ττ)$ events at $\sqrt{s}=240$ GeV, we reconstruct $τ$ lepton decay vertices and measure spin correlations as a function of the spacetime interval between the two $τ$ decays. Such a measurement would be able to test Bell-inequality-violating correlations for spacelike-separated decays, enabling direct exclusion of superluminal, finite-speed entanglement signaling theories. With 0.75 ab$^{-1}$ of integrated luminosity, entanglement signal propagation speeds below $\approx2c$ can be excluded at 95$\%$ CL. Signals establishing any spin correlation can be excluded for speeds below $\approx9c$. This constitutes the first proposed spacetime-resolved measurement of electroweak quantum entanglement at a particle collider and demonstrates a unique capability of future Higgs factories.

</details>


### [40] [Dark photon and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge boson from dark Higgs boson decays at FASER and SHiP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28882)
