<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索暗光子（dark photon）和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子在FASER和SHiP实验中的探测潜力，特别关注暗希格斯玻色子衰变产生的矢量玻色子产生机制。

Method: 方法包括分析暗希格斯玻色子衰变产生的矢量玻色子对产生过程（包括在壳和离壳衰变），并考虑单矢量玻色子伴随标准模型粒子的新产生过程。研究结合了FASER实验的最新结果来推导参数空间约束。

Result: 研究推导了暗光子的参数空间约束，并展示了未来FASER2和SHiP实验对暗光子和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子的预期灵敏度区域。同时讨论了U(1)$_{B-L}$模型中冻结产生（freeze-in）惰性中微子暗物质的灵敏度。

Conclusion: 该研究为FASER和SHiP实验探测暗光子和U(1)$_{B-L}$规范玻色子提供了全面的灵敏度分析框架，特别强调了暗希格斯玻色子衰变通道和新产生过程的重要性。

Abstract: We study the sensitivity to dark photons and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge bosons produced via dark Higgs boson decays at the FASER and SHiP experiments. In addition to pair production of these vector bosons from both on-shell and off-shell dark Higgs boson decays, a new production process of single vector boson associated with the standard model particles is taken into account. Constraints on the parameter space of dark photon are derived with including the latest results from the FASER experiment. The expected sensitivity regions to the dark photon and U(1)$_{B-L}$ gauge boson of the future FASER2 and SHiP experiments are presented. The sensitivity to the U(1)$_{B-L}$ model with freeze-in sterile neutrino dark matter is also discussed.

</details>


### [41] [Autonomous Discovery of Particle Physics Theories from Experimental Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28935)
*Stephon Alexander,Benjamin Bradley,Loukas Gouskos,Cooper Niu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了Albert——一个神经符号人工智能框架，用于系统探索超越标准模型（Standard Model）的物理理论空间。该框架通过将粒子物理编码为形式语言，在强化学习环境中强制执行理论约束，并成功从大型正负电子对撞机（LEP）数据中重新发现标准模型并推断出顶夸克（top quark）的存在及其质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越标准模型（Standard Model）的物理探索面临理论空间组合爆炸的挑战。传统方法难以系统性地导航这一庞大的理论空间，需要一种能够避免大语言模型常见幻觉（hallucinations）的严谨探索框架。

Method: 研究引入Albert神经符号人工智能框架，将粒子物理编码为形式语言（formal language），基于规则语法生成表示对称性、粒子和相互作用的标记化序列。强化学习环境强制执行第一性原理理论约束，计算包含辐射修正（radiative corrections）的可观测量，并通过χ²分析评估与实验数据的统计似然。

Result: 使用仅包含大型正负电子对撞机（Large Electron-Positron Collider）遗留数据的2500万参数Transformer模型进行概念验证。Albert成功重新发现标准模型，自主推断出顶夸克的必要性及其性质，预测其质量为178.9±5.0 GeV，与现代大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）测量结果一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，AI驱动的理论探索具有作为自主发现新物理的严谨、无幻觉且可扩展范式的潜力。Albert框架能够系统导航理论空间，避免大语言模型的常见问题，为超越标准模型的物理探索提供了新方法。

Abstract: The search for physics beyond the Standard Model is hindered by a combinatorial explosion of possible theories. We introduce \textsc{Albert}, a neuro-symbolic artificial intelligence framework to systematically navigate this vast theory space. By encoding particle physics as a formal language, \textsc{Albert} generates tokenized sequences representing symmetries, particles, and interactions under a rule-based grammar, eliminating the hallucinations common in large language models. The reinforcement learning environment enforces first-principle theoretical constraints, computes observables with radiative corrections, and evaluates statistical likelihood via $χ^2$ analysis against experimental data. As a proof of concept, we train a 25-million-parameter transformer model using only legacy data from the Large Electron-Positron Collider, which contains no direct evidence of the top quark. Remarkably, \textsc{Albert} successfully rediscovered the Standard Model and autonomously inferred necessity and properties of the top quark, predicting its mass at $178.9\pm 5.0~\text{GeV}$, consistent with its modern measurement at the Large Hadron Collider. These results demonstrate the potential of AI-driven theory exploration as a rigorous, hallucination-free, and scalable paradigm for autonomous discovery of new physics.

</details>


### [42] [Two-Dimensional Transverse-Momentum Subtraction and Semi-Inclusive Deep-Inelastic Scattering at N$^3$LO in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29673)
*Liang Dong,Shen Fang,Jun Gao,Hai Tao Li,Ding Yu Shao,Hua Xing Zhu,Yu Jiao Zhu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次计算了微扰QCD中非极化半单举深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）的N³LO阶修正，采用基于软共线奇异性QCD因子化的二维横向动量减除新方法，为即将运行的电子-离子对撞机（EIC）的精确核子层析成像奠定理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已识别强子产生对于研究高能下的核子结构和QCD强子化过程至关重要。当前需要匹配即将运行的电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider, EIC）预期实验精度的理论计算，为精确核子层析成像（nucleon tomography）建立理论基础。

Method: 基于软共线奇异性（soft and collinear singularities）QCD因子化的二维横向动量减除（two-dimensional transverse-momentum subtraction）新方法，计算非极化半单举深度非弹性散射（unpolarized SIDIS）的N³LO阶修正。

Result: N³LO修正总体上适中，但在阈值区域（threshold regions）可能显著，展现出优异的微扰收敛性（perturbative convergence）和减小的标度变化（scale variations）。完全微分框架允许任意选择截断，可直接支持精确核子层析成像。

Conclusion: 该方法为即将运行的电子-离子对撞机（EIC）的精确核子层析成像建立了所需的理论基础，其方法也可推广到极化SIDIS（polarized SIDIS）的计算中。

Abstract: Identified hadron production is essential for the study of nucleon structure and QCD hadronization at high energies. We present the first calculation of unpolarized semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (SIDIS) at next-to-next-to-next-to-leading order (N$^3$LO) in perturbative QCD. Our calculation is based on a novel method of two-dimensional transverse-momentum subtraction motivated by QCD factorization of soft and collinear singularities. The N$^3$LO corrections are moderate in general but can be significant in threshold regions, and exhibit excellent perturbative convergence and reduced scale variations. The fully differential framework allows for arbitrary selection cuts and directly enables precision nucleon tomography at the upcoming Electron-Ion Collider, establishing the theory foundation needed to match the anticipated experimental accuracy. Generalization of the method to calculations of polarized SIDIS is also feasible.

</details>


### [43] [Perturbative QCD fitting of the $e^+e^-$ to hadrons KEDR and BESIII data for R(s) and $α_s$ determination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29803)
*A. L. Kataev,K. Yu. Todyshev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究比较了KEDR和BESIII合作组在粲夸克阈值以下收集的实验数据与不同阶微扰论截断的QCD表达式，分析了截断阶数对提取的强耦合常数α_s(M_Z)值的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过比较实验数据与不同阶微扰论截断的量子色动力学（QCD）表达式，分析截断阶数对提取强耦合常数（strong coupling constant）α_s(M_Z)值的影响，并探讨微扰论展开固定阶数的应用问题。

Method: 方法包括：比较KEDR和BESIII合作组在粲夸克阈值以下收集的实验数据；使用不同阶微扰论截断的QCD表达式分析正负电子湮灭（e^+e^- annihilation）R-比和重整化群（renormalization group）β-函数；对组合数据进行次领头阶（next-to-leading order）和次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading order）拟合。

Result: 结果显示：次领头阶拟合给出α_s(M_Z)=0.1179^{+0.0051}_{-0.0069}，次次领头阶拟合给出α_s(M_Z)=0.1221^{+0.0063}_{-0.0723}，表明提取的α_s(M_Z)值对微扰论截断阶数具有依赖性。

Conclusion: 结论强调了微扰论展开固定阶数的应用需要考虑截断阶数的影响，并指出需要谨慎处理解析延拓效应（analytical continuation effects）以获得更精确的强耦合常数提取结果。

Abstract: The experimental data collected by KEDR and BESIII collaborations at the energies below charming quark thresholds are compared with the coordinally truncated at different orders of perturbation theory QCD expressions for the $e^+e^-$ annihilation R-ratio and the renormalization group $β$-function. The fits demonstrate the dependence of the extracted $α_s(M_Z)$ values from orders of the truncation of the corresponding approximations. The next-to-leading order and next-to-next-to-leading order fits of the combined KEDR data and BESIII data , truncated at the mass scale of $J/Ψ$ meson, give the following results $α_s(M_Z)= 0.1179^{+0.0051}_{-0.0069}$ and $α_s(M_Z)=0.1221^{+0.0063}_{-0.0723}$. The subjects related to the applications of the fixed orders of perturbation theory expansions and careful treatment of the analytical continuation effects are commented.

</details>


### [44] [Two-Loop Spacelike Splitting Amplitudes in Full-Color QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27123)
*Federico Buccioni,Hanyu Fang,Kai Yan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文首次完整计算了全色QCD中所有部分子通道和螺旋度配置下的两圈类空间分裂振幅（two-loop spacelike splitting amplitudes），确认了N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中一类贡献的普适性，并识别了新的共线因子化破坏效应来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究QCD散射振幅在共线区域（collinear regime）的行为对于理解强子截面的因子化性质至关重要。当前需要完整计算两圈类空间分裂振幅以深入探究共线因子化机制。

Method: 采用全色QCD（full-color QCD）框架，计算所有部分子通道（partonic channels）和螺旋度配置（helicity configurations）下的两圈类空间分裂振幅。通过与N=4超杨-米尔斯理论（N=4 super Yang--Mills theory）结果对比进行分析。

Result: 首次获得了全色QCD中两圈类空间分裂振幅的完整结果。确认了N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中发现的一类贡献具有普适性，并识别了先前未知的共线因子化破坏效应来源。所有共线因子化破坏贡献在颜色求和平方振幅中相消。

Conclusion: 与N=4超杨-米尔斯理论的最新观察一致，所有共线因子化破坏贡献在颜色求和平方振幅中相消，这意味着在QCD三阶水平上，单部分子共线因子化对于喷注截面具有普适性。

Abstract: The study of QCD scattering amplitudes in the collinear regime provides crucial insight into the factorization properties of hadronic cross sections. In this paper, we present the first complete results for two-loop spacelike splitting amplitudes in full-color QCD, in all partonic channels and helicity configurations. We confirm the universality of a class of contributions already found in N=4 super Yang--Mills (sYM) theory, and identify previously unknown sources of collinear factorization-violating (CFV) effects. Consistent with recent observations in N=4 sYM, all CFV contributions cancel in color-summed squared amplitudes, implying the universality of single-parton collinear factorization for jet cross sections at third order in QCD.

</details>


### [45] [Rotation of the polarization plane in axion fields: application to neutron star polar cap regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28826)
*Iver H. Brevik,Moshe M. Chaichian,Tiberiu Harko,Yuri N. Obukhov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了中子星极冠区域强局域不均匀轴子（axion）区域的性质，预测轴子产量可增加高达10^50倍，分析了轴子环境中电磁波的非互易性（nonreciprocity）和偏振旋转效应，并计算了轴子流入"间隙（gap）"区域的填充时间（filling time）为纳秒量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于Noordhuis等人的研究，中子星极冠区域存在强局域不均匀轴子区域，这些区域具有极强的静态磁场（B_0 ∼ 10^8 T）和电场（E_0 ∼ 10^{-6}cB_0）。这些特征对于理解弱场和强场轴子群中的偏振面旋转（polarization plane rotation）等现象至关重要。

Method: 论文首先调研了导电材料的特殊天线特性，指出需要强磁场才能实现探测。然后推导了轴子环境中电磁波的一般形式，包括标准形式和物理上更具启发性的混合形式，展示了轴子流体的非互易性（nonreciprocity），并计算了偏振旋转。最后通过计算轴子流入初始间隙的填充时间（filling time）来评估相关时间尺度。

Result: 研究发现偏振旋转在弱轴子场情况下有明确定义，但对于极强场情况微扰理论（perturbative theory）失效。偏振面旋转的关键特性是仅当轴子云在空间或时间上变化时才会发生。计算显示轴子流入间隙的典型填充时间约为纳秒量级，在原子钟（atomic clocks）精度范围内可探测。

Conclusion: 论文系统分析了中子星极冠区域强局域轴子区域的性质，阐明了轴子环境中电磁波的非互易性和偏振旋转机制，并验证了Noordhuis等人提出的局部"间隙"区域物理图像。纳秒量级的填充时间表明这些效应在现有探测技术范围内是可观测的。

Abstract: Recent investigations by Noordhuis et al. [1, 2] and others have demonstrated the occurrence of strong local inhomogeneous axion regions in the polar cap regions of neutron stars. These regions are characterized by static magnetic fields $B_0 \sim 10^8\,$T ($=10^{12}\,$G) directed normally outwards from the polar surface (magnetic dipole), together with static electric fields $E_0 \sim 10^{-6}cB_0$ in the same direction (electric dipole). An enormous increase of axion production, up to order $10^{50}$, is predicted in the polar regions. These features are important for phenomena such as polarization plane rotation under both weak and strong axion field populations. We survey the peculiar antenna property of conductive materials, which shows the need for having very strong magnetic fields to make the detection possible. We present the general form of electromagnetic waves in the axion environment, in both the standard form and in a physically instructive hybrid one, showing the nonreciprocity of axion fluid, and calculate the polarization rotation. The rotation is well defined in the case of weak, but still stronger than average value of axion fields in Universe. For very strong fields such a perturbative theory breaks down, however. A noteworthy general property of the rotation of polarization plane is that it can only occur when the axion cloud is varying in space or time. We limit ourselves only variation in space. Finally, as application we discuss the physical picture of local 'gap' regions proposed by Noordhuis et al. in the polar regions of a neutron star. The reason for occurrence of these gaps is plasma effects. To evaluate the time scales involved, we calculate the filling time for surrounding axions flowing into an initial gap. It turns out that the typical filling time is a moderate number of nanoseconds, within the accuracy of atomic clocks precision to be detectable.

</details>


### [46] [Entanglement in the $θ$-vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29287)
*Sebastian Grieninger,Dmitri E. Kharzeev,Eliana Marroquin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究计算了具有有限θ角的大质量Schwinger模型中真空态的纠缠熵和纠缠谱，揭示了θ=π处纠缠熵增强的物理机制源于不同电通量真空分支的竞争，并验证了Bisognano-Wichmann定理在红外区域的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解Schwinger模型中θ角对真空态纠缠特性的影响，特别是θ=π附近纠缠熵增强的物理起源。通过建立保持θ周期性且无晶格伪影的晶格哈密顿量，旨在精确表征θ依赖的真空结构。

Method: 采用手征旋转（chirally rotated）晶格哈密顿量实现θ项，该方法在算符层面保持θ周期性，并在无质量极限下避免θ依赖的晶格伪影。利用Bisognano-Wichmann（BW）定理构造晶格BW纠缠哈密顿量，并与精确的模哈密顿量（modular Hamiltonian）进行比较。

Result: 研究发现θ=π附近的纠缠熵增强源于具有相反电场取向的不同真空分支之间的最大竞争，此时由费米子对产生引起的量子涨落达到最大。纠缠隙（entanglement gap）的显著变窄仅出现在临界质量比m/g≈0.33附近。BW纠缠哈密顿量与精确模哈密顿量在红外区域一致，表明纠缠哈密顿量可由空间加权的微观哈密顿量良好近似。

Conclusion: 纠缠可观测量可作为探测θ依赖真空结构的灵敏探针，手征旋转公式为开放边界条件提供了自然框架。这些结果可应用于拓扑绝缘体和量子线中的纠缠研究，揭示了θ角对量子场论真空态纠缠特性的深刻影响。

Abstract: We compute the entanglement entropy and the entanglement spectrum of the vacuum state in the massive Schwinger model at a finite $θ$ angle. The $θ$ term is implemented through a chirally rotated lattice Hamiltonian that preserves the periodicity in $θ$ already at the operator level and maintains the correct massless limit without $θ$-dependent lattice artifacts. We clarify the physical origin of entanglement entropy enhancement at $θ=π$ by relating it to the competition between distinct electric-flux vacuum branches. We show that the peak near $θ=π$ persists across the range of masses studied and corresponds to the point of maximal competition between distinct vacuum branches with opposite electric-field orientation, where quantum fluctuations due to fermion pair creation are maximized. While this entropy enhancement is generic, a pronounced narrowing of the entanglement gap occurs only near the critical mass ratio $m/g\simeq0.33$. Using the Bisognano--Wichmann (BW) theorem, we construct a lattice BW entanglement Hamiltonian and compare it with the exact modular Hamiltonian obtained from the reduced density matrix. We observe agreement between these Hamiltonians in the infrared sector, indicating that the entanglement Hamiltonian is well approximated by a spatially weighted microscopic Hamiltonian. These results establish entanglement observables as sensitive probes of the $θ$-dependent vacuum structure and highlight the chirally rotated formulation as a natural framework for open boundary conditions. Additionally, we discuss possible applications to entanglement in topological insulators and quantum wires.

</details>

*Alessio Giarnetti,Simone Marciano,Davide Meloni*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在假设带电轻子混合矩阵Ul由三个扇区（(1,2)、(1,3)或(2,3)）中单个2×2旋转构成的条件下，研究中微子质量矩阵对角化矩阵Uν所受约束，并考虑了包含JUNO实验θ12精确测量的最新全局拟合数据。

Conclusion: 该分析为理解中微子混合结构提供了理论框架，通过将Uν矩阵元与实验观测的PMNS参数直接关联，有助于探索潜在的味对称性机制。

Abstract: The unprecedented precision now being achieved in the measurement of the Pontecorvo--Maki--Nakagawa--Sakata (PMNS) lepton mixing matrix opens a new window onto the underlying structure of the neutrino mass matrix and the possibly associated flavor symmetries. In this work, we investigate the constraints imposed on the unitary matrix $U_ν$ that diagonalises the neutrino mass matrix, under the hypothesis that the charged-lepton mixing matrix $U_l$ consists of a single two-by-two rotation in one of the three sectors: (1,2), (1,3), or (2,3). For this analysis, we considered the latest global fit which incorporates the precision measurement of $θ_{12}$ from the JUNO experiment. For each scenario, we also derive analytical expressions for the entries of $U_ν$ in terms of the measured PMNS parameters to obtain compact sum-rule-like formulae.

### [48] [From Sub-eikonal DIS to Quark Distributions and their High-Energy Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30000)
*Giovanni Antonio Chirilli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了深度非弹性散射（deep-inelastic scattering）的高能偶极子描述与有限比约肯变量$x_B$下标准光锥算符（light-ray operator）表述之间的关联，证明这一联系在次领头阶（first sub-eikonal order）已经出现，并构建了冲击波形式（shock-wave formalism）与非局域光锥展开（non-local light-cone expansion）之间的算符级桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立小$x$框架与常规部分子描述之间的连接，需要将深度非弹性散射的高能偶极子描述与有限比约肯变量$x_B$下的标准光锥算符表述联系起来。这一关联对于统一高能物理中的不同理论框架至关重要。

Method: 论文在次领头阶（sub-eikonal order）层面进行分析，证明该阶修正由类夸克横向动量依赖（TMD-like）光锥算符主导。通过完全相空间积分，在包含极限下重构出非零$x_B$处的标准非局域夸克和螺旋度分布。同时，从领头扭度（leading-twist）非局域算符乘积展开的高能极限独立推导出相同的包含算符内容。

Result: 在$x_B=0$时，相应算符的高能演化方程可以重写为偶极子型算符组合。论文识别出一个算符基，其双局域构建块在零偶极子尺寸极限下消失，使小偶极子行为和领头对数结构变得明显。在双对数近似下，当横向相空间独立处理时，演化方程允许通常的混合纵向-横向贝塞尔型解；当横向相空间受纵向排序约束时，第二个对数转换为能量对数，在对称双对数区域恢复具有完整有限$N_c$色因子$C_F$的固定耦合Kirschner-Lipatov指数。

Conclusion: 论文成功建立了冲击波形式（shock-wave formalism）与非局域光锥展开（non-local light-cone expansion）之间的明确算符级桥梁，证明高能偶极子描述与标准光锥算符表述之间的联系在次领头阶已经出现，为连接小$x$框架与常规部分子描述提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Relating the high-energy dipole description of deep-inelastic scattering to the standard light-ray operator formulation at finite Bjorken $x_B$ is essential for connecting the small-$x$ framework to the usual partonic description. I demonstrate that this connection already emerges at the first sub-eikonal order. At the differential level, the first sub-eikonal correction is governed by a quark TMD-like light-ray operator. In the inclusive limit, after complete phase-space integration, it reconstructs the standard nonlocal quark and helicity distributions at nonzero $x_B$. I then show independently that the same inclusive operator content follows from the high-energy limit of the leading-twist non-local operator product expansion, thereby establishing an explicit operator-level bridge between the shock-wave formalism and the non-local light-cone expansion.
  I further discuss the high-energy evolution of the corresponding operators at $x_B=0$. Rewriting the evolution equations in terms of dipole-type operator combinations, I identify an operator basis whose bilocal building blocks vanish in the zero-dipole-size limit, making the small-dipole behavior and the leading-logarithmic structure manifest. In the double-logarithmic approximation the evolution equations admit the usual mixed longitudinal-transverse Bessel-type solution when the transverse phase space is treated independently. When the transverse phase space is instead constrained by longitudinal ordering, the second logarithm is converted into a logarithm of energy, and in the symmetric double-logarithmic regime one recovers the fixed-coupling Kirschner-Lipatov exponent with the full finite-$N_c$ color factor $C_F$.

</details>


### [49] [Role of the equivalence principle in gauge and axial symmetries of Yukawa coupling, and the strong CP problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30024)
*Konstantin V. Grigorishin*

TL;DR: 该论文论证了引力中的等效原理（equivalence principle）在标量场与费米子场的汤川耦合（Yukawa coupling）中的基础作用，并指出全局规范对称性系统中基布尔-祖雷克机制（Kibble-Zurek mechanism）的失效，同时探讨了不同真空态与畴壁（domain walls）的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在阐明等效原理在基本粒子相互作用中的核心地位，特别是对汤川耦合机制的影响，并探讨拓扑缺陷形成机制在特定对称性条件下的局限性。

Method: 通过理论分析论证等效原理对汤川耦合的基础性作用，并考察基布尔-祖雷克机制在仅具有全局规范对称性（global gauge symmetry）系统中的失效情况。

Result: 研究发现等效原理使强CP破坏（CP invariance violation）成为不可能，从而使轴子假说（axion hypothesis）变得多余；同时，不同真空态可被畴壁分隔。

Conclusion: 等效原理在基本相互作用中具有根本性作用，它限制了CP破坏的可能性，并影响了拓扑缺陷形成机制的有效性，最终使轴子假说成为不必要。

Abstract: It is demonstrated the fundamental role of the equivalence principle in gravity for the Yukawa coupling between scalar and fermion fields. The Kibble-Zurek mechanism for formation of topological defects as vortexes and monopoles breaks down in system with a global gauge symmetry only. At the same time, the different vacuums can occur, which are separated be domain walls. The equivalence principle makes the strong violation of CP invariance impossible. Thus the axion hypothesis becomes redundant.

### [50] [A Unified Theory of Deterministic Magnetic Switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29136)
*Xizhi Fu,Lei Han,Xi Liu,Cheng Song,Junwei Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个统一的理论框架，通过引入开关对称性（switching symmetry）概念，建立了确定性磁开关的通用条件：打破所有开关对称性，可通过不对称状态、不对称势垒和不对称力矩实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定性磁序参量（magnetic order parameters）的开关切换至关重要，因为它是磁存储器件中操纵信息状态的基础。现有研究缺乏统一的理论框架来解释和设计各种磁材料的开关机制。

Method: 研究提出了一个通用的理论框架，引入开关对称性概念，并建立了确定性开关的必要条件：打破所有开关对称性。这一条件可通过三种方式实现：不对称状态（asymmetric states）、不对称势垒（asymmetric barriers）和不对称力矩（asymmetric torques）。

Result: 该理论能够成功且普遍地解释所有已报道的确定性磁开关实验案例。同时，它为所有磁材料的新型开关器件提供了统一且简单的设计原则，无需复杂的模拟计算。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统一的理论框架，通过开关对称性概念为确定性磁开关提供了普适性解释和设计指导，显著简化了新型磁开关器件的开发流程。

Abstract: The deterministic switching of magnetic order parameters is critically important, as it forms the fundamental basis for manipulating information states in magnetic memory devices. This work presents a general theoretical framework that unifies the mechanisms of magnetic switching by introducing the concept of switching symmetry and establishing that the necessary condition for deterministic switching is the breaking of all switching symmetries, which can be achieved through asymmetric states, asymmetric barriers, and asymmetric torques. Our theory can successfully and universally explain all reported experimental cases of deterministic magnetic switching and provides unified and simple design principles for new switching devices of all magnetic materials without the need of complicated simulations.

</details>


### [51] [Femtosecond all-optical coherent control of spin polarization in altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29641)
*Kevin Jäckel,Holger Grisk,Niklas Dornquast,Maik Gaerner,Günter Reiss,Timo Kuschel,Jakob Walowski,Markus Münzenberg*

Main category: cond-mat.other

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）作为新兴的自旋电子学材料平台，兼具补偿磁序与类铁磁体的自旋劈裂电子能带特性。研究旨在探索RuO₂这一d波交变磁体材料的超快自旋动力学行为。

Method: 采用圆偏振超短激光脉冲（circularly polarized ultrashort laser pulses）激发RuO₂样品，通过时间分辨磁光克尔效应测量技术（time-resolved magneto-optical Kerr effect measurements）探测其超快自旋响应，该技术对表面和界面态具有本征敏感性。

Result: 观测到与传统铁磁体退磁动力学不同的复杂克尔旋转（complex Kerr rotation）相干贡献，该贡献在光-物质相互作用期间出现并持续约200飞秒。这种特征与拓扑绝缘体（topological insulators）自旋劈裂表面态中的自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking）和定向能带劈裂相关，受有限拉曼相干时间（finite Raman coherence time）支配。

Conclusion: 将观测到的相干响应解释为RuO₂中瞬态自旋极化表面态（transient spin-polarized surface states）的证据，这与交变磁体表面态的出现一致，对表面和界面处的自旋极化输运具有直接相关性。

Abstract: Altermagnets constitute an emerging materials platform for spintronic technologies by combining compensated magnetic order with ferromagnet-like spin-split electronic bands. Here, we investigate the proposed d-wave altermagnetic material RuO2 using circularly polarized ultrashort laser pulses. Time-resolved magneto-optical Kerr effect measurements, which are intrinsically sensitive to surface and interface states, reveal the ultrafast spin response of RuO2. In contrast to the demagnetization dynamics characteristic of conventional ferromagnets, we observe a distinct coherent contribution to the complex Kerr rotation that appears during the light-matter interaction and lasts for about 200 fs. Similar signatures have been associated with spin-momentum locking and directional band splitting in spin-split surface states of topological insulators as well as spin-orbit-coupled semiconductors. They are governed by a finite Raman coherence time. We interpret this coherent response as evidence for transient spin-polarized surface states in RuO2, consistent with the emergence of altermagnetic surface states that are directly relevant to spin-polarized transport at surfaces and interfaces.

### [52] [Operational Criterion for Imaginary-Time Reconstruction in Time-Resolved Electronic Circular Dichroism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29850)
*Christian Tantardini*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究建立了时间分辨电子圆二色性（time-resolved electronic circular dichroism）模拟中，延迟核（retarded kernel）何时可以从虚时间关联函数（imaginary-time correlator）重构的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间分辨电子圆二色性通常通过弱圆探针的实时传播来模拟。在线性响应范围内，这种探针测量泵浦制备系综在延迟τ时的推迟混合电磁化率（retarded mixed electric-magnetic susceptibility）。研究旨在确定何时这种推迟核可以从虚时间关联函数重构。

Method: 研究建立了推迟核重构的条件：仅当泵浦制备态足够平稳且近似满足相对于有效参考哈密顿量的久保-马丁-施温格（Kubo-Martin-Schwinger）条件时，这种替换才合理。为评估这一区域，引入了延迟分辨标量失配（delay-resolved scalar mismatch）来衡量更大和更小混合光谱之间的差异，并结合了克拉默斯-克勒尼希（Kramers-Kronig）关系和交换子求和规则检查。

Result: 在精确可解驱动模型上的基准测试识别了松原延拓（Matsubara continuation）准确的延迟窗口，以及需要真正非平衡处理的延迟窗口。研究提供了评估何时可以使用平衡方法（虚时间关联函数）以及何时需要非平衡处理的具体判据。

Conclusion: 研究建立了时间分辨电子圆二色性模拟中推迟核重构的严格条件，区分了可以使用松原延拓的平稳区域和需要非平衡处理的区域。提出的延迟分辨标量失配结合克拉默斯-克勒尼希和交换子求和规则检查，为评估模拟方法的适用性提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Time-resolved electronic circular dichroism is commonly simulated by real-time propagation with a weak circular probe. Within linear response, such a probe measures the retarded mixed electric--magnetic susceptibility of the pump-prepared ensemble at delay $τ$, while finite probe envelopes enter through a known transfer function. Here we establish when this retarded kernel can be reconstructed from an imaginary-time correlator. We show that this replacement is justified only when the pump-prepared state is sufficiently stationary and approximately Kubo--Martin--Schwinger compliant with respect to an effective reference Hamiltonian. To assess this regime, we introduce a delay-resolved scalar mismatch between the greater and lesser mixed spectra and combine it with Kramers--Kronig and commutator sum-rule checks. Benchmarks on an exactly solvable driven model identify the delay windows in which Matsubara continuation is accurate and those in which a genuinely nonequilibrium treatment is required.

### [53] [A Unified Multiscale Auxiliary PINN Framework for Generalized Phonon Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28932)
*Roberto Riganti,Luca Dal Negro*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多尺度辅助物理信息神经网络（MTNet）来求解广义声子辐射输运方程（GEPRT），克服了传统数值方法和标准PINNs在纳米尺度热输运模拟中的计算瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度热输运受声子玻尔兹曼输运方程（BTE）支配，但由于相空间高维度和散射碰撞算符内在非线性，模拟亚连续介质动力学计算成本极高。传统数值求解器和标准物理信息神经网络（PINNs）因确定性求积限制、弛豫时间近似（RTA）引入的人工热化效应以及多尺度谱偏差而难以处理这类积分-微分方程。

Method: 本文引入多尺度辅助物理信息神经网络（MTNet）求解广义声子辐射输运方程（GEPRT）。通过利用辅助公式，这个无网格框架将GEPRT重铸为完全微分系统，实现通过自动微分解析评估散射算符，并促进可扩展的多GPU并行化。为规避优化刚度，架构采用解耦的浅层神经网络，并明确受辐射平衡约束。

Result: MTNet通过模拟硅薄膜中的稳态跨平面输运进行验证，成功捕获了弹道-扩散区域和极端温度梯度（ΔT = 100 K）下的特征边界滑移，超越了标准线性化方法。此外，该框架成功解决了平板几何中的几何反问题，仅基于介观区域界面温度约束反演未知平板厚度。

Conclusion: MTNet为预测下一代纳米结构中的高保真动力学输运和提取材料特性建立了稳健、完全可微分的基础。

Abstract: Nanoscale thermal transport is governed by the phonon Boltzmann transport equation (BTE). However, simulating the sub-continuum dynamics remains computationally prohibitive due to the high dimensionality of the phase space and the intrinsic nonlinearity of the scattering collision operator. Traditional numerical solvers and standard physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) inherently struggle with these integro-differential equations due to deterministic quadrature limitations, artificial thermalization introduced by the relaxation time approximation (RTA), and multiscale spectral bias. This work introduces a multiscale auxiliary physics-informed neural network (MTNet) to solve the generalized equation of phonon radiative transfer (GEPRT). By leveraging an auxiliary formulation, this mesh-free framework recasts the GEPRT into a fully differential system, enabling the analytical evaluation of scattering operators via automatic differentiation and facilitating scalable multi-GPU parallelization. To circumvent optimization stiffness, the architecture employs a decoupled, shallow neural network explicitly constrained by radiative equilibrium. MTNet is validated by simulating steady-state cross-plane transport in a silicon thin film, successfully capturing ballistic-diffusive regimes and characteristic boundary slips across extreme temperature gradients ($ΔT = 100$ K) beyond the standard linearization approach. Furthermore, we show that our framework successfully solves a geometric inverse problem in a slab geometry, retrieving the unknown slab thickness based only on interface temperature constraints in the mesoscopic regime. Ultimately, MTNet establishes a robust, fully differentiable foundation for predicting high-fidelity kinetic transport and extracting material properties in next-generation nanostructures.

Here, we present a strategy to overcome this limitation by introducing an auxiliary cavity, which serves as a stationary near-field excitation source. Furthermore, real-time wave-packet dynamics of eigenstates provide direct evidence of ballistic spreading, confinement, and re-entrant transport, in agreement with the underlying spectral characteristics. These results establish a unified framework where diverse mean-field observables and dynamical probes consistently capture correlation-driven localization phenomena in quasiperiodic systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过求解林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation），获得了任意初始光子态的时间依赖非线性光电流；理论预测利用激子极化激元的量子几何位移电流（quantum-geometric shift current）散粒噪声可直接测量非经典光的QFI。

Result: 研究发现，无论入射光的量子态如何，积分电流仅依赖于平均光子数；然而散粒噪声的法诺因子（Fano factor）与光子数方差成正比，从而编码了QFI。数值计算验证了光学薛定谔猫态和压缩真空态下的这些关系。

Abstract: Quantum Fisher information (QFI) sets the ultimate precision of optical phase measurements and reveals multiphoton entanglement, but it is not accessible with conventional photodetection. We theoretically predict that a photodetector utilizing the shot noise of the quantum-geometric shift current of exciton polaritons can directly measure the QFI of nonclassical light. By solving the Lindblad equation, we obtain the time-dependent nonlinear photocurrent for an arbitrary initial photon state. It turns out that, regardless of the quantum state of the incident light, the integrated current depends only on the mean photon number. In stark contrast, the shot noise retains the quantum information: its Fano factor is proportional to the photon number variance and therefore encodes the QFI. Numerical calculations confirm these relations for illumination with optical Schrödinger cat and squeezed vacuum states. Quantum correlations in nonclassical light, usually hidden from direct detection, become observable in the form of shift current shot noise

*Yunhyeon Jeong,Akinori Kamiyama,John N. Moore,Takaaki Mano,Ken-ichi Sasaki,Yuuki Sugiyama,Tokiro Numasawa,Masahiro Hotta,Go Yusa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究利用时间分辨光致发光显微光谱技术，首次实现了对ν=1/3分数量子霍尔边缘激发的时空成像，揭示了栅极控制的多路径传播动力学特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子霍尔边缘激发（quantum Hall edge excitations）的低能行为可用手性共形场论（chiral conformal field theory）描述，是模拟时空实验的理想平台。然而，在实际静电势景观中建立可控的边缘动力学对实验至关重要，且一直面临技术挑战。

Method: 采用具有约100 ps分辨率的频闪时间分辨光致发光显微光谱技术（stroboscopic time-resolved photoluminescence microscopy and spectroscopy），对ν=1/3分数量子霍尔器件中栅极控制的多路径边缘激发动力学进行时空成像。

Result: 通过调节控制栅极定义的势景观，观察到在台面定义路径和栅极定义路径之间的切换，并识别出单个激发可访问多个路径的中间状态。下游位置的时间分辨测量显示栅极依赖的到达时间和显著的时间展宽，表明传播动力学受局域限制强烈影响，在多路径景观中变得更具色散性。此外，观察到长程横向光学响应延伸至体区数十微米，并持续超过200 μm下游距离，与边缘磁等离激元（edge magnetoplasmon）的近场分量一致。

Conclusion: 该研究为分数量子霍尔体系中可控多路径边缘动力学提供了直接实验途径，为设计非平衡和基于干涉的实验以及未来在量子霍尔边缘系统中的模拟时空研究提供了平台。

Abstract: Quantum Hall edge excitations, whose low-energy behavior admits a chiral conformal-field-theory description, are a promising platform for engineered dynamical experiments, including analog-spacetime proposals. However, establishing their edge dynamics in realistic electrostatic landscapes is essential for controlled dynamical experiments and has remained experimentally challenging. Here we report spatiotemporal imaging of gate-controlled multipath dynamics of edge excitations in a $ν= 1/3$ fractional quantum Hall device using stroboscopic time-resolved photoluminescence microscopy and spectroscopy with $\sim$100-ps resolution. By tuning a control-gate-defined potential landscape, we observe switching between mesa-defined and gate-defined trajectories and identify an intermediate regime in which a single launched excitation accesses multiple pathways. Time-resolved measurements at downstream locations reveal gate-dependent arrival times and pronounced temporal broadening, showing that the propagation dynamics are strongly modified by the local confinement and become increasingly dispersive in a multipath landscape. We further observe a long-range transverse optical response extending tens of micrometers into the bulk and persisting over distances exceeding 200 $μ$m downstream, consistent with the near-field component of an edge magnetoplasmon. These results establish direct experimental access to controllable multipath edge dynamics in the fractional quantum Hall regime and suggest a platform for engineered nonequilibrium and interference-based experiments, as well as future analog-spacetime studies in quantum Hall edge systems.

### [62] [Thermodynamic Multipoles and Dissipative Conductivities in Metallic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29267)
*Takumi Sato,Satoru Hayami*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文扩展了多极子（multipole）框架，通过关注费米面对热力学多极矩的贡献，建立了与金属中耗散输运响应的直接联系，揭示了电导率在相应多极子贡献为零时出现极值的新规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多极子为从对称性角度描述量子材料的电子结构提供了系统框架，但现有的热力学多极矩与物理响应的关系仅限于平衡绝缘系统中的无耗散响应。本文旨在将这一框架扩展到金属系统中的耗散输运响应。

Method: 在启发式（heuristic）层面上扩展多极子框架，重点关注费米面对热力学多极矩的贡献，建立这些贡献与金属特征性耗散输运响应（包括电荷和自旋电导率）的直接关系。

Result: 研究发现电导率在相应费米面对多极子的贡献为零时出现极值（通常为最大值）：电荷电导率在电四极子（electric quadrupole）贡献为零时达到极值，自旋电导率在磁八极子（magnetic octupole）贡献为零时达到极值。

Conclusion: 这些发现揭示了热力学多极矩先前被忽视的方面，为理解金属系统中的耗散输运开辟了新的视角，建立了多极子框架与耗散输运响应之间的直接联系。

Abstract: Multipoles provide a systematic framework for describing the electronic structures of quantum materials from a symmetry perspective. Thermodynamic multipole moments in crystalline solids exhibit direct microscopic connections to certain allowed physical responses beyond symmetry; however, such relations have thus far been limited to dissipationless responses in equilibrium insulating systems. Here, this framework is extended at a heuristic level by focusing on the Fermi-surface contributions to thermodynamic multipole moments. These contributions establish direct relations to dissipative transport responses characteristic of metals, including charge and spin conductivities. A key consequence is that the conductivities exhibit extrema, typically maxima, at chemical potentials where the corresponding Fermi-surface contributions to the multipoles vanish, specifically, the electric quadrupole for charge conductivity and the magnetic octupole for spin conductivity. These findings uncover a previously overlooked aspect of thermodynamic multipole moments, opening a new perspective on dissipative transport in metallic systems.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过在强电场（strong E）和固定电荷密度（fixed n）条件下对扭曲双层石墨烯进行氢化处理，利用大扭转角（large twist angle）解耦两层电子系统，实现独立的电荷密度控制。

Result: 实现了层选择性导体-绝缘体转变，伴随质子通过双层的传输，能够在器件中构建多个并行可配置逻辑门（parallel and configurable logic gates）。

Abstract: Recent work investigated graphene's hydrogenation with independent control of the electric field, E, and charge density, n, in the crystal and showed that the process is controlled by n. Here, we demonstrate layer-selective conductor-insulator transitions in twisted bilayer graphene, driven by hydrogenation at fixed n under strong E. This process is accompanied by proton transport through the bilayer, enabling several parallel and configurable logic gates in the devices. Selectivity arises because the large twist angle decouples the two layers' electronic systems, enabling independent control of their charge densities. Polarisation by the field then induces a charge imbalance at fixed total n, triggering hydrogenation when one of the layers' charge densities reaches the threshold for monolayer hydrogenation. Our results introduce a new type of electrode-electrolyte interface in which electrochemical processes are controlled with two decoupled 2D electron gases, opening new design opportunities for energy and information processing devices.

### [64] [Heat Conduction and Energy Relaxation in an InAs Nanowire Approaching the Clean One-Dimensional Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29358)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用混合半导体-超导体（hybrid semiconductor-superconductor）架构，利用原位生长的量子点温度计（quantum dot thermometer）测量局部电子温度，并在纳米线不同位置施加可控焦耳加热以探测亚开尔文温度下的温度梯度。

Result: 基于一维热输运模型计算得出电子-声子热流（electron-phonon heat flow）标度为Q_{e-ph} ∝ T^2.6，与一维电子气（one-dimensional electron gas）耦合声子浴的T^3理论预测高度一致；进一步估算出特征长度l_{eq} = 370 nm，超过此尺度后声子介导的热输运在纳米线中占主导地位。

Abstract: We investigate heat conduction and energy relaxation in an InAs semiconductor nanowire using a hybrid semiconductor-superconductor architecture. Local electronic temperatures are measured with an in-situ grown quantum dot thermometer, while controlled Joule heating is applied at different locations along the wire to probe temperature gradients at sub-kelvin temperatures. With a onedimensional heat transport model, we calculate an electron-phonon heat flow that scales as Q_{e-ph} \propto T^2.6, which is in close agreement with the T^3 dependence predicted for a clean one-dimensional electron gas coupled to a phonon bath. We further estimate a characteristic length l_{eq} = 370 nm, beyond this length scale, phonon-mediated heat transport dominates over heat conduction in our nanowire. Our results provide a quantitative measure of energy relaxation mechanisms in a onedimensional semiconductor and provide a framework for studying heat flow in low-dimensional nanostructures.

*Hiroki Isobe*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子霍尔效应通常表现出线性电流-霍尔电压关系，但该研究旨在探讨在空间不均匀电场条件下非线性关系的可能性。研究动机源于对传统线性关系的挑战，特别是在非均匀电场环境中。

Method: 首先基于伽利略不变性（Galilean invariance）论证线性I-V_H关系的成立条件，然后采用量子霍尔液体的流体动力学描述处理轴对称电场。该方法通过分析弯曲流中的离心力和涡度引起的密度梯度来研究非线性响应。

Result: 研究发现，在空间不均匀电场条件下，量子霍尔效应可能出现非线性电子响应。这种非线性源于弯曲流动中的离心力以及涡度引起的密度梯度，从而破坏了传统的线性I-V_H关系。

Conclusion: 量子霍尔效应中的线性电流-霍尔电压关系并非普遍成立，在空间不均匀电场条件下可能出现非线性响应。这种非线性源于流体动力学效应，包括离心力和密度梯度的影响。

Abstract: The quantum Hall effect realizes a quantized Hall resistance $R_{xy} = h/(νe^2)$ whereas the longitudinal resistance vanishes. The quantized value consists of the fundamental physical quantities, the elementary charge $e$ and the Planck constant $h$, along with an integer or fractional constant $ν$. High precision measurements of $R_{xy}$ allude to a linear relation between the applied current $I$ and the Hall voltage $V_\mathrm{H}$. Here, we argue that a nonlinear relation between $I$ and $V_\mathrm{H}$ could arise when the electric field is spatially inhomogeneous. We first discuss that the linear $I$-$V_\mathrm{H}$ relation holds with Galilean invariance. Then we consider a hydrodynamic description of a quantum Hall liquid to deal with an axially symmetric electric field. It reveals a nonlinear electronic response arising from the centrifugal force exerted on a curved flow and the density gradient invoked by vorticity.

### [68] [Intrinsic Temporal Coherence Governs Heat Transport of Zone-Folded Phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29642)
*Xiaoyu Huang,Yuxiang Ni,Zhongwei Zhang,Yangyu Guo,Marc Bescond,Masahiro Nomura,Sebastian Volz*

TL;DR: 该研究从时间相干性（temporal coherence）角度探究了超晶格（superlattice）中的声子输运，发现折叠声子模式（folded phonon modes）的本征相干性主导了超短周期超晶格的热导率增强，而传统Wigner输运方程（Wigner transport equation）仅显示带折叠（band folding）的次要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究主要关注空间声子相干性（spatial phonon coherence）通过带折叠（band folding）对周期性结构异常热导率的影响，本研究旨在从时间相干性（temporal coherence）这一被忽视的视角探究声子输运机制。

Method: 采用模式分辨分析（mode-resolved analyses）量化时间相干贡献，阐明石墨烯/六方氮化硼超晶格（graphene/hexagonal boron nitride superlattices）中声子相干时间（coherence time）与寿命（lifetime）在热传导中的相互作用。

Result: 研究发现折叠声子模式（folded phonon modes）的本征相干性（intrinsic coherence）主导了超短周期超晶格（ultrashort-period superlattices）的热导率增强；而Wigner输运方程（Wigner transport equation）仅显示带折叠（band folding）对热导率的次要影响。

Conclusion: 时间相干性（temporal coherence）构成了先前被忽视但基本的热传导通道，扩展了空间相干输运的传统图像，深化了对超晶格（superlattices）中声子动力学的理解；包含与不包含时间相干性的模型在温度依赖性上的预测差异提供了可证伪的实验特征。

Abstract: While spatial phonon coherence manifested through band folding is believed to be a key factor governing the anomalous thermal conductivity of periodic structures, we investigate phonon transport from the perspective of temporal coherence. Using mode-resolved analyses, we quantify temporal coherent contributions and elucidate the interplay between phonon coherence time and lifetime in heat conduction of graphene/hexagonal boron nitride superlattices. We find that intrinsic coherence of folded phonon modes dominates the enhancement in ultrashort-period superlattices. In contrast, Wigner transport equation yields only a minor effect of band folding on thermal conductivity. The predictions in temperature dependence of models with and without temporal coherence provide a falsifiable experimental signature of this effect. Temporal coherence therefore constitutes a previously overlooked but fundamental channel for heat conduction, extending the conventional picture of spatially coherent transport and deepening the understanding of phonon dynamics in superlattices.

### [69] [Nonlinear response theory for orbital photocurrent in semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29653)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期关于自旋和轨道自由度非线性响应的理论研究发现了自旋和轨道的光电流类似物，这些响应在表征拓扑材料和实际应用中具有潜力。因此需要发展一个通用理论来系统研究这些非线性响应。

Method: 论文发展了一个计算半导体中自旋和轨道电流的通用理论框架，并应用于Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang（BHZ）模型和Luttinger模型，研究其中的光学响应特性，特别是非线性轨道响应和拓扑相变。

We study the evolution of optical responses at the topological phase transition and how they manifest. In addition, we find that the relaxation time dependence of the orbital conductivity is somewhat distinct from that of the photocurrent. The theory is straightforwardly applicable to complex models of real materials, allowing quantitative predictions of the nonlinear responses of orbital and spin.

### [70] [Fano Resonances in Mismatched C$_3$N Nanoribbon Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29662)
*Andor Che Papior,Van-Truong Tran,Roberto D'Agosta,Stefan Kurth*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析宽度不匹配的C₃N锯齿形纳米带结（mismatched C₃N zigzag nanoribbon junctions），揭示了边缘态与局域界面态耦合产生的显著法诺共振（Fano resonances），为调控量子干涉输运提供了可调谐平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究宽度不匹配的C₃N锯齿形纳米带结（mismatched C₃N zigzag nanoribbon junctions）为探究涉及边缘态输运的量子干涉效应提供了有用平台。关键动机在于理解界面局域态与边缘态之间的耦合机制及其对输运性质的影响。

Method: 在紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）框架下，研究通过施加外部栅极电势（external gate potential）选择性地将边缘态能带移动到局域界面态的能量范围内。该方法实现了边缘态与局域界面态之间的可控耦合。

Result: 边缘态与局域界面态的耦合在态密度和透射谱中产生了显著的法诺共振（Fano resonances），其线形可由经典法诺公式（canonical Fano formula）精确描述。结的几何不匹配不仅决定了共振数量，还控制了其不对称线形的能量取向。

Conclusion: 不匹配的C₃N纳米结（mismatched C₃N nanojunctions）构成了一个可调谐且稳健的平台，可用于工程化干涉驱动的输运现象。该平台通过外部栅压调控边缘态与界面态的耦合，实现对量子干涉效应的精细控制。

Abstract: Mismatched junctions formed by two C$_3$N zigzag nanoribbons of different widths provide a useful setting for studying quantum interference effects involving edge state transport. A crucial ingredient for this interference to appear is, besides the presence of edge states, the formation of localized interface states at the mismatched interface of the junction. At the level of a tight-binding model it is shown that, by means of an external gate potential, one of the edge state energy bands can selectively be shifted into the energy range of the localized interface states. The resulting coupling between the edge and localized interface states gives rise to pronounced Fano resonances in both the density of states and the transmission spectrum with line shapes well described by the canonical Fano formula. Furthermore, it is found that the geometrical mismatch of the junction not only determines the number of resonances but also the energetic orientation of their asymmetric line shapes. These results identify mismatched C$_3$N nanojunctions as a tunable and robust platform for engineering interference-driven transport.

### [71] [Theory of quantum decoherence and its application to anomalous Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29690)
*Xian-Peng Zhang,Yan-Qing Feng,Haiwen Liu,Wanxiang Feng,Yugui Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相干量子现象的出现需要最小化退相干，但自旋轨道耦合铁磁体中退相干的微观机制仍不清楚，定量处理长期面临挑战。解决这一基础重要且技术关键的问题对于设计功能量子器件至关重要。

Method: 开发了一个量子主方程（quantum master-equation）框架，采用非对角密度矩阵的一般ansatz，同时捕捉电场驱动的相干性和杂质散射诱导的退相干。这一统一方法扩展了玻尔兹曼输运方程以纳入退相干效应。

Result: 退相干重塑了本征反常霍尔效应（intrinsic anomalous Hall effect），揭示了本征和外在区域之间的清晰交叉。发现了一个先前未被认识的外在贡献：与量子退相干紧密相关的二阶散射过程，该过程在根本上不同于斜散射（skew scattering）和侧跳（side jump）机制，且比斜散射机制显著更重要。

Conclusion: 退相干是量子输运中的关键要素，该工作为玻尔兹曼输运方程提供了系统扩展以纳入退相干，对鲁棒自旋电子学功能具有广泛意义。

Abstract: Coherent quantum phenomena can only emerge when decoherence is minimized, and mastery over decoherence is technologically crucial for designing and operating functional quantum devices. However, its microscopic mechanisms in spin-orbit-coupled ferromagnets remain elusive, and quantitative treatments have long been challenging. To solve this fundamentally significant and technologically crucial problem, we develop a quantum master-equation framework with a general ansatz for the off-diagonal density matrix that simultaneously captures electric-field-driven coherence and impurity-scattering-induced decoherence. This unified approach enables quantitative analysis of how decoherence reshapes the intrinsic anomalous Hall effect, revealing a clear crossover between intrinsic and extrinsic regimes. Remarkably, we identify a previously unrecognized extrinsic contribution: a second-order scattering process tightly relative to quantum decoherence-that is fundamentally distinct from both skew scattering and side jump mechanisms, yet substantially more significant than the skew scattering mechanism. Our work establishes decoherence as a key element in quantum transport and provides a systematic extension of the Boltzmann transport equation to incorporate decoherence, with broad implications for robust spintronic functionality.

### [72] [Magnetically Induced Switching-Current Jumps in InAs/Al Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29757)
*Ofelia Durante,Roberta Citro,Elia Strambini,Valeria Demontis,Mirko Rocci,Alessandro Braggio,Sergio Battiato,Valentina Zannier,Lucia Sorba,Francesco Giazotto,Claudio Guarcello*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究纳米线约瑟夫森结中磁重构的干涉测量特性，通过切换电流跳变探测内在磁重排过程，为理解弱连接中的磁构型动力学提供实验依据。

Method: 使用n型掺杂InAs/Al纳米线约瑟夫森结作为干涉测量探针，在30-900 mK温度范围内追踪特征磁场尺度，通过测量切换电流模式的变化来探测局部磁织构（magnetic texture）的亚稳态构型。

Result: 在T=30 mK时观察到类似夫琅禾费（Fraunhofer-like）的调制，I_sw(0)≈0.24 μA，在|B|≈3 mT处出现分支间的急剧转变，ΔI_sw≈0.13 μA。跳变磁场基本与温度无关，而超导临界场随温度降低，符合薄铝膜预期。尖锐不连续性、扫描方向不对称性和重复性表明存在亚稳态磁构型间的雪崩式切换（avalanche-like switching）。

Conclusion: 在有效场框架内，每次磁重构都会修改局部磁场偏移，从而重塑干涉响应并导致切换电流模式的急剧重组，揭示了局部磁织构与弱连接之间的直接耦合机制。

Abstract: We report Barkhausen-like switching at millitesla fields in an $n$-doped InAs/Al nanowire Josephson junction, which serves as an interferometric probe of intrinsic magnetic reconfigurations, as evidenced by discrete switching-current jumps. At $T=30$~mK the device displays a Fraunhofer-like modulation with $I_{\mathrm{sw}}(0)\approx 0.24~μ\mathrm{A}$ and an abrupt transition at $|B|\approx 3~\mathrm{mT}$ between two branches differing by $ΔI_{\mathrm{sw}}\approx 0.13~μ\mathrm{A}$. By tracking the characteristic field scales from $30$ to $900$~mK, we find that the jump field is essentially temperature-independent, whereas the superconducting critical field decreases with temperature, as expected for thin Al films. The sharp discontinuity, sweep-direction asymmetry, and reproducibility across repeated scans point to avalanche-like switching between metastable magnetic configurations of the local magnetic texture, which are directly coupled to the weak link. Within an effective-field framework, each reconfiguration modifies a local field offset, thereby reshaping the interference response and leading to an abrupt reorganization of the switching-current pattern.

### [73] [Emergence of Non-Hermitian Magic Angles and Topological Phase Transitions in Twisted Bilayer $α$-$T_3$ Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29779)
*Shaina Gandhi,Gourab Paul,Srijata Lahiri,Saurabh Basu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非厄米（non-Hermitian）扭曲双层α-T₃晶格中的平带特性与拓扑相变。研究发现非互易（non-reciprocal）跳跃将传统单一魔角（magic angle）分裂为三个非厄米魔角（NHMAs），并揭示了非厄米性对拓扑特征的破坏作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索非厄米性对扭曲双层α-T₃晶格中平带性质和拓扑相变的影响。通过引入Hatano-Nelson型非对称跳跃（asymmetric hopping）和六方氮化硼衬底提供的交错子晶格质量（staggered sublattice mass），旨在理解非厄米性如何改变该莫尔（moiré）系统的拓扑特性。

Method: 研究方法包括在扭曲双层α-T₃晶格中引入Hatano-Nelson型非互易跳跃，并利用对齐的六方氮化硼衬底提供交错子晶格质量。通过映射整个莫尔布里渊区（moiré Brillouin zone）的复本征谱（complex eigenspectrum），计算直接带隙（direct band gap）和双正交陈数（biorthogonal Chern number）来表征拓扑相。

Result: 研究发现非互易跳跃将传统单一魔角分裂为三个非厄米魔角，这些NHMAs支持完美隔离的平带（flat bands）。随着非厄米参数强度增加，散射的能量本征值凝聚成闭合环状结构，表明非平凡点隙拓扑（point-gap topology）和非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）的出现。系统在弱非厄米性下向更高拓扑相转变，但强非厄米性导致带隙闭合边界合并及其拓扑电荷相互湮灭。

Conclusion: 结论表明非厄米性在破坏该莫尔系统稳健拓扑特征方面起关键作用。强非厄米性导致平庸带隙闭合和中间拓扑相的完全抑制，证实了非厄米性从根本上改变了系统的拓扑特性。

Abstract: We investigate the flat-band properties and topological phase transitions in a non-Hermitian twisted bilayer $α-T_3$ lattice. Here, non-Hermiticity is introduced via Hatano-Nelson-type asymmetric hopping, while an aligned hexagonal boron nitride substrate provides a staggered sublattice mass to the system. We find that the introduction of non-reciprocal hopping splits the conventional single magic angle into three distinct non-Hermitian magic angles (NHMAs). Unlike the exceptional magic angles driven by spectral singularities, these NHMAs host perfectly isolated flat bands where the real and imaginary parts of the bandwidth simultaneously vanish. By mapping the complex eigenspectrum across the moiré Brillouin zone, we show that the scattered energy eigenvalues coalesce into well-defined, closed loop-like structures as the non-Hermitian parameter strength increases, indicating emergence of a nontrivial point-gap topology and hence the non-Hermitian skin effect. Furthermore, we characterize the topological phases by computing the direct band gap and the biorthogonal Chern number. While the system exhibits a transition to a higher topological phase at weak non-Hermiticity, we demonstrate that stronger non-Hermiticity drives the gap-closing boundaries to merge and their topological charges to mutually annihilate. This convergence results in a trivial gap closing and a complete suppression of the intermediate topological phase, confirming that non-Hermiticity fundamentally plays a crucial role with regard to destabilizing the robust topological features of this moiré system.

</details>

*Michael P. Adams,Elizabeth M. Jefremovas,Andreas Michels*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了二维自旋翻转小角中子散射（SANS）模式的对称性分辨分类方法，针对含有磁性涡旋态的球形纳米颗粒稀薄系综。基于线性涡旋近似和轴向对称的涡旋轴分布，研究展示了散射模式可组织为四个不同的对称性区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在对含有磁性涡旋态的球形纳米颗粒稀薄系综产生的二维自旋翻转小角中子散射（spin-flip SANS）模式进行系统分类。通过分析散射图案的对称性特征，为实验偏振SANS数据提供紧凑且模型透明的分类框架。

Method: 采用线性涡旋近似（linear vortex ansatz）和轴向对称的涡旋轴分布，推导出取向平均的自旋翻转SANS截面的解析表达式。通过分析参数空间中的对称性边界，建立了涡旋振幅和涡旋轴分布宽度构成的紧凑对称性景观（symmetry landscape）。

Result: 研究识别出四种不同的对称性区域：四重各向异性对应相干场对齐磁化，垂直和水平二重各向异性分别对应对齐和均匀分布的涡旋系综，以及分离两个二重区域的各向同性环状条件。与非线性涡旋剖面的比较表明这些对称性区域对涡旋核心的详细径向结构具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 角各向异性主要受旋转对称性和涡旋轴的统计分布控制，为实验偏振SANS数据提供了紧凑且模型透明的分类框架。该对称性分类方法对涡旋核心的详细径向结构具有鲁棒性，突显了对称性原理在理解复杂磁性纳米结构散射模式中的重要性。

Abstract: We present a symmetry-resolved classification of two-dimensional spin-flip small-angle neutron scattering (SANS) patterns arising from dilute ensembles of spherical nanoparticles hosting magnetic vortex states. Based on a linear vortex ansatz with an axially symmetric distribution of vortex axes and the corresponding analytical expression for the orientationally averaged spin-flip SANS cross section, we show that the angular scattering patterns organize into four distinct symmetry regimes: a four-fold anisotropy corresponding to coherent field-aligned magnetization, vertical and horizontal two-fold anisotropies associated with aligned and isotropically distributed vortex ensembles, and an isotropic ring-like condition separating the two two-fold regimes. The corresponding symmetry boundaries are obtained analytically and define a compact symmetry landscape in the parameter space of vortex amplitude and vortex-axis distribution width. Comparison with a nonlinear vortex profile shows that these symmetry regions are robust with respect to the detailed radial structure of the vortex core. The angular anisotropies are therefore governed primarily by rotational symmetry and by the statistical distribution of vortex axes, providing a compact and model-transparent classification framework of experimental polarized SANS data.

Abstract: Disorder masks much of the rich physics in two-dimensional electronic systems, with charged impurities often the limiting factor. ### [77] [Negative Electronic Friction and Non-Markovianity in Nonequilibrium Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29951)
*Riley J. Preston,Samuel L. Rudge,Daniel S. Kosov,Michael Thoss*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非平衡条件下分子与金属表面相互作用时，负电子摩擦（negative electronic friction）与非马尔可夫效应（non-Markovian effects）之间的联系，揭示了导致负马尔可夫电子摩擦的机制同样会引入显著的非马尔可夫贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明分子与金属表面在非平衡条件下相互作用时，负电子摩擦与非马尔可夫效应之间的内在联系。当前对非绝热振动动力学（nonadiabatic vibrational dynamics）的理解需要更深入地探讨这些相互作用的机制。

Method: 通过研究包含振动耦合供体-受体模型（vibrationally coupled donor-acceptor model）的分子纳米结（molecular nanojunction）中的非平衡电荷输运（nonequilibrium charge transport）。采用数值精确的完全量子层次运动方程（hierarchical equations of motion）模拟进行验证。

Result: 研究发现导致负马尔可夫电子摩擦的通用非平衡机制同样会引入显著的非马尔可夫贡献。这些非马尔可夫效应对非平衡动力学具有重要影响，甚至会影响所得朗之万方程（Langevin equation）的稳定性。

Conclusion: 负电子摩擦与非马尔可夫效应在分子-金属表面非平衡相互作用中存在内在联系，这一发现对于理解非绝热振动动力学和分子纳米结中的能量输运机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: We address the connection between negative electronic friction and non-Markovian effects in the nonadiabatic vibrational dynamics of molecules interacting with metal surfaces under nonequilibrium conditions. We show that a generic nonequilibrium mechanism leading to negative Markovian electronic friction, where molecular vibrations couple directly to inelastic electronic transitions, also introduces significant non-Markovian contributions to the electronic friction. To demonstrate these ideas, we investigate nonequilibrium charge transport through a molecular nanojunction containing a vibrationally coupled donor-acceptor model, where negative electronic friction reflects driving of the vibrational mode beyond standard Joule heating. By comparison to numerically exact, fully quantum hierarchical equations of motion simulations, we verify that these non-Markovian effects have a significant impact on the nonequilibrium dynamics and even on the stability of the resulting Langevin equation.

### [78] [Nodal degeneration of chiral algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.30037)
*Elchanan Nafcha*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文定义了稳定曲线族上任意通用分解代数（universal factorization algebra）相关的分解代数层，并证明了相应手征同调（chiral homology）层的粘合公式，推广了顶点代数层及共形块（conformal blocks）粘合的Verlinde公式。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于推广顶点代数层和共形块粘合的Verlinde公式，为稳定曲线族上的通用分解代数建立更一般的理论框架。

Method: 方法包括定义稳定曲线族上任意通用分解代数相关的分解代数层，并证明相应手征同调层的粘合公式。

Result: 主要结果是建立了分解代数层的粘合公式，该结果推广了顶点代数层及共形块粘合的Verlinde公式。

Conclusion: 结论表明该工作成功推广了顶点代数层理论，为稳定曲线族上通用分解代数的研究提供了新的粘合公式框架。

### [79] [Copy-Spread-Annihilate Dynamics in Degree-Assortative Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29833)
*Yan Hao,Daniel J. Graham,Marc-Thorsten Hütt*

Here we introduce Copy-Spread-Annihilate dynamics, a minimal synchronous broadcasting model with annihilation. We show that signal lifetimes vary non-monotonically with assortativity and are maximized near neutral assortativity, where hub-driven amplification is strong but annihilation via short cycles is still limited. Result: 该方法自然地导出了这些函数的正交性关系（orthogonality relations）和双谱性质（bispectral properties），为两类函数提供了统一的代数解释和数学性质推导。

### [81] [Sampling at intermediate temperatures is optimal for training large language models in protein structure prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29529)
*L. Ghiringhelli,A. Zambon,G. Tiana*

TL;DR: 本研究采用统计力学框架分析蛋白质序列数据训练的transformer模型参数空间，通过朗之万动力学在不同温度下采样损失景观，揭示了transformer在蛋白质结构预测中优异性能的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解transformer模型在蛋白质结构预测中表现优异的机制，通过分析其参数空间特性来探索与常规前馈网络的差异。

Method: 采用统计力学（statistical mechanics）框架，通过朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）在不同温度下采样transformer模型的损失景观（loss landscape），并分析嵌入维度（embedding dimension）对参数保守性的影响。

Result: 研究发现transformer缺乏类似一阶相变（first-order-like transition）的损失变化，在中间温度范围具有良好学习特性；当嵌入维度最优时，多数层参数高度保守；注意力矩阵（attention matrix）在较高温度和较大嵌入维度下能更好地预测蛋白质接触图（contact maps）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了transformer在蛋白质序列建模中的独特学习机制，提供了确定最优嵌入维度的操作化方法，并表明注意力机制在特定条件下能有效捕捉蛋白质结构信息。

Abstract: We investigate the parameter space of transformer models trained on protein sequence data using a statistical mechanics framework, sampling the loss landscape at varying temperatures by Langevin dynamics to characterize the low-loss manifold and understand the mechanisms underlying the superior performance of transformers in protein structure prediction. We find that, at variance with feedforward networks, the lack of a first--order--like transition in the loss of the transformer produces a range of intermediate temperatures with good learning properties. We show that the parameters of most layers are highly conserved at these temperatures if the dimension of the embedding is optimal, and we provide an operative way to find this dimension. Finally, we show that the attention matrix is more predictive of the contact maps of the protein at higher temperatures and for higher dimensions of the embedding than those optimal for learning.

### [82] [The different localisation properties of the eigenmodes of the Laplacian and adjacency matrix of 2D random geometric graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29611)
*Luca Schaefer,Barbara Drossel*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值对角化比较了二维随机几何图中拉普拉斯矩阵和邻接矩阵的特征谱与特征模的局域化性质，分析了系统尺寸和连通性对结果的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于比较二维随机几何图（2D random geometric graphs）中拉普拉斯矩阵（Laplacian matrix）和邻接矩阵（adjacency matrix）的特征谱与特征模局域化性质的差异，理解不同矩阵表示对网络性质分析的影响。

Method: 研究方法包括对两种矩阵进行数值对角化（numerical diagonalization），针对不同系统尺寸和连通性参数，分析足够大的系统集合的谱分布、参与率（participation ratio）的概率分布及其与特征值的关系。

Result: 研究结果显示，对于足够大的系统尺寸，邻接矩阵的所有特征模都是局域化的（localised），而拉普拉斯矩阵由于守恒定律（conservation law）总是产生一小部分跨越系统的模，导致参与率概率分布及其与特征值关系中出现幂律尾部（power-law tails）。

Conclusion: 通过分离有限系统尺寸、平均度、组件尺寸分布和网络模体（network motifs）的影响，该研究为数据提供了全面理解，揭示了两种矩阵表示在特征模局域化性质上的本质差异。

Abstract: We compare the spectrum and the localisation properties of the eigenmodes of the Laplacian and the adjacency matrix of 2D random geometric graphs, using numerical diagonalization of these matrices for different system sizes and connectivities. For sufficiently large ensembles of systems, we evaluate the spectrum, the probability distribution of the participation ratio and the relation between participation ratios and eigenvalues. While all eigenmodes of the adjacency matrix are localised for sufficiently large system sizes, the Laplacian matrix always leads to a small proportion of system-spanning modes due to a conservation law, and therefore to power-law tails in the probability distribution of the participation ratio and its relation to the eigenvalues. By disentangling the effects of finite system size, of mean degree, of component size distribution, and of network motifs, we provide a thorough understanding of the data.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用生成模型在全局拓扑约束下对势序列进行逆向设计（inverse design）。基于生成结果提取的物理原理，手动构建了仅由两个S块组成的最小异质结构。

Result: 生成的势序列展现出由拓扑边界层和宏观S稠密域组成的特征结构，在保持拓扑性质的同时实现了增强的局域化（ξ=0.85）。最小异质结构进一步将局域长度降低至ξ=0.75。

Conclusion: 该研究为强局域化拓扑态提供了紧凑的设计原理，通过逆向设计和最小异质结构实现了拓扑π模的空间限制增强。

Abstract: This study investigates the spatial confinement of topological $π$-modes in one-dimensional chiral-symmetric systems. In conventional periodic and quasiperiodic structures, edge-mode wave functions inevitably penetrate the bulk. To suppress this, inverse design of a potential sequence is performed using a generative model under a global topological constraint. The generated sequence reveals a characteristic structure consisting of a topological boundary layer and a macroscopic S-dense domain, leading to enhanced confinement ($ξ=0.85$) while preserving topology. Based on the physical principle extracted from this result, a minimal heterostructure composed of only two S-blocks is manually constructed, which further reduces the localization length to $ξ=0.75$. These results provide a compact design principle for strongly localized topological states.

### [84] [Pattern Expansion of Spin Glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29984)
*Mutian Shen,Zohar Nussinov,Yang-Yu Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将自旋玻璃哈密顿量展开为Mattis相互作用的系统方法，揭示了短程Edwards-Anderson模型与平均场Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型之间的本质差异。该方法通过迭代提取耦合矩阵中的模式，将原系统展开为类Hopfield模型加残差系统，并展示了SK模型的自相似性以及EA模型中的超低能激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在理解短程Edwards-Anderson（EA）模型与平均场Sherrington-Kirkpatrick（SK）自旋玻璃之间的根本差异。通过开发系统性的展开方法，为理解这两种模型的不同物理特性提供新的视角。

Method: 提出了一种将一般自旋玻璃哈密顿量按Mattis相互作用展开的系统方法。该方法通过迭代提取耦合矩阵中的模式，将原始自旋玻璃系统展开为类Hopfield模型（一系列Mattis相互作用）加上残差系统。

Result: 分析揭示了EA与SK模型的深刻区别：二维和三维EA模型展开后分裂为孤立的子连接部分，而SK模型展现出显著的自相似行为，残差系统在整个展开过程中保持平均场结构和高斯统计。这种自相似性表现为残差矩阵范数和展开系数的指数衰减，反映了SK模型固有的平均场本质。

Conclusion: 模式展开方法能够识别EA模型中的超低能激发，揭示能量随展开步骤快速降低的激发态。通过连通分量分析，量化了这些独立激发簇的尺寸-能量关系，为理解自旋玻璃的低能景观和亚稳态性质开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce a systematic method for expanding general spin-glass Hamiltonians in terms of Mattis interactions, providing a novel perspective for understanding the fundamental differences between short-range Edwards-Anderson (EA) and mean-field Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK) spin glasses. By iteratively extracting patterns from the coupling matrix, we expand the original spin-glass system into a Hopfield-like model (a series of Mattis interactions) plus a residual system. Our analysis reveals profound distinctions between EA and SK models: while EA models in two and three dimensions break into isolated subconnected sections after expansion, the SK model exhibits remarkable self-similar behavior, with the residual system preserving the mean-field structure and Gaussian statistics throughout the expansion process. This self-similarity manifests in exponential decay of residual matrix norms and expansion coefficients, reflecting the inherent mean-field nature of the SK model. Furthermore, we demonstrate that pattern expansion can identify ultra-low energy excitations in EA models, revealing excitations with energies that decrease rapidly with expansion step. Through connected component analysis, we quantify the size-energy relationship of these independent excitation clusters, opening new avenues for understanding the low-energy landscape of spin glasses and providing insights into the nature of metastable states.

Abstract: Machine learning offers powerful tools to support experimental techniques, particularly for extracting latent features from large datasets. In magnetic materials, accurately estimating the interfacial Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction strength remains challenging, as existing experimental methods often rely on indirect measurements and can yield inconsistent results across techniques. Because this interaction is often extracted experimentally from bubble domain expansion, we investigate whether bubble textures alone contain sufficient and reliable information for data driven DMI inference. We therefore develop a compact convolutional neural network trained on a comprehensive micromagnetic dataset of magnetic bubble domains designed to emulate magneto optical Kerr effect imaging, including structural non uniformity, additive noise, and image pixelation. The proposed network demonstrates strong robustness against sample inhomogeneities, noise, and reduced spatial resolution. ### [86] [First principles electric field gradients at A and B site cations across the NaRTiO4 Ruddlesden Popper series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29004)
*L. F. Almeida,A. N. Cesário,P. A. Sousa,P. Rocha-Rodrigues,L. V. C. Assali,H. M. Petrilli,J. P. Araújo,A. M. L. Lopes*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究揭示了从稀土离子半径较小时的倾斜主导（tilt-dominated）体系向大离子半径时的畸变主导（distortion-dominated）体系的演化规律。随着离子半径增大，高温相与基态结构的竞争性增强，电子带隙呈现系统性演化。电场梯度张量在离子半径较大时各对称性趋于相似局部环境，而在偏离此极限时则表现出对称性特异性指纹特征。

Abstract: The $n = 1$ Ruddlesden-Popper titanates, NaRTiO$_{4}$ (R = rare-earth), exhibit a structural behaviour where non-centrosymmetry is driven by cooperative oxygen octahedral rotations (OORs) rather than conventional second-order Jahn-Teller distortions. In this work, we present an \textit{ab-initio} investigation of the structural, electronic and hyperfine properties of the entire NaRTiO$_{4}$ series across the two disputed ground states, $Pbcm$ and $P\bar{4}2_1m$, and the high temperature $P4/nmm$ symmetries. Our results reveal an ionic-radius-dependent evolution from a tilt-dominated regime for small rare-earth ions to a distortion-dominated regime for larger cations, leading to an asymptotic regime in which the high-temperature phase becomes increasingly competitive with the ground-state structures as the ionic radius increases. In parallel, the electronic band gap follows a systematic evolution across the series, reflecting the underlying structural changes and the increasing dominance of octahedral distortions at larger ionic radii. The Electric Field Gradient (EFG) tensor reveals that, in the large-radius limit, all symmetries tend locally towards a similar environment. Away from this limit, the EFG tensor for different symmetries progressively diverges, providing a sensitive probe for phase transitions and revealing symmetry-specific fingerprints, particularly for the rare-earth and Ti sites. By establishing these EFG signatures, this work provides a roadmap for experimental techniques, such as Nuclear Magnetic Resonance (NMR) and Perturbed Angular Correlation (PAC), to resolve the ground-state symmetry of these structures.

### [87] [Singing Materials: Initial experiments in applying sonification to phonon spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29037)
*Lucy Whalley,Rose Shepherd,Jorge Boehringer,Shelly Knotts,Paul Vickers,George Caselton,Christopher Harrison,Bennett Hogg,Daniel Ratliff,Carol Davenport,Antonio Portas*

TL;DR: SingingMaterials是一个用于将材料模拟数据（特别是声子态密度数据）转化为声音的Python软件包，通过三种核心方法实现声学化，用户研究表明该声学化方法能够帮助听众区分材料特性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体材料在原子尺度上存在持续的振动运动，这些由声子（phonons）描述的振动控制着材料的关键特性。理解声子物理对于设计具有目标功能的材料至关重要，而声学化（sonification）为此领域提供了新的探索途径。

Method: 开发了SingingMaterials模块化Python软件包，该软件与Materials Project数据库接口，基于Sonification Toolkit Strauss构建。当前实现支持三种核心声学化方法：光谱法（spectral）、合成法（synthesised）和基于样本的方法（sample-based）。

Result: 通过用户研究评估了声学化方法的有效性，研究听众是否能够从听觉表征中区分材料特性的差异。结果表明，声学化能够为探索振动材料数据提供可解释且互补的方法。

Conclusion: 声学化技术能够将材料振动数据转化为可感知的声音表征，为材料科学研究提供了新的数据探索工具，有助于理解和区分不同材料的物理特性。

Abstract: Solid materials may appear static, but at the atomic scale they are in constant vibrational motion. These vibrations, described by phonons, govern many key material properties, including structural stability, mechanical strength, optical behaviour, and thermal transport. Understanding phonon physics is therefore central to the rational design of materials with targeted functionalities.
  Singing Materials is a research project that explores how sonification can be applied to this domain. In this work, we introduce \texttt{SingingMaterials}, a modular Python package for sonifying materials simulation data. The software interfaces with the Materials Project database and is designed to be extensible, enabling the incorporation of additional sonification strategies and data sources. Built using the Sonification Toolkit \texttt{Strauss}, the current implementation supports three core approaches: spectral, synthesised, and sample-based.
  We demonstrate these approaches using phonon density-of-states data and evaluate their effectiveness through a user study, investigating whether listeners can distinguish differences in material properties from their auditory representations. The results show that sonification can provide an interpretable and complementary approach for exploring vibrational materials data.

</details>

Abstract: Vacancy-ordered double perovskites have emerged as lead-free alternatives, offering remarkable stability and compositional tunability for optoelectronic applications. We investigate the stability of these materials under simulated experimental conditions, considering both the rich and poor chemical potentials of their precursor salts. Finally, based solely on the intrinsic absolute energy levels, we identify promising candidates as charge transport and injection layers for typical photovoltaic and light-emitting applications. Method: 采用偏振分辨拉曼光谱直接解析结构-拓扑相变，通过角度依赖测量确定主要拉曼活性模（Raman-active modes）的对称性，并使用复杂拉曼张量形式（complex Raman tensor formalism）考虑吸收诱导的相位效应。结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算验证观察到的声子重整化（phonon renormalizations）方向。

Result: 拉曼光谱观测到跨越相变时，特定声子模（phonon modes）的频率、线宽和相对强度出现不连续、可逆的变化，尽管空间群保持不变。密度泛函理论计算再现了观察到的声子重整化方向，并确认其对堆叠依赖的力常数（stacking-dependent force constants）的敏感性。

Conclusion: 偏振分辨拉曼光谱能够探测驱动拓扑能带特性的细微堆叠驱动结构重排，即使全局晶体学对称性保持不变。这些结果为理解低维材料中晶格动力学、结构畸变和拓扑性质之间的相互作用提供了重要见解，具有实现独特功能的强大潜力。

Abstract: The quasi-one-dimensional material Bi4I4 hosts two crystallographically similar polymorphs that realize distinct topological insulating phases separated by a first-order structural transition near room temperature. This transition occurs without a change in space group, arising instead from a subtle rearrangement of chain stacking registry. Polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy directly resolves this structural-topological phase transition through abrupt, hysteretic modifications of the phonon spectrum. Angle-dependent measurements establish the symmetry of the dominant Raman-active modes and require a complex Raman tensor formalism to account for absorption-induced phase effects. Across the transition, selected phonon modes exhibit discontinuous, reversible shifts in frequency, linewidth, and relative intensity despite the absence of a space-group change. Density functional theory calculations reproduce the direction of the observed phonon renormalizations and confirm their sensitivity to stacking-dependent force constants. These results demonstrate that polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy can detect subtle stacking-driven structural rearrangements that underlie topological band character, even when global crystallographic symmetry remains unchanged. The obtained results provide valuable insights into the interplay among lattice dynamics, structural distortions, and topological properties in this class of low-dimensional materials, with strong potential for unique functionalities.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了包含长程相互作用的MACELES模型，并与先前报道的忽略长程相互作用的BaTiO3 MACE模型进行比较，评估了四个关键性质：声子色散、相变行为、力学响应以及包含介电常数的铁电性质。

Abstract: Bulk materials are governed by both short-range and long-range interactions, both of which are naturally captured in conventional density functional theory (DFT) calculations through Ewald summation of electrostatic contributions. In contrast, machine learning potentials (MLPs) typically rely on local atomic environment descriptors, and long-range interactions are often neglected. Such approximations may introduce systematic energetic errors and lead to inaccuracies in predicted material properties. To systematically investigate the impact of long-range interactions in ferroelectric BaTiO3 within the framework of MLPs, we developed a long-range MACELES model and compared its performance with the previously reported BaTiO3 MACE model across four key properties (phonon dispersion, phase transition behavior, mechanical response, and ferroelectric properties including dielectric constants). We find that qualitative behaviors, including phase transitions, stress-induced polarization switching, and polarization-electric field hysteresis, are consistently reproduced by both models. In contrast, quantitative properties such as transition temperatures, elastic constants, and dielectric constants exhibit systematic improvements in MACELES model, highlighting the importance of incorporating long-range electrostatics for accurately describing the structural and dielectric responses of BaTiO3. These results suggest that while long-range interactions play a role in improving quantitative accuracy, their omission does not significantly alter the qualitative ferroelectric behavior of BaTiO3.

Yet, direct control of a molecule's transition dipole moment and its resulting light emission via atomic-scale structural modification has remained elusive. Here, using scanning tunnelling microscopy-induced luminescence, we show that a single structural parameter-the vertical displacement of the central metal atom in a planar phthalocyanine molecule on a decoupling layer-enables active tuning of the transition dipole, allowing either suppression or enhancement of emission. Motivation: 二维范德华半导体（2D van der Waals semiconductors）集成到实际器件架构时，褶皱（wrinkles）和纳米气泡（nanobubbles）是固有且难以避免的结构特征。尽管这些应变特征普遍存在，但空间非均匀应变与局域电子结构改变之间的定量关联仍具挑战性。

Method: 研究方法结合了密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）与循环神经网络（recurrent neural network, RNN），从原子力显微镜（AFM）形貌和拉曼光谱图（Raman spectral maps）推导的应变图（strain maps）中重建单层MoS₂的局域电子结构（local electronic structure）。

Result: 分析表明，双轴弯曲诱导应变（biaxial bending induced strain）在改变电子和介电性质方面显著优于单轴弯曲或面内应变。约0.35%的双轴弯曲应变导致带隙（band gap）减少约22%，介电常数（dielectric constant）增加约7%，而可比单轴弯曲下仅减少约5%带隙和增加约1%介电常数。修正的能带结构显示带边态（band edge states）将电荷集中在高曲率或高应变区域。

Conclusion: 实际器件中常见的褶皱和纳米气泡等应变特征会影响带隙、载流子分布和介电响应，从而有利地影响电输运性质。该框架可轻松扩展到其他二维材料和异质结，为研究和利用应变效应提供了计算高效的途径。

Abstract: Wrinkles and nanobubbles are an integral and often unavoidable part of integrating 2D van der Waals semiconductors into actual device architectures. Despite their ubiquitous nature, quantitative correlation between such spatially non-uniform strain and modifications to the local electronic structure remains challenging. Here, density functional theory is combined with a recurrent neural network to reconstruct the local electronic structure of monolayer MoS2 from strain maps derived from atomic force microscopy (AFM) topography and Raman spectral maps. The analysis reveals that biaxial bending induced strain is significantly more effective than both uniaxial bending or in-plane strain in modifying electronic and dielectric properties. A ~ 0.35% strain induced by biaxial bending results in ~ 22% reduction in band gap and ~ 7% increase in dielectric constant, compared to a ~ 5% reduction in band gap and ~ 1% increase in dielectric constant under comparable uniaxial bending. The modified band structure reveals band edge states that concentrate charge in regions of high curvature or strain. While conductive AFM measurements indicate increased local conductance (carrier density) at wrinkles and nanobubbles, the spatial band gap maps predicted by the model are validated against experimental photoluminescence peak energy maps. The results indicate that strained features like wrinkles and nanobubbles commonly present in real devices influence the band gap, carrier distribution, and dielectric response, which favourably affects electrical transport in such systems. The framework developed here can be readily extended to other 2D materials and heterostructures, offering a computationally efficient route for studying and exploiting strain effects.

</details>


### [96] [Decoding Dopant-Induced Electronic Modulation in Graphene via Region-Resolved Machine Learning of XANES](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29370)
*Yinan Wang,Arpita Varadwaj,Teruyasu Mizoguchi,Masato Kotsugi*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示杂原子掺杂如何改变石墨烯的局部电子结构对于理解和控制其功能性质至关重要。本研究旨在解释硼和氮掺杂剂如何影响石墨烯的局部电子环境。

Method: 结合密度泛函理论（DFT）和机器学习（ML），分析来自91种不同构型的415个DFT模拟XANES光谱。采用区域特异性方法，将每个光谱分解为π*、σ*和后边缘区域，并在这些光谱片段上训练随机森林模型。

Result: 随机森林模型识别出π*区域对于预测关键局部电子描述符最具信息量，特别是Bader电荷和平均掺杂剂-碳键长。π*区域的增强预测能力源于其与扰动π电子网络的强耦合，能更有效地捕获电荷转移和杂化效应。

Conclusion: 研究确立了Bader电荷作为量化掺杂诱导电子调制的稳健且物理意义明确的描述符，并证明XANES光谱的区域分辨机器学习分析为揭示掺杂石墨烯及相关材料的结构-性能关系提供了有力途径。

Abstract: Revealing how heteroatom doping alters the local electronic structure of graphene is crucial for understanding and controlling its functional properties. In this study, we combine density functional theory (DFT) and machine learning (ML) to interpret how boron (B) and nitrogen (N) dopants influence the local electronic environments of graphene. A dataset of 415 DFT-simulated XANES spectra from 91 distinct configurations was analyzed using a region-specific approach by decomposing each spectrum into pi*, sigma*, and post-edge regions. Random forest models trained on these spectral segments identified the pi* region as the most informative for predicting key local electronic descriptors, particularly the Bader charge and mean dopant-carbon bond length. The Bader charge quantifies dopant-induced charge redistribution and local bonding polarity, directly reflecting the degree of electronic perturbation introduced by heteroatom substitution. The enhanced predictive power of the pi* region arises from its strong coupling to the perturbed pi-electron network, which captures these charge-transfer and hybridization effects more effectively than sigma* or post-edge regions. These findings establish Bader charge as a robust and physically meaningful descriptor for quantifying dopant-induced electronic modulation and demonstrate that region-resolved ML analysis of XANES spectra provides a powerful pathway to uncover structure-property relationships in doped graphene and related materials.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维材料中的等离子体激元为纳米尺度光-物质相互作用控制提供了强大平台，但目前调控其相干性和耗散的策略仍然有限。需要探索新的方法来工程化调控等离子体响应。

Method: 结合高分辨芯能级光电子能谱（high-resolution core-level photoemission spectroscopy）与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），研究铁和钴在2H-TaS₂中的插层效应。

Result: 过渡金属插层并非传统电子掺杂，而是通过轨道杂化（orbital hybridization）和结构重构（structural reconstruction）重塑低能电子结构。这引入了密集的低能激发连续谱，有效阻尼并最终抑制了等离子体模式。

Abstract: Plasmons in low dimensional materials provide a powerful platform for nanoscale control of light matter interactions, yet strategies to tailor their coherence and dissipation remain limited. Here, we demonstrate that transition metal intercalation offers a fundamentally distinct route to engineer plasmonic response in layered materials. By combining high-resolution core-level photoemission spectroscopy with first-principles calculations, we show that Fe and Co intercalation in 2H-TaS2 does not act as conventional electron doping, but instead reshapes the low energy electronic structure through orbital hybridization and structural reconstruction. This process introduces a dense continuum of low energy excitations that efficiently damp and ultimately suppress the plasmon mode. First principle calculations of the energy loss function reveal a transition from a well defined collective excitation to an overdamped response, signaling the breakdown of coherent charge dynamics. Our results establish intercalation as a chemically controlled pathway to tune plasmon losses and dielectric response in quantum van der Waals materials, providing a new design principle for plasmonic and optoelectronic functionalities at the nanoscale.

### [98] [Unquenched orbital angular momentum as the origin of spin inertia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29421)

  <summary>Details</summary>
