Notwithstanding recent progress, a clear identification of spin inertia's physical origin thereby offering predictive power remains to be accomplished. Here, discussing general principles for identifying this physical origin, we examine unquenched orbital angular momentum (OAM) finding it to be a key candidate, despite its typically small value. Treating OAM and spin within a two-sublattice model, we derive the equivalent single-sublattice framework for magnetization dynamics making appropriate approximations. The latter naturally manifests the spin inertia term and parameter, which are otherwise introduced phenomenologically. The inertia parameter evaluated within our model is found to be in good agreement with its experimentally observed value in cobalt. We further delineate key experimental signatures that could verify or rule out the unquenched OAM as the origin of the observed high-frequency mode, and avoid a spurious optical mode in a two-sublattice ferromagnet from being identified as nutation. Our analysis offers a potential link between the recently emerged fields of orbitronics and spin inertia, thereby motivating investigations at their intersection.

Here, we introduce a framework for dynamic electron tomography that combines continuous tilting with a self-supervised deep-learning reconstruction strategy. Our approach incorporates the temporal aspect into the electron tomography reconstruction process to recover 3D volumes at arbitrary time points from a single tilt series. We validate the method using simulations and demonstrate its merit in experimental studies of heat-induced transformations, including morphological evolution of Au nanostars and alloying in Au@Ag nanocubes. ### [100] [Fe-site-resolved anisotropy energies in Nd$_2$Fe$_{14}$B for atomistic spin dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29476)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Nd-Fe-B磁体作为广泛应用的高性能磁体，其Fe元素的各向异性贡献在原子自旋动力学（atomistic spin dynamics, ASD）模拟中难以准确建模，主要源于Fe的巡游磁性（itinerant nature of magnetism）特性。现有ASD模拟与第一性原理研究存在不一致性，需要建立更准确的模型。

Method: 研究首先回顾了ASD模拟中Fe各向异性的现有处理方法，识别出与第一性原理研究的差异。随后推导了两种修正模型：基于单离子理论（single-ion theory）的模型和基于各向异性交换（anisotropic exchange）的模型。通过将模型预测与Y₂Fe₁₄B的第一性原理扭矩计算（torque calculations）结果进行对比来验证模型性能。

Result: 扭矩计算结果显示，Fe的各向异性贡献无法用单离子模型解释，但自然地源于（反对称的）各向异性交换机制。这表明在ASD模拟中准确描述Fe各向异性需要考虑各向异性交换作用。

Conclusion: 研究提出了未来ASD模拟中建模Fe各向异性的实用策略，包括简化的（平均场）各向异性交换描述方法。这些策略不仅适用于R₂Fe₁₄B体系，还可推广到更广泛的巡游磁性材料（itinerant magnetic materials）类别。

Abstract: Nd-Fe-B magnets are the most widely used high performance magnets in the world today, and remain the subject of both experimental and computational research aimed at understanding and optimizing them. Atomistic spin dynamics (ASD) is one technique which has been used in recent years to provide insight into magnetic properties relevant to coercivity, such as domain wall width. Although it is relatively clear how to model magnetocrystalline anisotropy arising from rare-earth atoms in these simulations, the contribution from the transition metal Fe is less obvious, due to the itinerant nature of the magnetism. Here, we examine previous treatments of Fe anisotropy in ASD simulations and identify a discrepancy with previously-published first-principles studies. We derive two models which correct this discrepancy, one based on single-ion theory and the other on anisotropic exchange, and test their performance by comparing to first-principles torque calculations on Y$_2$Fe$_{14}$B. The torque calculations show a contribution which cannot be explained by the single-ion model but arises naturally from (antisymmetric) anisotropic exchange. We propose practical strategies to model Fe anisotropy in future ASD simulations, including a simplified (mean-field) description of anisotropic exchange, which may have applications beyond R$_2$Fe$_{14}$B to the wider class of itinerant magnetic materials.

Abstract: Existing acoustic topological textures are predominantly constructed within velocity fields, where the corresponding physical observables typically exhibit harmonic temporal oscillations. In contrast, stationary topological acoustic textures are highly desirable for characterizing topological phenomena and advancing potential applications of topological quasiparticles. Here, we propose a novel framework for topological acoustic spin textures rooted in acoustic spin, and experimentally demonstrate stable acoustic spin meron lattices supported by spoof surface acoustic-wave modes. We show that phase singularities in acoustic standing waves play a pivotal role in the formation of acoustic spin. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the phase differences among distinct groups of standing waves govern the polarization of the emergent topological quasiparticles and enable precise modulation of their intensities. Moreover, the resulting topological spin textures exhibit remarkable robustness against boundary scattering and local structural defects. Our findings establish acoustic spin as a fundamental degree of freedom for engineering topological quasiparticles in acoustics and open a new avenue toward programmable stationary topological acoustic textures.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体滑动接触区域温度升高可达数百开尔文，显著影响摩擦与磨损。经典闪温理论（Jaeger、Archard、Greenwood）忽略真实表面的多尺度特性，仅用圆形或方形近似摩擦热源，存在局限性。

Method: 提出适用于具有任意多尺度粗糙度随机粗糙表面的闪温分析理论，将应力相关函数（stress correlation functions）和峰值应力的成熟方法扩展到温度分析。

Result: 展示了橡胶在混凝土上滑动以及花岗岩在花岗岩上滑动的数值结果作为例证，证明经典闪温理论在处理多尺度粗糙表面时存在严重失效。

Conclusion: 经典闪温理论无法准确描述多尺度粗糙表面的温度分布，新提出的分析理论为此类表面提供了更准确的闪温预测框架。

Abstract: The temperature increase in the contact regions between solids in sliding contact can easily reach several hundred Kelvin and thereby dramatically affect friction and wear. The classical theories by Jaeger, Archard, and Greenwood, commonly used to estimate flash temperature, ignore the multiscale nature of real surfaces and instead approximate the frictional heat sources with circular or square shapes. Here, we present an analytical theory for the flash temperature valid for randomly rough surfaces with roughness across arbitrarily many decades in length scale. The theory extends established methods for stress correlation functions and peak stresses to temperature. Numerical results for rubber sliding on concrete, and granite on granite, are presented as illustrations. We show that classical theories for flash temperature fail severely for surfaces with multiscale roughness.

</details>


### [104] [Superlinear Temperature-Dependent Resistivity and Structural Phase Transition in BaNi$_2$P$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29797)
*E. H. Krenkel,M. A. Tanatar,E. I. Timmons,S. L. Bud'ko,P. C. Canfield,Qing-Ping Ding,Y. Furukawa,Lin-Lin Wang,M. Konczykowski,R. Grasset,J. L. Niedziela,O. Delaire,G. Viswanathan,J. Wang,K. Kovnir,R. Prozorov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过低温电子辐照研究BaNi₂P₄中异常超线性温度依赖性电阻率ρ(T)的机制，发现四方-正交相变主导电阻行为，局部Ba原子振动增强高温相残余电阻率，其衰减导致正交相异常温度依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究BaNi₂P₄金属非常规笼合物中异常超线性温度依赖性电阻率ρ(T)的物理机制，通过人工引入无序（低温电子辐照）探索其演化规律。

Method: 采用低温（~20 K）2.5 MeV电子辐照引入人工无序，结合电阻率、磁化率、霍尔效应、拉曼散射和³¹P核磁共振（NMR）等多种测量技术，分析四方-正交相变对电子输运性质的影响。

Result: 四方-正交相变（Ts ~373-378 K）主导电阻率行为：高温四方相呈现标准金属线性T-依赖电阻率，正交相则显示异常行为；相变伴随结构畴形成和约4 K磁滞，证实其一阶相变特征；马蒂森定则（Matthiessen rule）在相变两侧均成立，电子结构变化可忽略；电子辐照显著抑制相变温度；拉曼散射显示正交相中局部Ba振动模式软化；³¹P NMR谱线分裂表明Ba原子从笼中心部分位移。

Conclusion: 局部Ba原子振动（rattling）增强高温四方相残余电阻率贡献，其衰减导致正交相异常温度依赖性电阻率行为，相变主要影响晶格动力学而非电子结构。

Abstract: The mechanism of anomalous superlinear temperature-dependent resistivity, $ρ(T)$, in the metallic unconventional clathrate BaNi$_2$P$_4$ was studied by examining its evolution with artificial disorder induced by low-temperature ($\sim$ 20 K) 2.5 MeV electron irradiation. We find a dominant effect of the tetragonal-orthorhombic transition at $T_s$ ($ \sim$373 to 378 K, depending on heat cycle rate and direction) on $ρ(T)$, with standard metallic $T-$linear resistivity above the transition and anomalous behavior in the orthorhombic phase below. The transition is accompanied by the formation of structural domains and a notable (about 4~K) hysteresis in the magnetization and resistivity measurements, clearly showing its first order character. Matthiessen rule is obeyed both above and below the transition, suggesting negligible changes in the electronic structure. This conclusion is supported by the smooth evolution of the Hall effect through the transition. The Hall number is in good agreement with band structure calculations both above and below the transition. The transition temperature is notably suppressed with electron irradiation. Raman scattering at temperatures above room temperature find softening of local Ba vibration mode in the orthorhombic phase on approaching the transition. $^{31}P$ NMR line splits in the orthorhombic phase, suggesting a partial shift of the Ba atom from the central position in the cage. We suggest that local Ba rattling leads to enhanced residual contribution to resistivity in the high temperature tetragonal phase, the decay of which is responsible for the anomalous temperature-dependent resistivity in the orthorhombic phase.

### [105] [Molecular beam epitaxy of wafer-scale O-band InAs/InGaAs quantum dots on GaAs for quantum photonics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29934)

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种可扩展的MBE策略，能够可靠地制备低密度、O波段电可调的InAs/InGaAs量子点。该方法通过梯度沉积和应变调控实现了波长控制，利用表面调制技术实现了密度调控，为量子信息应用提供了高质量的量子光源。

Abstract: We report a scalable molecular beam epitaxy strategy to achieve a low density of O-band electrically tunable InAs/InGaAs quantum dots (QDs) on GaAs(001) substrates. Our approach is based on a gradient deposition of InAs in the sub-ML regime and subsequent capping with an InGaA strain-reducing layer to redshift the emission wavelength. For different growth conditions, we investigate the optical properties of the dots using photoluminescence mapping and correlate with structural properties determined by scanning transmission electron microscopy. Using a surface roughness modulation technique and synchronizing InAs sub-monolayer deposition cycles with substrate rotation, we control the dot density and position low-density regions (< 1 QD per um^2) on the substrate. Hyperspectral imaging is used to map the spatial and spectral characteristics of many individual dots in the low-density region, confirming that our approach is universally applicable to conventional MBE growth on (001) surfaces. Finally, we tune the QD emission wavelength within the O-band using electric fields and demonstrate single-photon emission with g(2)(0) = 0.020(14).

Abstract: 4D-STEM-based orientation and phase mapping has enabled rapid microstructure quantification that can be directly combined with standard TEM- and STEM-based imaging modes. Typically, orientation mapping is coupled with beam precession (i.e. precession electron diffraction) to achieve high indexing rates, adding to the cost and often decreasing the spatial resolution of the approach. This paper introduces a new post processing approach modeled after the non-local pattern averaging and reindexing algorithm developed for the electron backscatter diffraction community, wherein post-collection, patterns are averaged using a distance similarity parameter. Results from Ni and Au thin films show that indexing rates can be significantly improved using this post-processing technique due to improved signal-to-noise ratios in the diffraction patterns. ### [107] [Interplay between Temperature Oscillations and Melt Pool Dynamics in 3D Manufacturing Techniques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28811)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究提出了一个物理一致模型，并基于文献[Phys. Rev. Appl. 10, 044061 (2018)]中时间分辨吸收率（time-resolved absorptance）的详细数据进行验证。在该方法框架内推导了振荡谱的解析方程。

Result: 研究证明表面振荡可以在没有小孔效应（keyhole effect）的情况下被激发，但小孔形成会导致振荡谱中出现额外模式。获得了便于实时监测熔池表面温度和特征流速的实用公式，并深入研究了表面张力温度系数对最大温度、熔池长度、自由表面振荡固有频率和衰减系数的影响。

Conclusion: 所有结果均以闭式公式呈现，适用于工业激光系统的设计。该模型为激光熔化过程中温度振荡与熔池动力学的耦合机制提供了物理一致的解释框架。

Abstract: The aim of this paper is coupling of temperature oscillations and melt pool dynamics experimentally observed in laser melting. The literature survey has shown that the developed explanations are mainly focused on the capillary and hydrodynamic aspects of the problem. As shown, complete analysis is only possible if the temperature oscillations are properly accounted for. Specifically, this effect is a governing mechanism that controls the melt pool dynamics via feedback coupling of heating, evaporation, capillarity and free-surface contraction. The present study suggests a physically consistent model validated on the detailed data of the time-resolved absorptance measured in [Phys. Rev. Appl. 10, 044061 (2018)]. An analytical equation is derived for oscillation spectra within this approach. It has been proved that the surface oscillations can be initiated without the keyhole effect. However, keyhole formation can cause additional modes to appear in the oscillation spectrum. The practical results include the formulas that are convenient for real-time monitoring of the surface temperature and characteristic flow velocity in the molten pool using the measured absorptance spectra. The impact of the temperature coefficient of surface tension on the maximal temperature, pool length, natural frequency of the free surface oscillations, and attenuation coefficient is thoroughly studied. All results are presented as closed-form formulas suitable for design of industrial laser systems.

### [108] [Symmetry-Fractionalized Skin Effects in Non-Hermitian Luttinger Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28849)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在一维强关联无能隙系统中，共形不变性导致不同对称性扇区的低能自由度解耦，最典型的例子是自旋-电荷分离。本研究旨在将这一机制扩展到非厄米领域，探索不同对称性扇区对应的趋肤效应是否也会出现类似的解耦现象。

Method: 研究首先为N味费米子（N flavor fermions）建立了理论框架，然后通过哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）进行数值验证，最后构造了一个相互作用驱动的E8趋肤效应（E8 skin effect），该效应在自由费米子系统中不存在对应物。

Result: 研究证明在非厄米系统中，不同对称性扇区对应的趋肤效应确实会出现解耦现象。在哈伯德模型中，自旋和电荷的趋肤效应在低能区实现分离。此外，成功构造了一个仅由相互作用驱动的E8趋肤效应，这在自由费米子系统中没有对应物。

Conclusion: 该研究将一维强关联系统中的对称性分离机制成功扩展到非厄米领域，揭示了不同对称性扇区趋肤效应的解耦现象，并展示了相互作用在产生新型趋肤效应中的关键作用，为非厄米强关联系统的研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: In one dimension, strongly correlated gapless systems are highly constrained due to conformal invariance, leading to the decoupling of low energy degrees of freedom corresponding to different symmetry sectors. The most familiar example of this is spin-charge separation. Here, we extend this mechanism to the non-Hermitian realm by demonstrating that skin effects corresponding to different symmetry sectors exhibit an emergent decoupling. We establish this for $N$ flavor fermions and demonstrate it numerically for the special case of the Hubbard model, in which spin and charge skin effects separate at low energies. Finally, we construct an interaction-enabled $E_8$ skin effect with no free fermion counterpart.

### [109] [Higgs criticality of Dirac spin liquids on depleted triangular lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28860)
*Andreas Feuerpfeil,Atanu Maity,Ronny Thomale,Yasir Iqbal,Subir Sachdev*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了U(1)狄拉克自旋液体在三角、kagome和枫叶晶格中的希格斯临界性，发现尽管大费米子味数和希格斯场涨落抑制了汤川耦合的相关性，但所有三种情况下的耦合仍保持弱相关性，导致希格斯临界点渐近不稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究候选U(1)狄拉克自旋液体（Dirac spin liquids）在一系列耗尽三角晶格（depleted triangular lattices）——包括三角、kagome和枫叶晶格（maple-leaf geometries）——中的希格斯临界性（Higgs criticality）。重点在于理解这些系统从U(1)态到邻近ℤ₂自旋液体的对称性允许的自旋子配对通道。

Method: 研究方法包括：为每个晶格推导相应的量子电动力学-希格斯理论（quantum electrodynamics (QED₃)-Higgs theory）；使用大N_{f,b}展开（large-N_{f,b} expansion）计算临界指数和对称性允许的汤川耦合（Yukawa couplings）的标度维度；分析费米子味数（fermion flavor number）和节点几何结构（nodal geometry）的相互作用。

Result: 研究发现：三角和kagome晶格共享具有N_f=4狄拉克费米子的低能描述，而枫叶晶格产生类似的N_f=12理论，且具有独特的节点结构，其中狄拉克锥（Dirac cones）可在动量空间的高对称线上移动。希格斯场涨落和大费米子味数都抑制汤川耦合的相关性，使枫叶晶格比其对应晶格更接近稳定性，但所有三种情况下的耦合仍保持弱相关性。在枫叶晶格情况下，希格斯临界点的渐近不稳定部分由与狄拉克锥动量空间移动性相关的额外耦合驱动。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，费米子味数和节点几何结构之间的相互作用决定了QED₃-希格斯转变的命运。该工作提供了一个统一框架，展示了大费米子味数和节点几何如何共同影响希格斯临界点的稳定性，其中枫叶晶格的特殊节点结构引入了额外的相关耦合，导致其希格斯临界点呈现渐近不稳定性。

Abstract: We investigate Higgs criticality in candidate U(1) Dirac spin liquids across a family of depleted triangular lattices: the triangular, kagome, and maple-leaf geometries. For each, we identify the symmetry-allowed spinon-pairing channel connecting the U(1) state to a proximate $\mathbb{Z}_2$ spin liquid, deriving the corresponding quantum electrodynamics (QED$_3$)-Higgs theory. While the triangular and kagome lattices share a low-energy description with $N_f=4$ Dirac fermions, the maple-leaf lattice yields an analogous theory with $N_f=12$ and a distinct nodal structure where the Dirac cones can move along high-symmetry lines in momentum space. Using a large-$N_{f,b}$ expansion, we compute critical exponents and the scaling dimensions of the symmetry-allowed Yukawa couplings. We find that while Higgs-field fluctuations and a large fermion flavor number both act to suppress the relevance of the Yukawa coupling -- pushing the maple-leaf lattice closer to stability than its counterparts -- the coupling remains weakly relevant in all three cases. This rendering of the Higgs critical point as asymptotically unstable is partly driven in the maple-leaf case by an additional coupling associated with the momentum-space mobility of the Dirac cones. Ultimately, our results provide a unified framework demonstrating how the interplay between fermion flavor count and nodal geometry dictates the fate of the QED$_3$-Higgs transition.

### [110] [Fractionalization from Kinetic Frustration in Doped Two-Dimensional SU(4) Quantum Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28871)
*Wilhelm Kadow,Ivan Morera,Eugene Demler,Michael Knap*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究在受挫三角晶格上的SU(4)对称t-J模型中，发现了一种新的分数化机制：空穴掺杂时，空穴可分数化为费米子性自旋子和玻色子性空穴子，而电子掺杂则导致铁磁相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解分数化激发（fractionalized excitations）在何种条件下出现是重要的概念挑战，有助于实现量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquids）等长期寻求的物态。本研究旨在识别一种新的分数化机制。

Method: 研究基于受挫三角晶格（frustrated triangular lattices）上四分之一填充的SU(4)对称t-J模型。采用大N极限（large-N limit）解析分析，并结合矩阵乘积态（matrix product states）在柱状几何上的数值模拟，以及变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）方法在40×40系统上的计算。

Result: 空穴掺杂时，空穴分数化为费米子性自旋子（fermionic spinons）和玻色子性空穴子（bosonic holons）：空穴子通过自旋子形成自旋子费米面（spinon Fermi surface）来最小化动能。电子掺杂则驱动系统进入铁磁相，类似于永冈定理（Nagaoka's theorem）。

Conclusion: 该研究识别了一种新的分数化机制，揭示了掺杂对有序态和分数化之间相互作用的调控。研究讨论了在莫尔异质结构（moiré heterostructures）和超冷原子（ultracold atoms）中的可能实验实现，并提出了探测分数化准粒子关键特性的动力学探针。

Abstract: Separating electrons into emergent fractional quasiparticles is a hallmark of exotic quantum phases of matter with strong interactions. Understanding under which circumstances fractionalized excitations appear is a major conceptual challenge and can help realize long sought-after states, such as quantum spin liquids. Here, we identify a distinct mechanism for fractionalization. Starting from the plaquette-ordered ground state of an SU(4) symmetric t-J model at quarter filling on frustrated triangular lattices, we reveal a compelling interplay between order and fractionalization as a function of doping. For hole doping, we find that the kinetic frustration can be relieved by fractionalizing the holes into fermionic spinons and bosonic holons: the holons minimize their kinetic energy when the spinons form a spinon Fermi surface. We support this mechanism analytically in the large-N limit as well as numerically by simulating the SU(4) case with matrix product states on cylinder geometries and with variational Monte Carlo methods on system sizes up to 40x40. Conversely, electron doping drives the system into a ferromagnetic phase, akin to Nagaoka's theorem. We discuss possible experimental realizations in moiré heterostructures as well as ultracold atoms, and propose dynamical probes to search for key characteristics of the fractionalized quasiparticles.

</details>


### [111] [Effect of spin-orbit coupling on spin and orbital ordering in Sr$_{n+1}$Cr$_n$O$_{3n+1}$, $n=1,2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28904)
*Cristian Fanjul,A. A. Aligia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究将自旋轨道耦合（SOC）纳入Ruddlesden-Popper系列Sr₂CrO₄和Sr₃Cr₂O₇的有效Kugel-Khomskii模型中，发现SOC在单层Sr₂CrO₄中主导物理性质，而在双层Sr₃Cr₂O₇中影响较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）整合到Ruddlesden-Popper系列Sr_{n+1}Cr_nO_{3n+1}的有效Kugel-Khomskii模型中，以理解SOC对n=1和n=2成员（即Sr₂CrO₄和Sr₃Cr₂O₇）中自旋和轨道自由度的影响。

Method: 研究方法采用包含自旋轨道耦合的有效Kugel-Khomskii模型，其中每个格点包含相互作用的自旋1和赝自旋1/2，分别描述自旋和轨道自由度。在零温条件下使用赝自旋键算符（pseudospin bond operators）和自旋波（spin waves）方法求解模型。

Result: 研究结果显示，对于Sr₂CrO₄，SOC在真实参数下主导物理性质，自旋排列为反铁磁（antiferromagnetic），最近邻Cr自旋反平行排列，轨道构型为d_{xy↑}¹(d_{xz↑}¹-id_{yz↑}¹)或d_{xy↓}¹(d_{xz↓}¹+id_{yz↓}¹)。对于Sr₃Cr₂O₇，SOC效应较弱，系统倾向于在垂直于平面的z方向形成赝自旋单重态（pseudospin singlets），自旋在平面内反铁磁排列，平面间铁磁排列。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明自旋轨道耦合对Ruddlesden-Popper系列铬酸盐的物理性质具有显著影响，但在单层和双层结构中表现出不同行为：SOC在单层Sr₂CrO₄中起主导作用，而在双层Sr₃Cr₂O₇中影响较弱，系统表现出不同的自旋和轨道有序模式。

Abstract: We incorporate spin-orbit coupling (SOC) into effective Kugel-Khomskii models for the $n=1$ and $n=2$ members of the Ruddlesden-Popper series Sr$_{n+1}$Cr$_n$O$_{3n+1}$. These model contain interacting spins 1 and pseudospins 1/2 at each site describing spin and orbitals degrees of freedom respectively. We solve the models at zero temperature using pseudospin bond operators and spin waves. We find that for realistic parameters, SOC dominates the physics of the compound Sr$_{2}$CrO$_{4}$ with almost decoupled single CrO$_2$ planes. The spin ordering is antiferromagnetic, with nearest-neighbor Cr spins aligned antiparallel. The corresponding orbital configuration is $d_{xy \uparrow }^{1}(d_{xz\uparrow }^{1}-id_{yz\uparrow }^{1})$ or $d_{xy \downarrow }^{1}(d_{xz\downarrow }^{1}+id_{yz\downarrow }^{1})$ depending on the spin of the site. In contrast, for the bilayer compound Sr$_{3}$Cr$_{2}$O$_{7}$ we find that the effect of the SOC is weak and the system prefers to form pseudospin singlets in the $z$ direction perpendicular to the planes. The spin order is antiferromagnetic within each plane and ferromagnetic between planes, in agreement with previous studies.

### [112] [Three-Band Anderson Lattice Model Reveals Co-Evolution of Topological and Magnetic Phases Driven by Electron Correlation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29172)
*Zhong-Yi Wang,Ya-Min Quan,Yu-Xuan Sun,Liang-Jian Zou,Xiang-Long Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个三带安德森晶格模型（three-band Anderson lattice model），揭示了强关联、拓扑和磁序之间的相互作用机制，为解决高温量子反常霍尔效应（QAHE）中强关联与大能隙不相容的长期难题提供了统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解能带拓扑（band topology）、强电子关联（strong electron correlation）和磁序（magnetic order）之间的相互作用是实现高温量子反常霍尔效应（QAHE）的核心瓶颈。传统的两带安德森模型（two-band Anderson models）仅限于顺磁近藤拓扑绝缘体（paramagnetic Kondo topological insulators），无法捕捉与QAHE基准材料MnBi2Te4家族相关的拓扑-磁相耦合演化。

Method: 研究开发了一个包含哈伯德相互作用（Hubbard interaction）、s-d交换耦合（s-d exchange coupling）和类BHZ拓扑机制的最小三带安德森晶格模型（three-band Anderson lattice model）。采用Kotliar-Ruckenstein slave-boson方法，在填充数v=2条件下映射关联驱动的相变。

Result: 增加U驱动了从平庸到近藤拓扑绝缘体（Kondo topological insulator）的转变，随后激活第三带介导了从顺磁拓扑绝缘体到铁磁金属（ferromagnetic metal）的转变。能带重构——完全自旋极化的d轨道沉入费米能级以下，留下巡游p轨道主导低能物理——与MnBi2Te4的第一性原理结果定性匹配。在强关联区域，交换耦合J稳定了陈数近藤绝缘体（Chern-Kondo insulator，C=1）和外尔节线半金属（Weyl nodal-line semimetal）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了完全d轨道自旋极化（full d-orbital spin polarization）使拓扑能隙对关联诱导的变窄具有免疫力，解决了长期存在的强关联-大能隙不相容问题。结果与最新的QAHE实验在定性上高度一致，为关联磁性拓扑材料提供了统一框架和实现高温QAHE的新途径。

Abstract: Understanding the interplay of band topology, strong electron correlation, and magnetic order is the fundamental core bottleneck for realizing robust high-temperature quantum anomalous Hall effect (QAHE). Conventional two-band Anderson models are limited to paramagnetic Kondo topological insulators, failing to capture coupled topological-magnetic phase evolution relevant to the QAHE benchmark MnBi2Te4 family. We develop a minimal three-band Anderson lattice model incorporating Hubbard interaction, s-d exchange coupling, and a BHZ-like topological mechanism. Using the Kotliar-Ruckenstein slave-boson approach, we map correlation-driven phase transitions at filling v=2: increasing U drives a trivial-to-Kondo topological insulator transition, then activates the third band to mediate a paramagnetic topological insulator-to-ferromagnetic metal transition. The accompanying band reconstruction--fully spin-polarized d-orbitals sinking below the Fermi level, leaving itinerant p-orbitals to dominate low-energy physics--qualitatively matches published first-principles results for MnBi2Te4. In the strong-correlation regime, exchange coupling J stabilizes a Chern-Kondo insulator (C=1) and Weyl nodal-line semimetal. Critically, we reveal full d-orbital spin polarization renders the topological gap immune to correlation-induced narrowing, resolving the long-standing strong correlation-large gap incompatibility. Our results show excellent qualitative alignment with recent state-of-the-art QAHE experiments, providing a unified framework for correlated magnetic topological materials and new pathways to high-temperature QAHE.

</details>


### [113] [Parafermionic Truncated Wigner Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29344)
*Javad Vahedi,Martin Garttner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了parafermionic truncated Wigner approximation (pTWA)，一种用于模拟具有分数交换统计的晶格系统非平衡动力学的半经典相空间框架。该方法将适用于玻色和费米系统的截断Wigner方法推广到ℤₙ Fock parafermions，通过将哈密顿量表示为形成闭合李代数的局域Hubbard算符来实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有截断Wigner方法主要针对玻色和费米系统，缺乏适用于parafermionic系统的半经典相空间模拟框架。需要开发能够处理分数交换统计晶格系统非平衡动力学的实用计算工具，特别是在精确数值方法受限于希尔伯特空间增长的体系中。

Method: 方法通过将哈密顿量表示为形成闭合李代数的局域Hubbard算符，将截断Wigner方法推广到ℤₙ Fock parafermions。这导致了一个Lie-Poisson相空间表述，其中量子动力学通过初始条件的随机采样和确定性半经典演化来近似。

Result: 在多个体系中进行了基准测试，包括单点clock动力学、全连接ℤₙ clock模型、长程ℤ₃ clock链和disordered ℤ₃ Fock parafermion链。该方法再现了精确动力学的关键特征，包括激发扩散、无序诱导的输运抑制以及长时间不平衡平台的出现。

Conclusion: pTWA为探索parafermionic系统动力学提供了一个实用工具，特别是在精确数值方法受限于希尔伯特空间增长的体系中。该方法能够有效模拟分数交换统计系统的非平衡动力学行为。

Abstract: We introduce the parafermionic truncated Wigner approximation ($p$TWA), a semiclassical phase-space framework for simulating the nonequilibrium dynamics of lattice systems with fractional exchange statistics. The method extends truncated Wigner approaches developed for bosonic and fermionic systems to $\mathbb{Z}_n$ Fock parafermions by expressing the Hamiltonian in terms of local Hubbard operators that form a closed Lie algebra. This representation leads to a Lie--Poisson phase-space formulation in which quantum dynamics is approximated by stochastic sampling of initial conditions followed by deterministic semiclassical evolution. We benchmark the approach in several settings, including single-site clock dynamics, the fully connected $\mathbb{Z}_n$ clock model, long-range $\mathbb{Z}_3$ clock chains, and disordered $\mathbb{Z}_3$ Fock parafermion chains. The method reproduces key features of the exact dynamics, including excitation spreading, disorder-induced suppression of transport, and the emergence of long-time imbalance plateaus. Our results demonstrate that $p$TWA provides a practical tool for exploring the dynamics of parafermionic systems in regimes where exact numerical methods are limited by Hilbert-space growth.

*Cliò Efthimia Agrapidis,Satoshi Nishimoto*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索掺杂Kitaev系统中超导和绝缘相的物理机制，特别是磁阻挫在这些相形成中的作用。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group）方法研究空穴掺杂的Kitaev-Heisenberg链，分析不同耦合参数下的物理行为。

Result: 在纯Kitaev极限下，键方向交换（bond-directional exchange）本身促进配对，反铁磁和铁磁Kitaev耦合分别有利于自旋单重态和自旋三重态超导倾向。在完整Kitaev-Heisenberg链中，J和K交换协同作用广泛稳定超导性，而J和K之间的竞争导致强填充依赖，并能在两者都弱时实现超导。在四分之一填充时，这种竞争产生具有自发跳跃二聚化的Mott绝缘体。

Conclusion: 磁阻挫（magnetic frustration）是掺杂Kitaev系统中超导和相互作用驱动绝缘相的共同机制，揭示了这些相形成的统一物理图像。

Abstract: We study the hole-doped Kitaev-Heisenberg chain using the density-matrix renormalization group. In the Kitaev-only limit, the bond-directional exchange itself promotes pairing, favoring spin-singlet and spin-triplet superconducting tendencies for antiferromagnetic and ferromagnetic Kitaev couplings, respectively, together with finite-size Majorana edge correlations suggestive of topological superconductivity. In the full Kitaev-Heisenberg chain, cooperative $J$ and $K$ exchanges broadly stabilize superconductivity, while competition between $J$ and $K$ induces a strong filling dependence and enables superconductivity even when both $J$ and $K$ are weak. At quarter filling, this competition produces a Mott insulator with spontaneous hopping dimerization. These results identify magnetic frustration as a common mechanism underlying superconducting and interaction-driven insulating phases in doped Kitaev systems.

### [115] [Kondo scaling of $4f$-electron states and the Kondo singlet breakdown in heavy fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29599)
*B. Tegomo Chiogo,M. Tagliavini,D. Wong,C. Schulz,1 V. Porée,A. Nicolaou,R. Feyerherm,T. Schweitzer,T. Mazet,M. W. Haverkort,A. Chainani,D. Malterre,K. Habicht*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近藤材料的热力学性质和高能光谱学理论已较为成熟，但电子光谱学的表面敏感性限制了近藤标度（Kondo scaling）的定量验证。需要发展体敏感的光谱技术来定量研究强关联材料中的近藤效应。

Method: 采用体敏感的温度依赖共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, RIXS）技术，结合单杂质安德森模型（single-impurity Anderson model, SIAM）计算，研究CeSi₂材料中f电子态的演化。

Result: RIXS Ce M₅边光谱显示f⁰态占据随温度升高而减少，f¹L¹态谱重增加，与SIAM计算吻合良好。结果揭示了近藤单态（Kondo singlet）的破坏以及低激发磁态的热占据，其温度演化与光电子能谱和逆光电子能谱的结果形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种准确测定近藤能量k_BT_K的光谱方法，与热力学测量结果一致，并证明软X射线RIXS可作为定量探测强关联材料中低能和高能尺度杂化效应的体敏感探针。

Abstract: The low-energy spin- and charge-sensitive thermodynamic properties of a broad range of strongly correlated 4f-electron systems follow Kondo scaling, with a characteristic Kondo temperature, $T_K$. While the theory is known for thermodynamic properties and high-energy spectroscopies of Kondo materials, the surface sensitivity of electron spectroscopy limits the extent to which Kondo scaling can be quantitatively verified. In this study, bulk-sensitive photon-in photon-out temperature-dependent resonant inelastic X-ray scattering (RIXS), in combination with single-impurity Anderson model (SIAM) calculations, is used to provide quantitative evidence of low- and high-energy Kondo scaling in CeSi$_2$. RIXS Ce M$_5$-edge spectra show a clear decrease in the occupancy of the $f^0$ state as temperature increases accompanied by an increase of the spectral weight of the $f^1\underline L^1$ state, in good agreement with the SIAM calculations. The results demonstrate the breakdown of the Kondo singlet state, coupled with thermal occupation of the low-lying first-excited magnetic states. The RIXS data reveal a temperature evolution of the $f^n$ spectral weights, which is in stark contrast to that extracted from photoemission and inverse photoemission spectroscopies. This study provides an accurate spectroscopic method to determine the Kondo energy $k_B$$T_K$ that is consistent with thermodynamic measurements, and highlights soft X-ray RIXS as a quantitative bulk probe of low- and high-energy-scale hybridization effects in strongly correlated materials.

</details>


### [116] [Quantitative thermodynamic study of superconducting and normal states in UTe2 under pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29760)
*T. Vasina,M. Pfeiffer,R. Borth,M. Nicklas,M. Amano Patino,G. Lapertot,J. -P. Brison,E. Hassinger,G. Knebel,D. Braithwaite*

Method: 采用定量量热学研究方法，直接测量UTe₂在压力下的Sommerfeld系数γ，分析γ随两个超导转变处比热跳跃幅度的演化，以及超导临界温度随压力的变化。

Conclusion: 分析表明，被称为弱磁有序的未识别相的量子临界点可能起主要作用，而非反铁磁相的临界压力。在长程反铁磁有序边界处，超导性从弱磁有序相中出现时，比热跳跃的显著增加和形状变化揭示了超导转变与磁性有序之间的复杂相互作用。

Abstract: We report a quantitative calorimetric study of UTe2 under pressure with a direct measurement of the Sommerfeld gamma coefficient, showing a three-fold enhancement of electronic effective mass when approaching the critical pressure where superconductivity is suppressed and ordered states occur. We analyse the evolution of gamma with the amplitude of the jumps in the specific heat at the two superconducting transitions, and the superconducting critical temperature with pressure. This analysis would suggest that the high pressure superconducting phase nucleates only on a fraction of the Fermi surface. It also points to the possible major role of a quantum critical point of the unidentified phase that has been called weak magnetic order, rather than to the critical pressure of the antiferromagnetic phase. Just at the border of long-range antiferromagnetic order, where superconductivity emerges from the weak magnetic order phase, a significant increase in the specific heat jump for both superconducting transitions is found, accompanied by a noticeable change of their shapes.

### [117] [A Covariant Phase Space Approach to Einstein-AEther Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28851)
*Walter Arata,Stefano Liberati,Giulio Neri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在洛伦兹破缺（Lorentz-violating）的爱因斯坦-以太（Einstein-AEther）引力理论中，通过协变相空间（covariant phase space）方法推导了稳态黑洞的一致第一定律，并发展了扩展热力学框架，解决了文献中关于熵和温度定义的明显矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 洛伦兹破缺引力中的黑洞热力学具有微妙性，因为不同激发以不同速度传播，从而识别不同的因果视界（causal horizon）。本文旨在重新审视爱因斯坦-以太引力理论，建立一致的热力学描述。

Method: 采用带边界的协变相空间形式体系（covariant phase space formalism），为传播速度为$c_s$的模式引入一个反形式框架（disformal frame），使相应的因果视界成为Killing视界，从而能够进行标准的Wald型推导，然后将结果映射回原始框架。

Result: 推导出的视界荷（horizon charge）包含通常的Komar项和不可约的以太熵贡献，可解释为以太穿过视界的通量所产生的热量；总熵分裂为引力部分和以太部分。建立了扩展热力学框架，允许理论耦合变化，得到广义Smarr关系。

Conclusion: 通过适当考虑独立的以太贡献，调和了文献中两种看似矛盾的方法：一种固定熵与面积成正比并推断相应温度，另一种施加与从普适视界（universal horizon）剥离的模式相关的霍金温度并推断熵。两种方案在正确考虑以太贡献后得到协调。

Abstract: Black hole thermodynamics in Lorentz-violating gravity is subtle because different excitations propagate at different speeds and hence identify different causal horizons. We revisit Einstein--AEther gravity using the covariant phase space formalism with boundaries and derive a consistent first law for stationary black holes. For a mode of propagation speed $c_s$, we introduce a disformal frame in which the corresponding causal horizon is a Killing horizon, so that the standard Wald-type derivation can be carried out. The result is then mapped back to the original frame, where it mantains the same structure. The associated horizon charge contains, besides the usual Komar term, an irreducible entropic AEther contribution that can be interpreted as heat due to the AEther flux across the horizon; accordingly, the total entropy splits into a gravitational part and an AEther part. We further develop an extended-thermodynamics framework in which the couplings of the theory are allowed to vary, obtaining generalized Smarr relations. Finally, we analyze the probe-mode limit $c_s \to +\infty$, clarifying its connection to universal-horizon thermodynamics and resolving the apparent tension in the literature between approaches that (i) fix the entropy to be proportional to the area and infer a corresponding temperature, and (ii) impose the Hawking temperature associated with modes peeling from the universal horizon and infer the entropy. Once the independent AEther contribution is properly taken into account, the two prescriptions are reconciled.

</details>


### [118] [Charged scalar fields on Reissner--Nordström spacetimes II: late-time tails and instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28861)
*Dejan Gajic*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文作为系列论文第二部分，通过纯物理空间方法建立了带电标量场在近极端Reissner-Nordström时空上的精确晚期行为，包括满足逆幂律的振荡衰减尾迹，无需假设小电荷条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究带电标量场在黑洞背景下的精确晚期行为与（不）稳定性性质，特别关注无需小电荷假设的点态衰减估计。这些分析将为未来非线性黑洞动力学研究提供重要基础。

Method: 采用纯物理空间方法（purely physical-space based methods），基于全局积分能量衰减估计（global integrated energy decay estimates）建立带电标量场方程的精确晚期行为。该方法不依赖于小电荷假设。

Result: 首次获得了无需小电荷假设的黑洞背景下带电标量场的点态衰减估计（pointwise decay estimates），证明了满足逆幂律的振荡衰减晚期尾迹。同时证明了沿未来类光无限远（future null infinity）和极端情况下的未来事件视界（future event horizon）存在渐近不稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文建立的能量方法和精确晚期渐近行为预计将在球对称（Einstein-）Maxwell-带电标量场方程以及极端Kerr时空的黑洞动力学非线性研究中发挥重要作用。

Abstract: This is the second part of a series of papers deriving the precise, late-time behaviour and (in)stability properties of charged scalar fields on near-extremal Reissner--Nordström spacetimes via energy estimates. In this paper, we use purely physical-space based methods to establish the precise late-time behaviour of solutions to the charged scalar field equation in the form of oscillating and decaying late-time tails that satisfy inverse-power laws, assuming global integrated energy decay estimates, which are proved in the companion paper [Gaj26].
  This paper provides the first pointwise decay estimates for charged scalar fields on black hole backgrounds without an assumption of smallness of the scalar field charge.
  We also prove the existence of asymptotic instabilities for the radiation field along future null infinity and, in the extremal case, also along the future event horizon. Both the energy methods and the precise late-time asymptotics derived in this paper are expected to play an important role in future nonlinear studies of black hole dynamics in the context of the spherically symmetric (Einstein--)Maxwell--charged scalar field equations, as well as in the context of extremal Kerr spacetimes.

</details>


### [119] [The Depletion of Collisionless Dark Matter Spikes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28866)
*Charlie Sharpe,Yonadav Barry Ginat,Thomas F. M. Spieksma,Bence Kocsis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了经典Gondolo-Silk模型中黑洞周围暗物质尖峰（DM spike）的稳定性，发现在核星团环境中，质量分层加速弛豫过程，而极端质量比旋近（EMRIs）通过弹弓效应（slingshots）不可逆地耗尽暗物质，显著降低了LISA可探测的暗物质尖峰参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞周围的致密暗物质分布为探测暗物质本质提供了重要机会。经典Gondolo-Silk模型预测黑洞绝热增长会形成陡峭的暗物质尖峰（ρ∝r^{-7/3}），可能通过中度和极端质量比旋近（IMRIs/EMRIs）产生可测量的引力波相位偏移（gravitational-wave dephasings）。

Method: 研究采用一维轨道平均Fokker-Planck（FP）模拟各向同性核星团（NSC），分析多质量恒星尖峰中的质量分层（mass segregation）效应。在FP描述失效的内区，使用后牛顿三体模拟（post-Newtonian 3-body simulations）建模暗物质粒子与EMRIs之间的强三重相互作用。

Result: 多质量恒星尖峰中的质量分层加速弛豫过程，使暗物质在≲1 Gyr内演化为较低密度的Bahcall-Wolf分布（r^{-3/2}）。EMRIs通过弹弓效应（slingshots）在几Gyr内耗尽内区暗物质尖峰，且这种耗尽是**不可逆的**，因为EMRI数密度不足以驱动二体弛豫，而无碰撞暗物质无法有效重新填充耗尽的相空间。

Conclusion: EMRI诱导的暗物质耗尽显著降低了暗物质密度（数个数量级），使得LISA在z=3（2.14 Gyr）对质量≲10^5 M⊙（EMRI率约10 Gyr^{-1}）或更乐观情况下≲10^6 M⊙的黑洞的暗物质诱导相位偏移探测阈值可能无法达到。这些发现**大幅缩小**了可容纳可探测无碰撞暗物质尖峰的大质量黑洞参数空间。

Abstract: Dense concentrations of dark matter (DM) surrounding black holes provide a compelling opportunity to probe the nature of DM. In the classic Gondolo-Silk model, the adiabatic growth of a massive black hole (MBH) in a DM cusp produces a steep density spike ($ρ\propto r^{-7/3}$), potentially inducing measurable gravitational-wave dephasings in intermediate and extreme mass-ratio inspirals (IMRIs/EMRIs). We challenge this paradigm by considering a collisionless spike embedded in a realistic nuclear star cluster (NSC). Using 1D orbit-averaged Fokker-Planck (FP) simulations of isotropic NSCs, we show that mass segregation in a multi-mass stellar cusp accelerates relaxation, relative to single-mass models, thereby driving the DM to the lower density $r^{-3/2}$ Bahcall-Wolf profile within $\lesssim 1 \mathrm{Gyr}$. In the inner regions, where the FP description breaks down, we model strong triple interactions between DM particles and EMRIs using post-Newtonian 3-body simulations. We show that EMRIs eject DM particles via slingshots, depleting the inner spike over a few Gyrs. Because EMRI number densities are too low to drive two-body relaxation, and collisionless DM cannot efficiently repopulate the depleted phase space, this depletion is irreversible. While the extent of EMRI-induced depletion depends on the EMRI rate and mass, we find reductions in DM densities by several orders of magnitude. Hence, DM-induced dephasings for EMRIs may fall below the detectability threshold of LISA for MBHs at $z = 3$ (2.14 Gyr) with masses $\lesssim 10^{5}\,M_\odot$ (for an $\mathcal{O}(10) \, \mathrm{Gyr}^{-1}$ EMRI rate), extending to $\lesssim 10^6\,M_\odot$ for more optimistic rates of $\mathcal{O}(300-1000) \, \mathrm{Gyr}^{-1}$. Our findings substantially reduce the parameter space over which MBHs can host detectable collisionless DM spikes.

Abstract: This is the first part of a series of papers deriving the precise, late-time behaviour and (in)stability properties of charged scalar fields on near-extremal Reissner--Nordström spacetimes via energy estimates. In this paper, we establish global, weighted integrated energy decay and energy boundedness estimates for solutions to the charged scalar field equation on (near-)extremal Reissner--Nordström(--de Sitter) spacetimes. These estimates extend to Reissner--Nordström spacetimes away from extremality under the assumption of mode stability on the real axis.
  Together with the companion paper [Gaj26], this paper forms the first global quantitative analysis of the charged scalar field equation on asymptotically flat black hole spacetimes, without a smallness assumption on the scalar field charge. Due to a coupling of the degeneration of the red-shift effect with the presence of superradiance at the linearized level, charged scalar fields on Reissner--Nordström spacetimes also probe some of the main difficulties encountered when studying the (neutral) wave equation on extremal Kerr spacetimes.

### [121] [Spin the black circle II: tidal heating and torquing of a rotating black hole by a test mass on generic orbits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28982)
*Rossella Gamba,Danilo Chiaramello,Estuti Shukla,Simone Albanesi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值研究克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）赤道轨道上测试粒子的视界能量和角动量通量（horizon fluxes），揭示了圆形、偏心率和双曲线轨道的复杂通量现象，并提出了改进的解析后牛顿（post-Newtonian）表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值方法研究测试粒子在克尔黑洞赤道测地线（equatorial geodesics）上的轨道，涵盖圆形、偏心率和双曲线轨迹，覆盖广泛的轨道参数和黑洞自旋范围。将数值结果与现有解析后牛顿表达式进行比较，并探索重整化（resummation）策略以改进其性能。

Result: 数值研究重现了圆形轨道的已知结果，并揭示了偏心率和双曲线轨道更丰富的现象学：瞬时通量（instantaneous fluxes）可呈现多个峰值和符号变化，表明超辐射（superradiant）与非超辐射（non-superradiant）机制间的复杂相互作用。提出的因子化重整化通量表示（factorized and resummed representation）能预测超辐射机制的起始频率，对于≥73%的配置，能量和角动量通量的预测误差在10%以内。

Conclusion: 解析模型在大分离距离和低偏心率下能达到可接受的精度（相对误差在10%水平或以下），但在强场区域（strong-field regime）可能出现约100%的偏差，这表明需要改进通量描述并开展进一步研究。提出的重整化表示通过构造精确还原到圆形极限，独立于剩余解析项的微扰阶数。

Abstract: Horizon fluxes of energy and angular momentum are a key strong-field effect in the dynamics of black holes, encoding direct information about their nature. In this work, we present a numerical study of these fluxes for a test particle orbiting a Kerr black hole on equatorial geodesics, covering circular, eccentric, and hyperbolic trajectories across a wide range of orbital parameters and black hole spins. We reproduce known results for circular orbits and uncover a richer phenomenology for eccentric and hyperbolic ones: the instantaneous fluxes can exhibit multiple peaks and sign changes, indicating a complex interplay between superradiant and non-superradiant regimes. We then compare these results against existing analytical post-Newtonian expressions, exploring resummation strategies to improve their performance against numerical data. In particular, we propose a factorized and resummed representation of the horizon fluxes that predicts the onset frequency of the superradiant regime to within $10\%$ for $\gtrsim 73\%$ of configurations for both the energy and angular momentum fluxes. This representation exactly reduces to the circular limit by construction, independently of the perturbative order of the remaining analytical terms. For peak and orbit-averaged fluxes, the analytical models achieve acceptable accuracy -- with relative errors at the $10\%$ level or below -- at large separations and low eccentricities. However, they can exhibit deviations of $\sim \mathcal{O}(100\%)$ in the strong-field regime, motivating the need for improved flux prescriptions and further investigations.

### [122] [No hair but plenty of feathers: are birds black holes?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29064)
*Andrew Laeuger,Taylor Knapp*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于"chirp"一词的语言学重叠：该词既指16世纪中古英语中的鸟类模仿动词，又自1990年代以来用于描述致密天体（如黑洞和中子星）合并产生的引力波（gravitational waves）。纯粹基于这种语言学联系，作者探索鸟类鸣叫是否可用致密双星波形建模。

Method: 方法上，作者以北红雀（Northern cardinal, Cardinalis cardinalis）为测试案例，将其时间反转的鸣叫（time-reversed chirp）与致密双星波形进行比较。特别关注高质量比、进动黑洞双星（high mass ratio, precessing black hole binary）的波形特征。

Result: 研究发现北红雀的时间反转鸣叫可近似建模为高质量比、进动黑洞双星的波形，并显示出极端物质效应或超越标准模型物理（beyond the Standard Model physics）的迹象。然而，并非所有鸟类鸣叫都适用此对应关系，某些鸣叫形态更类似于引力波天文台观测到的故障信号（glitches）。

Conclusion: 基于波形比较，作者提出了对"鸡与蛋"哲学难题的替代解决方案：或许并非鸡或蛋谁先出现，而是宇宙大爆炸（Big Bang）真正最先发生。这一结论将语言学观察延伸至宇宙学哲学思考。

Abstract: The imitative verb "chirp" is thought to originate from 16th-century Middle English. Meanwhile, this same word has been used to describe the gravitational waves (GWs) emitted from the merger of compact objects, such as black holes and neutron stars, since at least the 1990s. Motivated purely by this linguistic overlap, we study whether the chirps of birds can be modeled by compact binary waveforms. In particular, we consider a test case of the Northern cardinal (Cardinalis cardinalis), finding that its time-reversed chirp can be approximately modeled by that of a high mass ratio, precessing black hole binary, with a number of indications towards extreme matter effects or beyond the Standard Model physics. Importantly, this waveform correspondence is not so straightforward for all bird species, as some chirp morphologies are far more akin to glitches seen in GW observatories. With these comparisons made, we propose an alternative solution to the longstanding philosophical conundrum: rather than the chicken or the egg, perhaps it was the Big Bang which truly came first.

### [123] [Photon emission from the ISCO of a rotating black hole in Asymptotic Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29156)
*Miguel A. Enrí quez,Luis A. Sánchez*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索量子引力效应如何影响旋转黑洞最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）的光子发射特性，特别是比较渐进安全（asymptotic safety）框架下的量子黑洞与经典Kerr黑洞在光子逃逸概率（PEP）和最大可观测蓝移（MOB）方面的差异。

Method: 研究方法包括计算亚极端旋转黑洞在渐进安全框架下ISCO的光子逃逸概率和最大可观测蓝移，并与经典Kerr黑洞的相应结果进行对比分析，重点关注量子参数（quantum parameter）对ISCO半径和光子发射特性的影响。

Result: 研究发现，尽管量子引力效应减小了ISCO半径，但在高自旋旋转黑洞中，当量子参数趋近其临界值时，光子逃逸概率和最大可观测蓝移反而增加，这表明量子引力效应在ISCO层面开始主导经典背景。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，量子引力效应对旋转黑洞ISCO光子发射特性的影响与经典预期相反，这些量子修正与渐进安全框架下旋转黑洞阴影的特定特征存在关联，为通过观测检验量子引力理论提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the isotropic emission of photons from the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) of a subextremal rotating black hole (BH) in asymptotic safety (AS). We calculate both the photon escape probability (PEP) and the maximum observable blueshift (MOB) of photons to reach infinity, and compare with the corresponding results for photon emission from the ISCO of a classical Kerr BH. In AS, quantum gravity effects reduce the radius of the ISCO, therefore quantum gravity effects should reduce the PEP and MOB of photons from emitters moving on the ISCO. We show that this is not the case and that, when rotating BHs with high spin are considered and the quantum parameter (which encodes the quantum gravity effects) increases towards its critical value, which is different for different spin values, the PEP and MOB also increase despite the reduction in ISCO radius. Our results on the PEP show explicitly how quantum gravity effects start to dominate over the classical background at the level of the ISCO. We also discuss the relation between these quantum gravity modifications and particular features of the shadow of a rotating BH in AS.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A novel semiclassical gravity model proposed by Oppenheim et al., that consistently describes interactions between quantum systems and a classical gravitational field, has recently attracted considerable attention. However, the limitations and phenomenological viability of this model have not yet been thoroughly investigated. In this work, based on the model, we study quantum fluctuations of geodesic deviation coupled with a classical gravitational field. We analytically derive the strain spectrum expected from the fluctuations and show that the original Oppenheim et al. model can be tested with the current observational sensitivity of gravitational-wave experiments. Furthermore, motivated by the novel semiclassical model, we construct two additional models: a modified Oppenheim et al. model that is manifestly consistent with Einstein equation, and a classical-quantum model with environment-induced noise. We analyze the strain spectra predicted by these two models through comparison with those of the original Oppenheim et al. model and perturbative quantum gravity.

### [125] [Quantum Einsteinian Cubic Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29304)
*Nephtalí Eliceo Martínez Pérez,Cupatitzio Ramírez Romero*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在迷你超空间量子宇宙学框架下分析宇宙学爱因斯坦立方引力理论（CECG）。通过哈密顿公式化和Wheeler-DeWitt量子化，获得了空间平坦情况的精确解和空间闭合情况的WKB近似解，并探讨了含暴胀势标量场的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索爱因斯坦立方引力理论（CECG）在量子宇宙学背景下的行为。CECG作为爱因斯坦引力的立方曲率修正，能在保持弗里德曼方程为二阶的同时，对FRW背景动力学产生非平凡贡献，这为研究高阶导数引力理论的量子性质提供了理想平台。

Method: 研究方法采用哈密顿公式化，使用Ostrogradski正则变量和Dirac约束系统算法处理有效一维FRW CECG作用量。通过正则变换$(a,p_a)\to (A,P)$显式写出哈密顿约束，随后进行Wheeler-DeWitt量子化。对于空间闭合情况采用WKB近似方法，并引入含暴胀势的均匀标量场。

Result: 研究获得了空间平坦FRW背景的精确Wheeler-DeWitt方程解，以及空间闭合情况的WKB型近似解。虽然FRW CECG除了标度因子外没有额外自由度，但其非标准哈密顿量产生了高阶导数Wheeler-DeWitt方程。在引入暴胀势标量场后，得到了导致坐标与动量强相关的WKB波函数。

Conclusion: 该研究成功实现了宇宙学爱因斯坦立方引力理论（CECG）在迷你超空间量子宇宙学中的哈密顿公式化和量子化。尽管理论具有高阶导数特性，但仍可获得解析解，为研究高阶曲率修正引力理论的量子性质提供了重要范例。

Abstract: We study Cosmological Einsteinian Cubic Gravity (CECG) arXiv:1810.08166v3 in the context of minisuperspace quantum cosmology. CECG is a modification of Einstein's gravity by cubic curvature terms that yield a nontrivial contribution to the dynamics of FRW backgrounds while keeping the Friedmann equations at second order. First, we study the Hamiltonian formulation of the effective one-dimensional FRW CECG action using Ostrogradski's canonical variables and Dirac's algorithm for constrained systems. Since the momentum $p_a$ conjugate to the scale factor is a polynomial of degree five in $\dot{a}$, we implement canonical transformations $(a,p_a)\to (A,P)$ that enable us to write the Hamiltonian constraint explicitly. Second, we perform the Wheeler-DeWitt quantization using the new canonical variables. Although FRW CECG has no extra degree of freedom besides the scale factor, its non-standard Hamiltonian yields a higher-derivative Wheeler-DeWitt equation. We obtain exact solutions for the spatially flat case, and WKB-type solutions for the spatially closed case. Finally, we consider a homogeneous scalar field $φ$ with inflationary potential and obtain WKB wave functions leading to strong correlations between coordinates and momenta.

</details>


### [126] [Revisiting the Coprecessing Frame in the Presence of Orbital Eccentricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29307)
*Lucy M. Thomas,Katerina Chatziioannou,Sam Johar,Taylor Knapp,Michael Boyle*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究评估了共进动框架变换（coprecessing frame transformation）在同时包含轨道偏心率和自旋进动效应的引力波波形建模中的效用与局限性。研究发现该变换能降低波形失配但未达到精确建模所需水平，同时有助于代理建模（surrogate modeling）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波波形模型中同时精确包含自旋进动（spin precession）和轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity）效应是准确表征致密双星系统特性的关键挑战。当前大多数进动建模都依赖于共进动框架变换，但该变换在非零偏心率情况下的有效性需要评估。

Method: 研究基于20个数值相对论（numerical relativity）模拟，这些模拟包含了强场区域中完整的自旋进动和偏心率物理效应。通过比较惯性框架（inertial frame）和共进动框架中的波形，并参考偏心自旋对齐模型SEOBNRv5EHM进行评估。

Result: 在共进动框架中波形失配（waveform mismatches）有所降低，但仍高于精确波形建模所需水平（约0.01或更高，对于大倾角情况）。该框架通过去除波形中的主要振幅和相位调制，有助于代理建模，在固定基元数量下相比惯性框架获得更低误差。

Conclusion: 共进动框架作为偏心进动双星波形建模的基石具有实用价值但也存在局限性。需要进一步改进，例如对模式不对称性（mode asymmetries）进行建模，正如在准圆轨道双星中已开展的工作。

Abstract: Accurate inclusion of both spin precession and orbital eccentricity effects in gravitational waveform models represents a key hurdle in our ability to fully characterize the properties of compact binaries. Virtually all efforts to model precession rely on a coprecessing frame transformation, a time-dependent spatial rotation that tracks the dominant emission direction and simplifies the waveform morphology. We assess the utility of the coprecessing frame transformation to separate out the effect of the precession of the orbital plane from the waveform in the presence of non-negligible orbital eccentricity. We rely on 20 numerical relativity simulations, which include the complete physical effects of spin precession and eccentricity in the strong-field, and compare waveforms in both the inertial and coprecessing frames. Comparing against the eccentric, spin-aligned model SEOBNRv5EHM, we find that while the waveform mismatches decrease in the coprecessing frame, they remain above the level required for accurate waveform modeling, $\sim$ 0.01 or higher for large inclinations. Further improvements, e.g., modeling mode asymmetries as already pursued for quasicircular binaries, will likely prove essential. We also find that by removing the dominant amplitude and phase modulations from the waveform, the coprecessing frame facilitates surrogate modeling, achieving lower errors at a fixed number of basis elements compared to the inertial frame. Our results demonstrate both the utility and the limitations of the coprecessing frame as a cornerstone in waveform modeling for eccentric and precessing binaries.

### [127] [Extracting Energy from Magnetized Rotating Black Holes in Horndeski Gravity via the Magnetic Penrose Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29319)
*Ke Wang,Xiao-Xiong Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在Horndeski引力理论中，基于磁彭罗斯过程（Magnetic Penrose Process）研究了从浸没在均匀磁场中的旋转黑洞提取能量的方法。通过理论分析和数值模拟，分析了能量提取效率与毛参数（hair parameter）的关系，发现毛参数越大，黑洞的能层（ergosphere）和负能区域越小，且效率变化取决于衰变半径（decay radius）和磁场参数的特定组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在Horndeski引力理论框架下，如何从浸没在均匀磁场中的旋转黑洞提取能量。该研究基于磁彭罗斯过程（Magnetic Penrose Process），旨在探索黑洞的毛参数（hair parameter）对能量提取效率的影响。

Method: 通过映射该时空的能层（ergosphere）和负能区域，结合理论分析和数值模拟，研究能量提取效率与毛参数（hair parameter）之间的关系。分析了不同衰变半径（decay radius）和磁场参数（$\hat{q}B$）条件下的效率变化规律。

Result: 毛参数$h$越大，黑洞的能层（ergosphere）和负能区域越小。当$\hat{q}B \geq 0$时：若衰变半径$r_x > 2$，效率随$h$增大而减小；若$r_x < 2$，效率随$h$增大而增大；若$r_x = 2$，效率与$h$无关。当$\hat{q}B < 0$时，除$r_x = 2$外，效率随$h$的变化取决于$r_x$和$\hat{q}B$的具体值，可能单调递减或先增后减。

Conclusion: 在Horndeski引力中，磁彭罗斯过程的能量提取效率强烈依赖于黑洞的毛参数（hair parameter）、衰变半径（decay radius）和磁场条件。无磁场时，$r_x > 2$的效率为负且无意义；$\hat{q}B \geq 0$时，$h$越大最大效率越低；$\hat{q}B < 0$时，小磁场下效率为负，大磁场下带毛黑洞在高衰变半径处可获得正的高效率，而Kerr黑洞效率仍为负。

Abstract: In Horndeski gravity, we investigate how to extract energy from a rotating black hole immersed in a uniform magnetic field $B$ based on the Magnetic Penrose Process. We map the ergosphere and negative energy regions of this spacetime, and analyze the relationship between the energy extraction efficiency and the hair parameter through both theoretical analysis and numerical simulations. The results show that the larger the hair parameter $h$, the smaller the ergosphere and negative energy regions of the black hole. For the same decay radius, in the case of $\hat{q} B \geq 0$, if the decay radius $r_x > 2$, the efficiency decreases as $h$ increases; if $r_x < 2$, the efficiency increases as $h$ increases; if $r_x = 2$, the efficiency is independent of $h$. However, when $\hat{q}B < 0$, except for the special case $r_x = 2$ where the efficiency is independent of $h$, the variation of efficiency with $h$ depends on the specific values of $r_x$ and $\hat{q}B$, and may exhibit either monotonic decrease or an initial increase followed by a decrease. We also find that in the absence of a magnetic field, the efficiency is negative and meaningless when $r_x > 2$, and such cases are excluded. In addition, when $\hat{q} B \geq 0$, the larger the $h$, the lower the maximum efficiency; when $\hat{q} B < 0$, in the case of a small magnetic field, the efficiency is negative and meaningless, while in the case of a large magnetic field, the efficiency of the black hole with hair is positive at high decay radius and reaches a high value, whereas the efficiency of the Kerr black hole remains negative.

*Frederic V. Hessman,Christian Jooss*

Method: 研究方法包括分析蟾蜍叫声与引力波信号的相似性，推测其神经系统中的铁磁物质可能通过声子（phonons）和磁振子（magnons）机制检测引力波应变，并利用拉曼激光（Raman laser）机制进行指数放大。同时分析了池塘中蟾蜍叫声的相位偏移，试图检测引力波事件的影响。

Result: 研究未发现蟾蜍叫声因引力波事件而产生的相位偏移，且LIGO/VIRGO联盟在录音期间未报告相关事件。这一结果验证了该方法的有效性，表明蟾蜍叫声分析可作为引力波探测的补充验证手段。

Conclusion: 结论认为大规模使用墨西哥穴居蟾蜍可作为光学干涉引力波探测器（optical interferometric gravitational wave detector）设施的低成本支持方式。该机制所需的精细调节解释了为何仅此物种具备这种非凡能力。

Abstract: It is generally assumed that gravitational waves are extremely difficult to detect. However, we show that the call of the Mexican Burrowing Toad has an amazing resemblance to cosmic gravitational wave signals due to the merging of neutron stars and/or black holes. It is known that toads exhibit magnetoreception - the ability to detect magnetic fields - and that magnetic fields thus subtly affect ion channel activities in toad neurons. We speculate that gravitational strains produce phonons and magnons in a ferromagnetic substance embedded in the nervous system of the toads and that these coherent signals are exponentially amplified by a Raman laser mechanism to the point where they can be detected. The fine tuning necessary for this mechanism to work would help to explain why this species of toad show this remarkable ability and others do not. We analyze the sound of a pond full of Mexican Burrowing Toads in the hopes of detecting slight phase shifts in their calls due to a gravitational wave event. No effect was found and the the LIGO/VIRGO consortia have not reported an event during the recording, illustrating the power of this approach. We suggest the massive use of these toads would be an inexpensive way to support the operation of optical interferometric gravitational wave detector facilities.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用包含物质拉格朗日量（matter Lagrangian）线性和指数依赖的函数形式，通过引入适当的无量纲变量构建自治系统（autonomous system）。对临界点进行详细动力系统分析，并运用中心流形理论（center manifold theory）确定非双曲临界点的稳定性。进一步扩展模型，加入具有动能项和指数自相互作用势的最小耦合广义标量场。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the cosmological dynamics of the $f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$ gravity framework with a particular focus on the contributions of the scalar field. Considering a functional form that includes linear and exponential dependence on the matter Lagrangian, we perform a detailed dynamical system analysis by introducing appropriate dimensionless variables and constructing the corresponding autonomous system. The critical points are obtained and analyzed, and due to their non-hyperbolic nature, center manifold theory is employed to determine their stability. The analysis reveals the existence of matter-dominated and accelerated phases of the Universe, along with a transition from a decelerated to an accelerated expansion. We further extend the model by incorporating a minimally coupled generalized scalar field with a kinetic term and an exponential self-interacting potential, which enriches the dynamical behavior and leads to stable late-time attractor solutions. The evolution of cosmological parameters, including the deceleration parameter and the effective equation of state, indicates that the model approaches a de Sitter-like phase at late times. These results demonstrate that the $f(R, \mathcal{L}_m)$ gravity framework, with scalar field extensions, provides a viable mechanism to explain the late-time acceleration of the Universe without invoking a cosmological constant.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过考虑相对论效应和不同间隙区域（极冠和外间隙），估计连续引力波的应变幅度。方法涉及对磁层中电场能量密度变化的物理建模。

Result: 极冠区域的引力波应变过小，与先前研究结果相反；而外间隙区域的应变可达~2×10⁻²⁴，这一幅度足以被未来的引力波探测器如爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）探测到。

Abstract: The pulsar magnetosphere is a potential source of continuous gravitational waves due to the rapid charge-discharge process in short timescale, varying the electric-field energy density. We estimate the strain of the continuous gravitational waves, considering relativistic effects and different gap regions. We find that the strain from the polar cap is too small, in contrast to previous results. On the other hand, the strain from the outer gap is as large as $\sim2\times10^{-24}$, enough for future gravitational-wave detection such as the Einstein Telescope. Our result presents a new approach for the future detection of gravitational waves to probe the physics in the magnetosphere.

### [131] [Towards Gravitational Wave Turbulence within the Hadad-Zakharov metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29699)
*Benoît Gay,Eugeny Babichev,Sébastien Galtier,Karim Noui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在广义相对论框架下，使用Hadad-Zakharov度量研究引力波湍流（gravitational wave turbulence），通过解析分析和GPU数值模拟验证了弱非线性条件下爱因斯坦方程的兼容性，并揭示了双级联（dual cascade）和间歇性相干结构等典型湍流特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波湍流理论描述弱非线性相互作用波的长期统计行为。本研究旨在广义相对论框架内，使用Hadad-Zakharov度量研究引力湍流，特别关注该度量中七个非平凡爱因斯坦方程的相互兼容性问题，这一问题此前被忽视。

Method: 采用Hadad-Zakharov度量参数化方法，该度量由四个函数（对角度量系数）描述，需满足七个非平凡爱因斯坦方程。研究结合解析分析和基于GPU的新代码TIGER进行直接数值模拟，比较Ricci标量和Kretschmann标量的演化。

Result: 解析研究表明，在特定条件下弱非线性区域中这些方程可以兼容。数值模拟显示引力波湍流对应真实物理自由度的传播，并再现了波湍流（wave turbulence）的双级联（dual cascade）和Kolmogorov-Zakharov谱。正则变量（canonical variables）演化趋向近高斯统计分布，但存在间歇性相干结构；而规范不变度量分量的结构函数（structure functions）呈现单分形（monofractal）行为。

Conclusion: 引力波湍流在弱非线性条件下可能实现，表现为典型的波湍流统计特征，包括能量和波作用（wave action）的双级联、Kolmogorov-Zakharov谱、近高斯分布伴随间歇性相干结构，以及规范不变分量的单分形行为。但需谨慎解释数值结果，因同时满足所有七个爱因斯坦方程具有挑战性。

Abstract: The theory of gravitational wave turbulence describes the long-term statistical behaviour of a set of weakly nonlinear interacting waves. In this paper, we aim to study aspects of gravitational turbulence within the framework of general relativity using the Hadad-Zakharov (HZ) metric. The latter is parameterised by four functions (the coefficients of a diagonal metric) that must satisfy seven non-trivial Einstein equations, six of which are independent. The issue of their mutual compatibility is therefore essential, yet it has so far been overlooked. In this work, we argue that these equations can be compatible in the weakly nonlinear regime under specific conditions. Our analytical investigation is complemented by direct numerical simulations performed with a new GPU-based code, TIGER. A comparative analysis of the evolution of the Ricci and Kretschmann scalars indicates that gravitational wave turbulence corresponds to the propagation of a genuine physical degree of freedom. These numerical findings, however, must be interpreted with caution, given the difficulty of satisfying all seven Einstein equations simultaneously with sufficient accuracy. On the other hand, our simulations reproduce well the expected properties of the wave turbulence regime, with the emergence of a dual cascade of energy and wave action, and for the latter the observation of the Kolmogorov-Zakharov spectrum. In addition, our analysis reveals that the canonical variables of the problem evolve towards a nearly Gaussian statistical distribution punctuated by intermittent coherent (spatially localised and long-living) structures. In contrast to the canonical variables, the structure functions of the gauge-invariant metric components exhibit monofractal behaviour, which is a classical property of wave turbulence.

### [132] [On the mapping between bound states and black hole quasinormal modes via analytic continuation: a spectral instability perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29704)
*Guan-Ru Li,Wei-Liang Qian,Xiao-Mei Kuang,Ramin G. Daghigh,Jodin C. Morey,Michael D. Green,Peng Xu,Rui-Hong Yue*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了黑洞微扰理论中束缚态与准正则模（quasinormal modes）在谱不稳定性（spectral instability）背景下的关系，发现谱映射的可靠性超出了解析延拓（analytic continuation）的有效域，但数值方案要求参数变换在泰勒展开（Taylor expansion）收敛区域内进行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究黑洞微扰理论中束缚态与准正则模之间的关系，特别是在谱不稳定性背景下，以审视束缚态能否忠实编码准正则谱的条件，并阐明黑洞谱不稳定性的基础物理机制。

Method: 采用解析可处理的显式例子，包括微扰的δ函数（delta-function）和Pöschl-Teller势垒（potential barriers）。对于后者，构建了两个不同的微扰设置，其中微扰理论涉及的级数展开（series expansion）收敛性可以严格控制。

Result: 当变形位于势的极值点附近时，束缚态能量的修正可以通过解析延拓得到微扰后的准正则频率，与已知的半解析结果一致。然而，当微扰局域于远离致密天体的渐近区域时，束缚态仅轻微修正且可由一阶微扰展开准确描述，但相关的解析延拓产生强烈变形的谱，与准正则模无明显关联。

Conclusion: 这些发现有助于审视束缚态忠实编码准正则谱的条件，并阐明黑洞谱不稳定性的基础物理机制。研究结果表明谱映射的可靠性超出了所采用解析延拓的有效域，但数值方案要求参数变换在泰勒展开收敛区域内进行。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the relation between bound states and quasinormal modes within black hole perturbation theory in the context of spectral instability. Our analysis indicates that the reliability of such spectral mapping stretches beyond the domain of validity of the analytic continuation employed to connect the perturbative bound-state problem to the corresponding open-system dynamics. However, for the numerical scheme proposed by Völkel to work, the transformations of the metric parameters must be carried out in a region where the underlying Taylor expansion is convergent. As analytically accessible explicit examples, we explore the perturbed delta-function and Pöschl-Teller potential barriers. For the latter, we construct two distinct perturbative setups for which the convergence of the series expansion involved in the perturbation theory can be rigorously controlled. When the deformation is placed near the potential's extremum, the resulting corrections to the bound-state energies can be analytically continued to yield perturbed quasinormal frequencies, in agreement with known semi-analytic results. In contrast, when the perturbation is localized asymptotically far from the compact object, the bound states are only mildly modified and are accurately described by a perturbative expansion to the first order. However, the associated analytic continuation yields a strongly deformed spectrum that shows no clear connection to the quasinormal modes. These findings contribute to the effort to scrutinize the conditions under which bound states faithfully encode quasinormal spectra and to shed light on the underlying physics of black hole spectral instability.

### [133] [Tidal deformations of general-relativistic multifluid compact stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29726)
*Ethan Carlier,Nicolas Chamel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究建立了任意多流体相互作用致密星的全相对论性绝热潮汐形变理论框架，发现相互夹带（entrainment）在绝热潮汐响应中不产生可观测效应，但为超流体中子星和暗物质混合致密星等应用提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着第三代引力波探测器的发展，潮汐形变参数（tidal deformabilities）的测量精度将大幅提升，可能揭示次要潮汐贡献。这需要发展包含更丰富微观物理的精确致密星模型，超越常用的完美流体近似。

Method: 采用多流体框架（multifluid framework）和Carter的多流体变分形式（Carter's multifluid variational formalism），建立了任意数量相互作用流体组成的致密星的全相对论性绝热潮汐形变描述。该方法包含流体组分间的非耗散相互夹带（nondissipative mutual entrainment）。

Result: 推导了多流体构型的流体静力学平衡方程（hydrostatic equilibrium equations）以及控制任意阶稳态引力电型和引力磁型潮汐响应的扰动方程。使用多流体状态方程（multifluid equation of state）的解析表示，证明相互夹带不改变绝热潮汐响应，因此在内部模式共振激发前的旋近阶段对引力波信号无可观测效应。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为超流体中子星（superfluid neutron stars）和暗物质混合致密星（dark matter admixed compact stars）等具体应用提供了基础，表明在绝热潮汐形变背景下相互夹带效应不可观测，但为更复杂的多流体系统建模提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Over the past decade, gravitational-wave astronomy has opened a new window onto the extreme states of matter inside compact stars. At some point during the inspiral of a binary system, each star starts to experience adiabatic tides, characterized by tidal deformabilities. The dominant tidal deformability, first measured with the GW170817 event, has already constrained the dense-matter equation of state. With the advent of third-generation detectors, tidal deformabilities are expected to be inferred with much higher precision, potentially revealing subleading tidal contributions. This motivates the development of more accurate compact-star models that incorporate richer microphysics. With this in mind, we move beyond the commonly adopted perfect-fluid approximation and model compact stars through a multifluid framework. In this work, we present the fully general-relativistic description of adiabatic tidal deformations of compact stars composed of an arbitrary number of interacting fluids, using Carter's multifluid variational formalism. A distinctive feature of this approach is the presence of nondissipative mutual entrainment between fluid species. We derive the hydrostatic equilibrium equations for multifluid configurations, along with the perturbed equations governing stationary gravitoelectric and gravitomagnetic tidal responses of arbitrary order. We then investigate how entrainment modifies the corresponding tidal deformabilities. Using an analytical representation of the multifluid equation of state, we show that entrainment leaves adiabatic tidal responses unchanged and therefore produces no measurable effect on the gravitational-wave signal emitted during the inspiral long before the excitation of internal mode resonances. We subsequently discuss two specific applications: superfluid neutron stars and dark matter admixed compact stars.

</details>


### [134] [Beyond Expectation Values: Generalized Semiclassical Expansions for Matrix Elements of Gauge Coherent States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29826)
*Haida Li,Hongguang Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究推导了规范理论中非多项式算符非对角相干态矩阵元的渐近展开式，结合了驻相分析和算子级泰勒余项处理，为圈量子引力中的体积和通量相关算符提供了显式的半经典误差控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在推导允许全纯相干态表示的规范理论中非多项式算符的非对角相干态矩阵元的渐近展开式，以提供半经典误差控制，并特别应用于圈量子引力（Loop Quantum Gravity）中的几何算符。

Method: 方法结合了驻相分析（stationary-phase analysis）与算子级的泰勒余项处理，围绕真正的非对角Berezin符号而非对角期望值组织展开，保留了几何相位的完整全纯结构。

Result: 推导出的展开式在测试的数值范围内能准确再现基准矩阵元，特别是在相干态标签（coherent-state labels）充分分离时，与arXiv:gr-qc/0607101中提出的标准对角展开相比具有优势。

Conclusion: 该方法为圈量子引力中的体积和通量相关算符提供了有效的渐近展开，通过保留几何相位的全纯结构，在相干态标签分离时能更准确地再现矩阵元。

Abstract: We derive an asymptotic expansion for off-diagonal coherent-state matrix elements of non-polynomial operators in gauge theories admitting holomorphic coherent-state representations. The derivation combines stationary-phase analysis with an operator-level treatment of the Taylor remainder, and yields explicit semiclassical error control under stated assumptions. As a primary application, we formulate the expansion for volume and flux related operators in Loop Quantum Gravity and compare it with the standard diagonal expansion proposed in arXiv:gr-qc/0607101. By organizing the expansion around the genuine off-diagonal Berezin symbol rather than a diagonal expectation value, the resulting formula preserves the full holomorphic structure of the geometric phase and reproduces benchmark matrix elements accurately in the numerical regimes tested here, particularly when the coherent-state labels are well separated.

### [135] [QTAM: QTransform Amplitude Modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29785)
*Lorenzo Asprea,Francesco Sarandrea,Alessio Romano,Jacob Lange,Federica Legger,Sara Vallero*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出Q变换幅度调制（QTAM），一种完全可逆的常数Q变换实现方法，旨在解决引力波观测中信号去噪和重叠瞬态事件分离问题，通过幅度调制技术实现无损数据压缩和低延迟处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时频分析面临基本困境：临界采样变换计算高效但缺乏时移不变性，影响模式识别和深度学习应用；过完备变换虽具时移不变性但数据冗余度高，不适用于低延迟处理。现有方法在引力波啁啾信号和仪器干扰同时表示方面存在不足。

Method: QTAM采用受幅度调制无线电广播启发的方法，将Q变换输出建模为由确定性高频项承载的缓慢变化复包络，通过频谱搬移到基带实现无损数据抽取。该方法保持线性且完全可逆，利用原生GPU加速实现低延迟处理。

Result: QTAM能够以机器精度精确重建原始信号，同时保留密集时频谱图的时移不变性。该方法使时频处理管道能在O(1秒)的低延迟范围内运行，并在引力波数据和信号注入上验证了去噪和分离潜力。

Conclusion: QTAM通过创新的幅度调制方法，在计算效率、时移不变性和信号重建精度之间实现了平衡，为当前和下一代引力波观测台的信号处理提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: We present Q-Transform Amplitude Modulation (QTAM), a novel, fully invertible implementation of the Constant-Q Transform algorithm, designed to enable robust signal denoising and the disentanglement of overlapping transient events in current and next generation gravitational wave (GW) observatories. Time-frequency (TF) analysis faces a fundamental dichotomy: critically sampled transforms are computationally efficient but lack time-shift invariance, limiting their efficacy for robust pattern recognition and Deep Learning applications. While alternative approaches such as the Dual-Tree Complex Wavelet Transform provide efficient approximate shift-invariance, their wavelet constructions remain tied to dyadic scale frequency tilings that are poorly matched to the simultaneous representation of GW chirps and instrumental glitches. Conversely, overcomplete transforms provide the necessary shift-invariance and tunable frequency resolution, but their implementations generate highly redundant data volumes that are prohibitive for low-latency (LL) processing. Furthermore, standard attempts to compress these dense representations rely on lossy interpolation, destroying the phase coherence required to reconstruct the signal. QTAM bridges this gap by employing a methodology inspired by Amplitude Modulation radio broadcasting. By modeling the Q-transform output as a slowly varying complex envelope carried by a deterministic high-frequency term, we achieve lossless data decimation via spectral shifting to baseband. We demonstrate that QTAM is linear and fully invertible, allowing exact reconstruction of the original signal with machine precision while retaining the shift-invariance of dense spectrograms. Leveraging native GPU acceleration, QTAM enables TF pipelines to operate within LL O(1s) bounds. We validate the method's potential for denoising and disentanglement on GW data and signal injections.

</details>


### [136] [Exceptional Points in Quasinormal Spectra of Hairy Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22261)
*Lang Cheng,Xiaobo Guo,Yuhan Li,Jun Tao,Peng Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论（Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory）的有毛黑洞（hairy black holes）标量准正规模（quasinormal mode）谱中发现了一个例外点（exceptional point），并证明基于例外点的拟合方案（EP ansatz）比标准方案能更稳健地描述环降（ringdown）信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准正规模（QNM）谱中的例外点（EPs）是非厄米简并（non-Hermitian degeneracies），其特征值和特征函数同时合并。研究旨在探索有毛黑洞标量准正规模谱中例外点的存在及其对环降信号的影响。

Method: 通过扫描参数空间识别爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中有毛黑洞标量准正规模谱中的例外点，并从时域波形（time-domain waveforms）中提取准正规模，研究其对环降信号的物理意义。

Result: 研究发现，包含时间线性项共振贡献的例外点拟合方案（EP ansatz）比基于独立阻尼模式叠加的标准方案能更稳健地描述例外点处的环降信号。该方案更自然地捕捉了与谱合并相关的共振贡献，即使使用标准方案拟合波形，结果仍可能呈现例外点拟合方案的特征。

Conclusion: 例外点拟合方案为描述准正规模谱中例外点附近的环降信号提供了更优越的理论框架，能够更准确地捕捉非厄米简并的物理效应，这对黑洞扰动理论和引力波数据分析具有重要意义。

Abstract: Exceptional points (EPs) in quasinormal mode (QNM) spectra are non-Hermitian degeneracies at which both the eigenvalues and eigenfunctions coalesce. In this paper, we identify an EP in the scalar QNM spectrum of hairy black holes in the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory by scanning the parameter space. We then investigate its implications for ringdown signals by extracting QNMs from time-domain waveforms. Our results show that an EP ansatz, which includes a resonant contribution containing a term linear in time, provides a more robust description of ringdown at the EP than the standard ansatz based on a superposition of independent damped modes. In particular, it captures the resonant contribution associated with spectral coalescence more naturally, and even when the waveform is fitted with the standard ansatz, the resulting fit may still exhibit characteristic features of the EP ansatz.

</details>


### [137] [Bridging Quantum and Semiclassical Volume: A Numerical Study of Coherent State Matrix Elements in Loop Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29839)
*Haida Li,Hongguang Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在圈量子引力（Loop Quantum Gravity）中，体积算符（volume operator）的量子作用对于理解量子动力学至关重要。然而，需要一种能够广泛计算其在规范变（gauge-variant）和规范不变（gauge-invariant）自旋网络态（spin-network states）上量子作用的数值方法。

Method: 本文实现了一种广义数值算法（generalized numerical algorithm），可计算体积算符（volume operator）在广泛类别的自旋网络态（spin-network states）上的量子作用。该算法随后被用于计算体积算符的相干态期望值（coherent state expectation value）和相干态矩阵元（coherent state matrix elements）。

Result: 通过将数值模型结果与近半经典区域（near-semiclassical region）各种场景下的解析结果进行比较，不仅以高精度验证了数值模型，还提供了体积算符完整量子作用如何与其半经典近似（semiclassical approximations）相联系的完整图景。进一步发现，在半经典区域（semiclassical regime），最大本征值趋近于经典多面体体积（classical polyhedral volume）。

Conclusion: 对于不规则几何（irregular geometries），研究还观察到相对体积大小（relative volume magnitudes）在深量子区域（deep quantum regime）可能发生变化。该数值算法为理解圈量子引力中体积算符的量子行为提供了有效工具。

Abstract: In Loop Quantum Gravity, the quantum action of the volume operator is crucial in understanding quantum dynamics. In this work, we implement a generalized numerical algorithm that can compute the quantum action of the volume operator on a broad class of gauge-variant and gauge-invariant spin-network states. This algorithm is later used to calculate the coherent state expectation value and coherent state matrix elements of the volume operator. By comparing the results generated by our numerical model with the analytical results in various scenarios at the near-semiclassical region, not only is our numerical model validated with high accuracy, but it also provides a complete picture of how the full quantum action of the volume operator connects with its semiclassical approximations. We further find that the maximal eigenvalue approaches the classical polyhedral volume in the semiclassical regime. For irregular geometries, we also observe that the relative volume magnitudes can change in the deep quantum regime.

### [139] [Waveform degeneracy of binary systems and Lagrange three-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29991)
*Carlos Jaimel Doctolero,Ian Vega*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究准圆轨道双星系统与拉格朗日三体系统在引力波波形上的简并性（degeneracy），发现两者在0.5PN阶存在质量四极矩简并，且某些情况下波形重叠度可达0.97以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 假设已知双星系统参数，确定能产生相同波形的拉格朗日三体系统参数。研究聚焦于质量四极矩简并（mass quadrupole degeneracy），分析两种偏振模式（plus and cross modes）的简并特性，并计算波形归一化重叠度（normalized overlap）。

Result: 发现质量四极矩简并由两个参数表征，且存在双星系统与线性稳定拉格朗日三体系统具有相同质量四极矩波形直至并合时间（coalescence time）。当双星质量接近对称时，波形与先进LIGO设计功率谱密度的归一化重叠度保持在0.97以上。在0.5PN阶存在唯一简并，但满足该简并的拉格朗日三体系统不稳定。

Conclusion: 准圆轨道双星系统与拉格朗日三体系统在0.5PN阶存在显著的引力波波形简并性，特别是质量四极矩简并。虽然存在线性稳定系统能产生高度相似的波形，但满足0.5PN阶完整简并的系统不稳定，这对引力波天体物理的参数推断具有重要启示。

Abstract: A particular solution to the three-body problem is the circular Lagrange three-body system, where the masses move in circular orbits such that they always constitute an equilateral triangle. Such a system has been found to emit gravitational waves with a waveform similar to that of a binary system. In this work, we study the gravitational waveform degeneracy between quasi-circular binary systems and Lagrange three-body systems up to 0.5PN order. Assuming we know the parameters of a given binary system, we determine the parameters of the Lagrange triple that produces the same waveform as that of the binary. We show that there exists a mass quadrupole degeneracy in both the plus and cross modes, characterized by two parameters. We also find that there are binary systems and linearly stable Lagrange three-body systems that can have the same mass quadrupole waveform up to the coalescence time. In such cases, the normalized overlap of the waveforms with respect to the power spectral density of the advanced LIGO design remains above 0.97 as long as the binary has nearly symmetric masses. Beyond the mass quadrupole, there is a unique degeneracy at the 0.5PN. However, the Lagrange triple that satisfies this degeneracy is unstable.

Method: 通过松弛能量-动量守恒，单模引力引入了一个动态宇宙学项Λ(x)，允许物质与真空之间的半经典能量交换。利用这一机制，作者构造了精确的标量-麦克斯韦-Λ(x)虫洞（Scalar-Maxwell-Λ(x) wormholes）。

Result: 研究表明，只要形状函数b(r)满足特定的几何条件，这些精确时空可以完全由幻象标量场（phantom scalar field）和标准线性麦克斯韦电动力学（standard linear Maxwell electrodynamics）支撑。该方法完全绕过了非线性电动力学。

Conclusion: 单模引力作为一个强大框架，能够用简化且易于理解的经典场来建模非平凡拓扑结构，为虫洞构造提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: In General Relativity, constructing exact traversable wormholes coupled to electromagnetic fields typically requires complex Non-Linear Electrodynamics (NED). We demonstrate that Unimodular Gravity (UG) elegantly resolves this limitation. By relaxing energy-momentum conservation, UG introduces a dynamical cosmological term, $Λ(x)$, enabling a semi-classical energy exchange between matter and the vacuum. Exploiting this mechanism, we construct exact Scalar-Maxwell-$Λ(x)$ wormholes. We show that, provided the shape function $b(r)$ satisfies specific geometric conditions, these exact spacetimes can be fully supported by a phantom scalar field and standard linear Maxwell electrodynamics. This approach entirely bypasses NED, highlighting UG as a powerful framework for modeling non-trivial topologies with simplified, well-understood classical fields.
