### [142] [Optical creation of dark-bright soliton lattices in multicomponent Bose-Einstein condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28876)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发一种广泛可及且实验上可实现的技术，用于在原子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates）中受控创建暗-亮孤子和孤子晶格，以探索这些非线性激发态的特性与动力学。

Method: 该方法基于将凝聚体制备在Λ耦合（Λ-coupled）三能级系统的暗态（dark state）中，通过数值模拟（numerical simulations）研究了该方案创建的孤子动力学行为。

Result: 数值模拟表明，通过该方案创建的单个暗-亮孤子可以在实验可及的时间尺度上存活，即使耦合激光场被关闭。孤子晶格的命运取决于散射长度（scattering lengths）：当散射长度相等时，晶格可在与凝聚体寿命相当的时间尺度上持续存在，尽管存在不稳定模式；当散射长度不等时，晶格结构会在不稳定性出现后被破坏。

Conclusion: 该技术为在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中可控创建和研究暗-亮孤子及孤子晶格提供了有效方法，揭示了散射长度对孤子晶格稳定性的关键影响，为相关非线性动力学研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We present a widely accessible and experimentally realizable technique for the controlled creation of dark-bright solitons and soliton lattices in atomic Bose-Einstein condensates. The method is based on preparing the condensate in a dark state of a $Λ$-coupled three-level system. Numerical simulations reveal that individual dark-bright solitons created through this scheme can survive over experimentally accessible timescales, even when the coupling laser fields are switched off. Meanwhile, the fate of soliton lattices upon the quench of the fields depends on the scattering lengths. When they are all equal, the lattice is found to persist on timescales comparable to the condensate lifetime, even though the analysis of dynamical stability reveals that they possess unstable modes. In this case the resulting destabilization is not found to be detrimental, as it leads to recurrent dynamics. On the other hand, for unequal scattering lengths the lattice structure gets destroyed once the instability sets in.

</details>


### [143] [Dissipation-induced Nonlinear Topological Gear Switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29160)
*Xuzhen Cao,Xiaolin Li,Liang Bai,Zhaoxin Liang,Li-Chen Zhao,Ying Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于耗散诱导的拓扑齿轮切换机制，实现了通过绝热泵浦速度本身来开关量子化孤子输运的新现象，这为非线性拓扑物质在非平衡条件下的动态重构开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统非线性Thouless泵浦（nonlinear Thouless pump）要求时间周期性哈密顿量和静态非线性，且量子化输运与泵浦速度无关。本研究旨在探索一种新型的非线性拓扑现象，其中量子化输运可通过泵浦速度本身进行动态调控。

Method: 研究采用耗散诱导的拓扑齿轮切换机制，通过构建一个有效保守模型（effective conservative model）来捕捉非平衡机制，该模型的非线性随时间非周期变化（nonlinearity varies aperiodically in time）。

Result: 实现了量子化孤子输运（quantized soliton transport）可通过绝热泵浦速度（adiabatic pumping speed）本身进行开关控制。即使系统从线性区域被泵浦到非线性区域，这种非周期非线性驱动也能诱导量子化输运。

Conclusion: 该研究为非线性拓扑物质（nonlinear topological matter）在非平衡条件下的动态重构开辟了新途径，其中拓扑效应可通过随时间变化的非线性进行动态调控，对光子学、原子物理和超导平台等实验系统具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: Nonlinear interaction enables topological phenomena impossible in linear systems. A paradigm is nonlinear Thouless pump, where the transport of solitons can be topologically quantized even when band occupation is nonuniform. Such nonlinear quantization traditionally requires a time-periodic Hamiltonian with static nonlinearity and, much as in the linear case, is inherently independent of pumping speed. Instead, we demonstrate a dissipation-induced topological gear switching, where quantized soliton transport can be switched on and off via the adiabatic pumping speed itself. This phenomenon has no counterpart in prior conservative nonlinear pumps, nor in linear non-Hermitian pumps. Crucially, quantization here no longer requires a time-periodic nonlinear Hamiltonian; it stems from a genuinely non-equilibrium mechanism captured by an effective conservative model whose \textit{nonlinearity varies aperiodically in time}. Remarkably, a quantized nonlinear transport can be induced even when this nonlinear aperiodic driving is such that the system is pumped from the linear to nonlinear regimes. Our results open a route toward nonequilibrium nonlinear topological matter, where topological effect is dynamically reconfigurable via time-varying nonlinearities, with experimental implications for photonic, atomic, or superconducting platforms and beyond.

### [144] [Generation of dipolar supersolids through a barrier sweep in droplet lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29203)
*E. L. Brakensiek,G. A. Bougas,S. I. Mistakidis*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用扩展的Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation）结合量子修正作为理论框架，通过扫描排斥性高斯势垒（repulsive Gaussian barrier）通过非相干准一维液滴阵列（incoherent quasi-one-dimensional droplet array）来诱导超固体形成。

Result: 研究发现，在势垒扫描过程中，系统产生了持久的超流背景（superfluid background），晶体在其上同步振荡，表明相位相干性（phase coherence）的建立。该过程伴随着能量重新分布和较高动量向零动量模式（zero momentum mode）的逐渐转移。

Conclusion: 超固体分数（superfluid fraction）对势垒速度和高度具有依赖性，研究明确了促进超流背景形成的参数区域。这些结果为使用实验可实现的协议工程化生成超固体铺平了道路。

Abstract: We propose a dynamical protocol to generate supersolids in dipolar quantum gases by sweeping a repulsive Gaussian barrier through an incoherent quasi-one-dimensional droplet array. Supersolidity is inferred by monitoring the ensuing dynamics of the density, momentum distribution, center-of-mass motion, and superfluid fraction within the framework of the extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation with quantum corrections. A persistent superfluid background arises, atop which the crystals oscillate in unison, indicating the establishment of phase coherence. This process is accompanied by energy redistribution and the gradual transfer of higher-lying momenta toward the zero momentum mode. The dependence of the superfluid fraction on the barrier velocity and height is also elucidated evincing the parametric regions which facilitate the rise of a superfluid background. Our results pave the way for engineering supersolid generation using experimentally accessible protocols.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 提出的相空间测量协议扩展了量子气体显微镜的功能，为研究量子多体系统提供了新的实验工具，特别是在相空间表征方面具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Quantum gas microscopes offer unprecedented insights into quantum many-body states of cold atomic gases. Here we introduce concrete protocols for extending quantum gas microscopes to measure in phase space, by mapping momentum onto auxiliary degrees of freedom and using positive operator-valued measures. We distinguish between two distinct operational modes. In the Husimi-Q phase space microscope, position and momentum are jointly measured; in this mode the fundamental quantum noise appears in the position measurement. Conversely, the averaged-mode phase space microscope extracts the spatial dependence of averages of the momentum density (and its moments); these averages can be retrieved with arbitrary spatial resolution. We illustrate the utility of these techniques in diverse physical settings.

### [148] [Phase diagram of rotating Bose-Einstein condensates trapped in power-law and hard-wall potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29738)
*G. M. Kavoulakis*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 研究准二维弱相互作用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体在幂律势阱和硬壁势阱中的旋转相图，发现弱相互作用下系统经历多重量子化涡旋态之间的不连续相变，而强相互作用下则出现向混合态的连续相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究不同约束势阱（幂律势阱和硬壁势阱）对旋转玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体相变行为的影响，特别关注约束势类型导致的定性差异和可观测的实验特征。

Method: 通过理论分析准二维弱相互作用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体在旋转条件下的行为，比较其在幂律势阱（power-law traps）和硬壁势阱（hard-wall traps）中的相变特性。

Result: 发现弱相互作用下系统经历多重量子化涡旋态（multiply-quantized vortex states）之间的不连续相变，而强相互作用下则出现向包含单重和多重量子化涡旋态的混合态的连续相变。关键发现是两种约束势阱存在定性差异：硬壁势阱中主导不稳定性总是涉及阱中心密度非零的态，而幂律势阱中密度随旋转频率增加而消失。

Conclusion: 两种不同类型的约束势阱导致相图具有不同的标度特性（scaling properties），这些差异在实验上可观测，为理解旋转玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的相变行为提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate the rotational phase diagram of a quasi-two-dimensional, weakly-interacting Bose-Einstein condensate confined in power-law and in hard-wall trapping potentials. For weak interactions, the system undergoes discontinuous transitions between multiply-quantized vortex states as the rotation frequency of the trap increases. In contrast, stronger interactions induce continuous phase transitions toward mixed states involving both singly and multiply-quantized vortex states. A central result is the qualitative (and experimentally observable) difference between power-law and hard-wall confinement: In hard-wall traps, the leading instability always involves states with nonzero density at the trap center, whereas in power-law traps the density vanishes as the rotation frequency increases. The two different types of confinement give rise to scaling properties in the derived phase diagrams.

### [149] [Separable neighbourhood of identity in C$^{\ast}$-algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29556)
*Mizanur Rahaman,Mateusz Wasilewski*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 该论文研究了二分C*-代数中可分元素的结构，重点关注单位元周围可分邻域的存在性和大小。通过将问题约化为估计收缩正映射的完全有界范数，作者建立了邻域大小与代数结构性质（特别是秩）之间的关系，并解决了Musat和Rørdam的一个猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二分C*-代数（bipartite C*-algebras）中可分元素（separable elements）的结构，特别是单位元周围可分邻域的存在性和大小。虽然在有限维情形下这一现象已有充分理解，但将其推广到一般C*-代数面临额外挑战。

Method: 将确定可分邻域的问题约化为估计收缩正映射（contractive positive maps）的完全有界范数（completely bounded norm）。这种方法允许通过代数的结构性质（特别是其秩）来刻画邻域的大小。

Result: 建立了可分邻域大小与代数结构性质（特别是秩）之间的明确关系。作为推论，解决了Musat和Rørdam最近提出的一个猜想。

Conclusion: 通过将可分邻域问题约化为完全有界范数估计，成功刻画了二分C*-代数中单位元周围可分邻域的结构特性，并解决了相关猜想，为无限维情形下的可分性研究提供了新方法。

Abstract: We study the structure of separable elements in bipartite C$^{\ast}$-algebras, focusing on the existence and size of a separable neighbourhood around the identity element. While this phenomenon is well understood in the finite-dimensional setting, its extension to general C$^{\ast}$-algebras presents additional challenges. We show that the problem of determining such a neighbourhood can be reduced to estimating the completely bounded norm of contractive positive maps. This approach allows us to characterize the size of such neighbourhoods in terms of structural properties of the algebra, notably its rank. As a consequence, we also resolve a recent conjecture of Musat and Rørdam.

### [150] [Dispersive estimates for Schrödinger operators with negative Coulomb-like potentials in one dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29731)
*Akitoshi Hoshiya,Kouichi Taira*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者采用了两步法：首先推导了谱密度（spectral density）的WKB表达式；其次，利用退化驻相公式（degenerate stationary phase formula）的变体来分析低能区（low-energy regime）的振荡行为。这种方法克服了传统微扰论不适用于缓慢衰减势的困难。

Result: 本文成功建立了具有库仑型衰减势的一维薛定谔算子的色散估计。作为应用，作者为该模型同时建立了标准Strichartz估计（standard Strichartz estimates）和正交Strichartz估计（orthonormal Strichartz estimates）。

Conclusion: 本文发展了一种处理缓慢衰减势的新方法，通过WKB近似和退化驻相分析克服了传统微扰论的局限性。所得结果为库仑型势场下的色散估计和Strichartz估计提供了理论基础，扩展了该领域的研究范围。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider the dispersive estimates for Schrödinger operators with Coulomb-like decaying potentials, such as $V(x)=-c|x|^{-μ}$ for $|x|\gg 1$ with $0<μ<2$, in one dimension. As an application, we establish both the standard and orthonormal Strichartz estimates for this model. One of the difficulties here is that perturbation arguments, which are typically applicable to rapidly decaying potentials, are not available. To overcome this, we derive a WKB expression for the spectral density and use a variant of the degenerate stationary phase formula to exploit its oscillatory behavior in the low-energy regime.

### [151] [Maximally heavy dynamics in the causal diamond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28853)
*David Poland,Gordon Rogelberg*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究为无限标度维度（infinite scaling dimension）的CFT算符四点关联函数建立了严格框架，通过定义"最大重可观测量（maximally heavy observables）"来刻画其空间结构，这些可观测量类似于热力学极限下的统计系统内禀量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无限标度维度CFT算符的关联函数是丰富而多面的对象，涵盖经典全息（classical holography）、黑洞动力学（black hole dynamics）和平坦时空散射振幅（flat-space scattering amplitudes）等物理领域。需要建立严格框架来系统刻画这类算符的四点关联函数空间。

Method: 通过定义"最大重可观测量（maximally heavy observables）"来表征相同算符的四点关联函数空间，这些可观测量类似于热力学极限下统计系统的内禀量。该框架受到交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）和幺正性（unitarity）的强约束。

Result: 最大重可观测量通过动力学相变（dynamical phase transitions）的出现为体态（bulk states）的局域性（locality）提供了新见解。在某些情况下，这些结果直接关联到大中心荷（large central charge）下更熟悉的环面配分函数（torus partition functions）图像。

Conclusion: 该框架应用于多个示例，包括广义自由场（generalized free fields）、手征乘积关联子（chiral product correlators）以及平面$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM中的最大巨引力子（maximal giant gravitons），验证了其有效性和适用性。

Abstract: Correlation functions of CFT operators with infinite scaling dimension are rich, multifaceted objects that describe physics ranging across classical holography, black hole dynamics, and flat-space scattering amplitudes. In this work, we provide a rigorous framework for characterizing the space of four-point functions of identical operators with infinite dimension in terms of well-defined ``maximally heavy observables,'' which are akin to intrinsic quantities describing statistical systems in the thermodynamic limit. These observables are highly constrained by crossing symmetry and unitarity, and give novel insights into the locality of bulk states through the emergence of dynamical phase transitions. In certain cases, these results connect directly to the more familiar picture of torus partition functions at large central charge. We apply our framework to a number of illustrative examples including generalized free fields, chiral product correlators, and maximal giant gravitons in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM.

</details>

### [157] [Spontaneous BRST symmetry breaking in infrared QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29401)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 提出了一种低能杨-米尔斯量子场论的有效拉格朗日量新方案，该方案展示了自发BRST对称性破缺，并再现了Curci-Ferrari模型作为特例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了与杨-米尔斯基本场（elementary field）耦合的Fujikawa模型，将Fujikawa场解释为基本胶子（gluon）和鬼场（ghost field）的复合有效场。为确保Fujikawa场中存在两个无质量的Nambu-Goldstone模式，要求有效拉格朗日量不仅具有BRST对称性，还具有反BRST（anti-BRST）对称性，且两者均自发破缺。

Result: 该方案最显著的结果是有效胶子和鬼场质量的出现。通过自发BRST对称性破缺，Curci-Ferrari模型被再现为有效模型的特例。为重现Curci-Ferrari模型特有的非幂零（non-nilpotent）修正BRST对称性，进一步修改有效拉格朗日量使其对扩展BRST（extended-BRST）对称性不变，该对称性混合基本场和Fujikawa场并保持幂零性。

Abstract: We present a novel proposal for the effective Lagrangian of the low-energy Yang--Mills quantum field theory. The proposed effective Lagrangian exhibits the spontaneous BRST symmetry breaking. We built the Fujikawa model that we couple to the Yang--Mills elementary field sector, motivated by the analogy with Chiral Quark Model. We interpret the Fujikawa fields as effective fields composite of the elementary gluon and ghost fields. In order to justify the existence of two massless Nambu--Goldstone modes among the Fujikawa fields, we require not only the BRST but also the anti-BRST invariance of the effective Lagrangian, both to be spontaneously broken. The most striking consequence of that is the emergence of the effective gluon and ghost masses. We reproduce the Curci--Ferrari model as a special case of our effective model upon the spontaneous BRST symmetry breaking. In order to reproduce also the non-nilpotent modified BRST symmetry, characteristic for the Curci--Ferrari model, we modify our effective Lagrangian to be invariant with respect to the extended-BRST symmetry, which mixes the elementary and Fujikawa field sectors, and which is nilpotent. The Curci--Ferrari is reproduced by the elementary field sector of the resulting Lagrangian. The remaining Fujikawa's field dependent terms guarantee the underlying nilpotent extended-BRST symmetry, which is now hidden in the sense of the spontaneous symmetry breaking.

### [158] [Cosmological brick walls & quantum chaotic dynamics of de Sitter horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29443)
*José M. Begines,Suman Das,Hyun-Sik Jeong,Juan F. Pedraza*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将砖墙模型（brick wall model）应用于渐近德西特时空，通过分析纯德西特空间和史瓦西-德西特黑洞中无质量标量场的本征模，研究了视界物理的量子特性。研究发现，纯德西特谱显示出混沌的长程特征，而史瓦西-德西特情况则呈现更丰富的定性行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 计算了纯德西特空间和史瓦西-德西特（Schwarzschild-de Sitter）黑洞中无质量标量场的本征模（normal modes）。使用能级间距分布（level-spacing distribution）、谱形状因子（spectral form factor）和Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）分析得到的单粒子谱。

Result: 纯德西特谱显示出明显的混沌长程特征，尽管不遵循传统的维格纳-戴森（Wigner-Dyson）能级间距分布。史瓦西-德西特情况更丰富：在WKB区域，事件视界和宇宙学视界的存在产生了两个独立的近视界区域，导致全谱是两个子序列的叠加。叠加谱在谱形状因子中仍显示出近似线性斜坡，在Krylov复杂度中呈现显著峰值。

Conclusion: 严格的能级排斥（level repulsion）缺失本身不应被视为混沌不存在的证据。谱形状因子和Krylov复杂度为底层混沌动力学提供了更敏锐的诊断工具，表明这些指标在识别混沌特征方面比传统的能级间距分布更具判别力。

Abstract: Originally proposed by 't Hooft, the brick wall model has recently reemerged as a useful framework for probing quantum aspects of horizon physics, particularly in the context of holography. In this paper, we apply it to asymptotically de Sitter spacetimes. We compute the normal modes of a massless scalar field in pure de Sitter space and in the Schwarzschild-de Sitter black hole, and analyze the resulting single-particle spectra using the level-spacing distribution, the spectral form factor, and Krylov complexity. In pure de Sitter, the spectrum exhibits clear long-range signatures of chaos despite not obeying a conventional Wigner-Dyson level-spacing distribution. The Schwarzschild-de Sitter case is qualitatively richer: in the WKB regime, where tunneling between the two classically allowed regions is exponentially suppressed, the presence of both an event horizon and a cosmological horizon gives rise to two independent near-horizon sectors, so that the full spectrum is the superposition of two subsequences. As a result, the combined level-spacing distribution develops a nonzero value at $s=0$ even when spectral correlations remain. Nevertheless, for sufficiently small stretched-horizon fluctuations, the superposed spectrum still exhibits an approximately linear ramp in the spectral form factor and a pronounced peak in Krylov complexity. Our results show that the absence of strict level repulsion should not, by itself, be taken as evidence against chaos, and that the spectral form factor and Krylov complexity provide sharper diagnostics of the underlying chaotic dynamics.

Starting from exact solutions of the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, we study a conditional density matrix of the system. We find that the ground state is a mixed state, rather than a pure Hartle-Hawking state. Our results are consistent with the semiclassical double-trumpet amplitude, and with recent work on complex geometries containing bra-ket wormholes. We also analyze semiclassical wave functions for metric, dilaton, and an additional inflaton field. The probability distribution for the size of the universe is flat.

</details>


### [161] [Critical dimensions and small cycle dominance from all-orders asymptotics of $d$-matrix theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29610)
*Yang Lei,Sanjaye Ramgoolam*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了$\mathcal{N}=4$超对称杨-米尔斯理论中矩阵模型配分函数$\mathcal{Z}_d(x)$的大$N$渐近展开。发现该展开具有基于置换循环大小的组合结构（小循环主导），并在临界维度$d_{\rm crit}=13$以上收敛。这揭示了配分函数可以从其高能（UV）极限完全重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $\mathcal{N}=4$超对称杨-米尔斯理论（super-Yang-Mills theory）的超对称扇区（supersymmetric sectors）激发了对$d=2,3$矩阵的规范不变函数计数配分函数的研究。该配分函数在大$N$极限下的Hagedorn相变（Hagedorn phase transition）为SYM热配分函数的相结构提供了简单模型。

Method: 基于复平面上极点（poles）在自然边界（natural boundary）处累积的几何图像，研究了$\mathcal{Z}_d(x)$的全阶渐近展开（all-orders asymptotic expansion）。通过分析Dedekind eta函数的模性质（modular property），确定了渐近展开的收敛性。

Result: 发现阶乘结构具有精确的组合解释，由置换（permutations）枚举中循环大小（cycle size）递增组织，称为小循环主导（small-cycle dominance）。渐近展开在$d\ge d_{\rm crit}=13$时收敛，而费米版本（fermionic version）的临界维度为$d_{\rm crit}=7$。

Conclusion: 对于$d\ge d_{\rm crit}$，矩阵模型的配分函数可以从其高能（UV）极限完全重构；而对于$2\le d \le d_{\rm crit}-1$，则需要额外输入来精确重构低能（IR）展开系数。这一区分揭示了配分函数重构的维度依赖性。

Abstract: Supersymmetric sectors of $\mathcal{N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills theory motivate the study of the partition function for the counting of gauge-invariant functions of $d=2,3$ matrices transforming under the adjoint action of $U(N)$. The partition function $ \mathcal{Z}_d ( x) $ in the large $N$ limit has a known Hagedorn phase transition at $ x = d^{-1} $ which provides a simple model for the phase structure of the thermal partition function of SYM. We study the all-orders asymptotic expansion of $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x)$ based on a geometric picture of concentric circles of poles in the complex plane accumulating in a natural boundary at $|x| =1$. We find that the order by order structure has a precise combinatorial interpretation organized in terms of increasing cycle size of permutations arising in the enumeration of the invariants. We refer to this organization as small-cycle dominance, and find that it extends to refined versions of the partition functions depending on several complex variables. An analysis of the coefficients in the asymptotic expansion of $ \mathcal{Z}_d(x) $ using the modular property of the Dedekind eta function reveals that the asymptotic expansion is actually convergent for $d\ge d_{ \rm crit } = 13$. A fermionic version of $\mathcal{Z}_d (x)$ has an analogous critical dimension of $ d_{ \rm crit} = 7$. This distinction indicates that the partition functions of the matrix models can be completely reconstructed from their high-energy (UV) limit for $d\ge d_{ \rm crit}$ whereas additional input is required to reconstruct the exact coefficients of the low-energy (IR) expansion for $2\le d \le d_{ \rm crit } -1 $.

### [162] [5d Higgs branch and instanton magnetization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29679)
*Amihay Hanany,Alessandro Tomasiello,Elias Van den Driessche*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了5维Sp(k)规范理论在弱耦合与强耦合下的希格斯分支（Higgs branch），发现其可由SO(2N_f)纯旋量（pure spinors）描述的一对瞬子（instantons）来刻画。泊松结构（Poisson structure）受对称性约束，表明这些希格斯分支构成代数可积系统（algebraic integrable systems）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究5维Sp(k)规范理论在不同耦合强度下希格斯分支的几何与物理特性，特别是理解其对称性约束的泊松结构如何导致代数可积系统的出现，以及强耦合极限下希格斯分支的分层（stratification）现象。

Method: 采用对称性论证（symmetry arguments）约束泊松结构，分析由SO(2N_f)纯旋量描述的一对瞬子如何刻画希格斯分支。通过考察旋量湮灭算符（spinor annihilators）重叠时辛形式（symplectic form）的退化（degeneration）现象，研究系统的可积性。

Result: 发现希格斯分支构成代数可积系统，其辛形式的退化发生在旋量湮灭算符重叠时。在无限耦合（infinite coupling）下，希格斯分支的分层对应于瞬子权重（instanton weights）的排列（alignment），导致非零磁化（magnetization）并获得质量（mass）。

Conclusion: 5维Sp(k)理论的希格斯分支可由SO(2N_f)纯旋量描述的一对瞬子统一刻画，其泊松结构受对称性约束而构成代数可积系统。强耦合极限下的分层现象源于瞬子权重的排列，这导致磁化与质量生成。

Abstract: Higgs branches of 5d $Sp(k)$ theories with $N_f$ flavours, whether at weak or strong coupling, are described by a pair of instantons transforming as pure spinors of $SO(2N_f)$. The Poisson structure is constrained by symmetry arguments and implies that these Higgs branches are algebraic integrable systems; the degeneration of the symplectic form occurs when the spinor annihilators overlap. We argue that the stratification of the Higgs branch at infinite coupling corresponds to the alignment of the instantons weights, leading to a non vanishing magnetization, and their acquisition of a mass.

### [163] [Warm Warped Throats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29781)
*Dibya Chakraborty,Rudnei O. Ramos*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准膜暴胀场景依赖于单个移动D3膜径向朝向喉道尖端的反D3膜运动。本文旨在探索更丰富的暴胀图景，将径向和角坐标作为独立暴胀子场，并在温暴胀框架下研究其可行性。

Method: 提出两种不同的暴胀图景：在弯曲变形锥面（warped deformed conifold）上，D3膜的径向和角坐标作为两个独立的暴胀子场。通过引入超对称嵌入的D7膜（supersymmetrically embedded D7-brane）实现模稳定化，生成必要的径向和角标量势。在温暴胀范式下评估这些径向和角膜暴胀设置。

Result: 在温暴胀范式下评估这些径向和角膜暴胀设置，证明耗散效应（dissipation effects）使得模型在给定参数空间内比冷暴胀（cold inflation）对应物更自然地满足近期观测约束。

Conclusion: 研究表明，将D3膜的径向和角坐标作为独立暴胀子场，结合D7膜实现模稳定化，并在温暴胀框架下考虑耗散效应，能够为膜暴胀提供更符合观测约束的理论实现方案。

Abstract: We investigate brane inflation, focusing on warm inflation realizations within a warped throat geometry. While the standard scenario relies on a single mobile $D3$-brane moving radially toward an anti-$D3$-brane at the tip of the throat, we propose two distinct inflationary pictures. In our approach, the radial and angular coordinates of a $D3$-brane on a warped deformed conifold act as two independent inflaton fields. We address moduli stabilization by incorporating a supersymmetrically embedded $D7$-brane, which generates the necessary radial and angular scalar potentials. Evaluating these radial and angular brane inflation setups within the warm inflation paradigm, we demonstrate that dissipation effects allow the models to satisfy recent observational constraints more naturally than their cold inflation counterparts for a given parameter space.

### [164] [Exponential Periods for Integrals in Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29787)
*Anthony Massidda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种系统方法，通过将Feynman积分重新表述为指数周期（exponential periods），构建适当的同调与上同调理论，以分析wall crossing结构和Stokes现象，从而精确计算主积分（master integrals）数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交截理论（intersection theory）为Feynman积分分析提供了统一框架，但扭曲de Rham上同调（Twisted de Rham cohomology）在处理具有丰富几何结构（如奇点和复杂单值性）的积分时存在局限。需要发展更一般的理论框架来处理参数表示中的Feynman积分。

Method: 提出系统方法识别和构建适当的同调与上同调理论，将参数表示中的Feynman积分重新解释为指数周期（exponential periods）。结合维度正规化（dimensional regularization）的解析延拓，为分析wall crossing结构和正确考虑Stokes现象提供完整框架。

Result: 该框架不仅能够处理量子场论和弦理论中的微扰积分，还能涵盖从傅里叶计算到统计力学配分函数（statistical mechanics partition functions）、从量子力学期望值到共形场论关联函数（conformal field theory correlators）等广泛物理相关积分。

Conclusion: 通过将Feynman积分重新表述为指数周期并构建适当的同调理论，建立了一个统一形式体系，能够系统分析多圈贡献中的主积分计数问题，同时涵盖广泛的物理积分类型。

Abstract: The study of Feynman integrals through the lens of intersection theory offers a unifying framework for their analysis, capturing both the linear and quadratic relations that arise among integrals. In doing so, it provides a powerful method for systematically reducing them to the so called master integrals, a necessary strategy for multiloop contributions, whose huge number make direct calculation unfeasible. The Twisted de Rham cohomology offers a powerful tool for describing integrals with multivalued integrands, arising in dimensional regularization. However, it fails whenever the underlying geometry shows richer structures, as singularities and intricate monodromies. In this thesis we propose a systematic approach to identify and construct the appropriate homology and cohomology that allows to interpret Feynman integrals in parameter representation as exponential periods. This reformulation, together with the analytic continuation of the dimensional regularizator, provides a perfect framework to properly analyze the wall crossing structure and to correctly take into account Stokes phenomena for a sharp counting of the number of Master integrals. This framework allows to embed within the same formalism not only perturbative integrals, coming both from quantum field theories and string theory, but also wide class of physically relevant integrals, from Fourier calculus to statistical mechanics partition functions, from quantum mechanics expectation values to conformal field theory correlators.

</details>

*Hongliang Jiang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种新颖且内在的方法，直接从VOA恢复麦克斯韦指数的特殊非舒尔极限（special non-Schur limit），该方法无需额外假设且适用于所有幺正（unitary）的4d理论。

Result: 在多种示例中验证了该提议，并将其扩展到含表面缺陷（surface defects）的情形，提出了缺陷存在时的分级幺正性（graded unitarity）概念，同时引入了一类新的VOA级数。

Abstract: The SCFT/VOA correspondence provides a powerful framework for studying 4d $\mathcal N=2$ superconformal field theories (SCFTs) through the mathematical machinery of 2d vertex operator algebras (VOAs). It captures the Schur operators of the underlying SCFT, whose spectrum is encoded by the Schur index and its refinement, the Macdonald index. While the Schur index is identified with the vacuum character of the associated VOA, a general VOA-based derivation of the Macdonald index has remained elusive. In this letter, we propose a novel and intrinsic method for recovering a special non-Schur limit of the Macdonald index directly from the VOA. The construction requires no additional assumptions and applies whenever the underlying 4d theory is unitary. We test the proposal in a variety of examples, and further extend it to the case with surface defects, suggesting a notion of graded unitarity in the presence of defects. Our method also introduces a new class of series for general VOAs, analogous to but distinct from the conventional character, and potentially useful in broader contexts.

### [167] [Microscopic Origin of Page Curve](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29872)
*Artem Averin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用最近证明的广义Ryu-Takayanagi公式，该公式保持与理论哈密顿相空间的联系。在包含具有分叉Killing视界的稳态黑洞的任何微分同胚不变场论中，通过分叉表面上的哈密顿表面荷可区分的相空间态必须提供黑洞Wald熵的自由度。

Result: 证明了在微分同胚不变场论中，通过分叉表面上的哈密顿表面荷可区分的相空间态必须负责黑洞的Wald熵。这是更大研究计划的一部分，其中量子理论的可测量量被表达为相空间路径的加权和。

Conclusion: 该研究计划通过相空间路径求和的新框架，揭示了传统时空解释中可能隐藏的黑洞"毛发"，为解决信息悖论提供了新视角，并展示了引力熵界和广义Ryu-Takayanagi公式等先前结果。

Abstract: Applications of the Ryu-Takayanagi formula to evaporating black holes are known to reproduce the Page curve, although leaving open the microscopic origin of the necessary black hole degrees of freedom responsible for the entanglement and microstates. Here, we fill this gap by utilizing a recently proven generalized Ryu-Takayanagi formula which keeps the contact to the theory's Hamiltonian phase space. Precisely, we show that in any diffeomorphism invariant field theory containing stationary black holes with bifurcate Killing horizons the phase space states distinguishable by their Hamiltonian surface charges over the bifurcation surface must provide the degrees of freedom responsible for the black hole's Wald entropy. This result is part of a larger program where measurable quantities of a quantum theory are expressed as weighted sums over paths in the theory's phase space. Suited reorganization tools for those sums make then physical phenomena evident which might be obscured in a naive summation relying on spacetime notions such as field configuration spaces and Feynman diagrams. Besides presenting this result, we provide here a conceptual overview of the program as an entry point for unfamiliar readers explaining the central notion of the program and why it reveals the results obtained so far. These include especially the gravitational entropy bound and the here applied generalized Ryu-Takayanagi prescription shown earlier within the program. Using the information paradox as a leitmotif, our proposed program uncovers black hole hair that may be hidden within a naive spacetime interpretation.

Abstract: We develop a recursive algebraic framework for solving the closed string tachyon vacuum equation, derived from the hyperbolic recursion relations of Fırat and Valdes-Meller. We restrict to the sector of zero-momentum Lorentz-scalar states. Lorentz symmetry ensures that this sector is closed under the equations of motion. In this sector, we introduce a seam-graded expansion and show that the equation is entirely algebraic at every order: the unknown at each grade enters only through point evaluations at the systolic length, so each grade reduces to a matrix inversion with no Fredholm equations. The expansion is formal; convergence in the multi-level system is the subject of ongoing work. This work was conducted with a publicly available version of Claude Code (Anthropic, Claude Opus 4.6). The complete research repository, including all computations, adversarial review logs, and the full human-AI collaboration history, is publicly available at https://github.com/mk2427/csft-tachyon-vacuum.

### [169] [Holographic Weyl Anomaly and Kounterterms in AdS gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29952)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现，对于任意奇数维度，都能从作用量变分中计算出相当一部分的韦尔反常（Weyl anomaly）。这表明Kounterterms方法能够有效提取共形反常的全息信息。

Conclusion: Kounterterms方法不仅为渐近AdS空间提供有限作用量，还能有效提取共形反常的全息信息，特别是在奇数维度下能够计算出韦尔反常的显著部分，展示了该方法在全息研究中的实用价值。

Abstract: The addition of Kounterterms to Einstein gravity leads to a finite action for asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) spaces with a conformally flat boundary. On the other hand, this method has the clear advantage that the variation of the action has a closed form in an arbitrary dimension.
  In this work, it is shown how to extract holographic information on conformal anomalies from the variation in $(2n+1)$-dimensional Einstein-AdS plus Kounterterms. Remarkably enough, a considerable part of the Weyl anomaly can be worked out for any odd dimension.

### [170] [Permeation behaviour of hydrogen isotopes in molten FLiBe (2LiF-BeF2): Identifying sources of uncertainty and associated measurement challenges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28991)
*Abhishek Saraswat,Weiyue Zhou,Nayoung Kim,Jaron F. Cota,Guiqiu Zheng,Alexander A. Khechfe,Caroline S. Barthel,Michael P. Short,Rémi Delaporte-Mathurin,Kevin B. Woller*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过HYPERION实验设施系统量化了FLiBe中氢同位素在773K-973K温度范围内的渗透率，揭示了先前研究中广泛分散的传输参数源于未经验证的假设，并发现盐侧充氢方法能有效解决渗透屏障问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前关于FLiBe中氢同位素传输的研究报告了广泛分散的传输参数，存在知识空白。本研究旨在通过系统实验量化氢同位素在FLiBe中的渗透率，并探究先前研究中未经验证的假设。

Method: 在HYPERION实验设施中，通过特定设计来验证先前研究中未经验证的假设，包括一维渗透、盐覆盖膜表面以及盐-金属界面的理想润湿性。研究比较了金属侧充氢和盐侧充氢两种方法。

Result: 实验发现金属侧充氢会抑制同位素传输行为，揭示了气泡负载的Ni-FLiBe界面的渗透屏障特性，使渗透率降低高达77%。盐侧充氢方法为解决这一问题提供了途径，并为未来研究的渗透充氢方法提供了约束条件。

Conclusion: HYPERION实验的初步见解对先前研究中的设计选择和估计的传输特性提出了质疑。本研究为观察到的FLiBe中H/D/T传输的分散性提供了合理解释，并强调了渗透充氢方法选择的重要性。

Abstract: This paper presents results from systematic investigations conducted in the HYPERION facility to quantify permeabilities of hydrogen isotopes in FLiBe over a temperature range of 773K - 973K. To address the knowledge gap resulting from widely scattered transport parameters reported in the earlier studies, HYPERION experiments incorporate specific provisions to probe unsubstantiated assumptions, including a one-dimensional permeation, membrane surface coverage by the salt, and ideal wettability of the salt-metal interface. Suppression of the isotopic transport behaviour for metal-side charging highlights the permeation barrier characteristics of a bubble-laden Ni-FLiBe interface, impacting permeability by up to 77%. This work attempts to resolve this issue via salt-side charging and informs constraints on the permeant charging methodology for future studies. The initial insights from HYPERION experiments call into question the design choices and estimated transport properties in earlier works. This study provides a plausible explanation for the observed scatter in H/D/T transport in FLiBe.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Driven by the MagNet Challenge 2025 (MC2), increased research interest is directed towards modeling transient magnetic fields within ferrite material. Within the scope of this investigation, a selection of model structures with varying degrees of physically motivated structure are compared. Based on a Pareto investigation, a rather black-box gated recurrent unit (GRU) model structure with a graceful initialization setup is found to offer the most attractive model size vs. model accuracy trade-off, while the physics-inspired models performed worse. For a GRU-based model with only 325 parameters, a sequence relative error of 8.02 % and a normalized energy relative error of 1.07 % averaged across five different materials are achieved on unseen test data. With this excellent parameter efficiency, the proposed model won the first place in the performance category of the MC2.

### [172] [A Floer Theoretic Approach to Energy Eigenstates on one Dimensional Configuration Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29201)
*Kevin Ruck*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 该论文从辛拓扑（symplectic topology）视角重新审视量子力学中的两个经典问题："环上粒子（particle on a ring）"和"盒中粒子（particle in a box）"。通过将薛定谔方程的解解释为适当选择的含时哈密顿系统（time dependent Hamiltonian system）中的轨道，并利用Floer理论进行分析，扩展了Rabinowitz Floer同调（Rabinowitz Floer homology）的定义，证明了模空间紧致性，从而为广泛外部势能下的能量本征态存在性提供了证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在从辛拓扑的视角重新审视量子力学中的两个经典问题："环上粒子"和"盒中粒子"。通过将量子力学问题转化为辛几何框架，可以利用现代辛拓扑工具（特别是Floer理论）来研究这些系统的本征态存在性问题。

Method: 方法包括将时间无关薛定谔方程（time independent Schrödinger equation）的解解释为适当选择的含时哈密顿系统中的轨道。核心技术创新是扩展Rabinowitz Floer同调的定义，使其适用于标准辛结构（standard symplectic structure）下ℝ²ⁿ上的非自治哈密顿量（non-autonomous Hamiltonians），并证明J-全纯曲线模空间（moduli space of J-holomorphic curves）的紧致性仍然成立。

Result: 通过建立的同调理论，能够证明在广泛外部势能（exterior potentials）范围内，"环"或"盒"中能量E本征态（energy E eigenstates）的存在性结果。这为量子力学经典问题提供了基于辛拓扑框架的新证明途径。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将量子力学经典问题纳入辛拓扑框架，通过扩展Rabinowitz Floer同调理论并证明相关紧致性，为"环上粒子"和"盒中粒子"系统的本征态存在性提供了新的数学证明方法，展示了辛拓扑工具在量子力学问题分析中的应用潜力。

Abstract: In this article we consider two classical problems in Quantum Mechanics, namely the 'particle on a ring' and the 'particle in a box' from the viewpoint of symplectic topology. Interpreting the solutions of the corresponding time independent Schrödinger equation as orbits in a suitably chosen time dependent Hamiltonian system allows us to investigate them using Floer theory. More precisely we extend the definition of Rabinowitz Floer homology to non-autonomous Hamiltonians on $\mathbb{R}^{2n}$ with its standard symplectic structure and show that compactness of the moduli space of J-holomorphic curves still holds. With this homology we are then able to prove existence results for energy $E$ eigenstates on the 'ring' or in the 'box' for a big range of exterior potentials.

</details>

### [173] [Comment on "Lattice QCD constraints on the critical point from an improved precision equation of state"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29279)
*Roy A. Lacey*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该论文对近期一篇使用格点QCD（lattice QCD）计算和熵密度等值线分析来约束QCD临界点（critical endpoint）位置的研究提出了方法论上的批评，指出其方法并非直接探测临界行为，因此所得的下界约束不能被视为模型无关的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期一篇研究使用格点QCD的状态方程计算结合熵密度等值线分析，对QCD临界点（CEP）的位置给出了下界约束。本文旨在分析该方法在推断CEP约束方面的局限性，强调其并非直接敏感于临界行为。

Method: 通过分析该研究所采用的方法论，指出其熵密度等值线分析存在三个主要问题：不直接探测与CEP相关的奇异结构、未明确纳入相关的热力学标度场、以及依赖在有限系统中不能严格满足的假设。

Result: 分析表明，该方法不能提供模型无关的约束，因为它缺乏对临界现象相关的奇异标度行为的直接敏感性。因此，所报告的排除μ_B ≈ 450 MeV以下CEP的结论不能被视为模型无关的。

Conclusion: 基于熵密度等值线分析来约束QCD临界点位置的方法存在根本性局限，无法提供模型无关的约束。要获得可靠的CEP约束，需要采用对临界奇异标度行为直接敏感的观测量。

Abstract: A recent Letter~\cite{Borsanyi:2025dyp} employs lattice QCD calculations of the equation of state, combined with entropy-density contour analysis, to place a lower bound of $μ_B \gtrsim 450$~MeV on the location of the QCD critical endpoint (CEP). While the underlying lattice calculations represent an important advance in precision and systematic control, the method used to infer constraints on the CEP is not directly sensitive to critical behavior. In particular, the use of entropy contours does not directly probe the singular structure associated with the CEP, does not explicitly incorporate the relevant thermodynamic scaling fields, and relies on assumptions that are not strictly satisfied in finite systems. Consequently, the reported exclusion of a CEP below $μ_B \approx 450$~MeV cannot be regarded as model-independent, as model-independent constraints require observables that are directly sensitive to the singular scaling behavior associated with critical phenomena.

</details>


### [174] [Imprint of the adjoint meson spectrum in the decay patterns of hidden-bottom tetraquarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29581)
*Sipaz Sharma,Juan Andrés Urrea-Niño,Nora Brambilla,Francesco Knechtli,Michael Peardon*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究通过Born-Oppenheimer有效场论（BOEFT）和格点QCD计算，解释了实验观测到的隐藏底四夸克态Z_b(10610)和Z_b(10650)的近简并性及其衰变模式差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在澄清实验观测到的同位旋I=1隐藏底四夸克态Z_b(10610)和Z_b(10650)的近简并性及其衰变模式差异，特别是Z_b'到B\bar{B^*}衰变的压低现象。

Method: 采用Born-Oppenheimer有效场论（BOEFT）框架，将Z_b和Z_b'分解为Z_1和Z_2四夸克构型的叠加；同时使用格点QCD计算伴随介子关联函数。

Result: 发现Z_b'到B\bar{B^*}衰变的压低可在BOEFT框架下得到解释；通过格点QCD计算获得良好迹象表明与Z_1和Z_2四夸克相关的伴随介子（分别为1^{--}和0^{-+}）是简并的。

Conclusion: Z_b和Z_b'的衰变模式差异可通过其作为Z_1和Z_2四夸克构型叠加的分解来理解，而这两种构型对应的轻自由度（伴随介子）的简并性解释了观测到的近简并现象。

Abstract: We aim to clarify the experimentally observed near-degeneracy and decay patterns of the isospin, $I=1$, hidden-bottom tetraquarks $Z_b(10610)$ and $Z_b(10650)$ with quantum numbers $J^{P}=1^{+}$.We refer to them as $Z_b$ and $Z_b^{'}$, respectively. In particular, we find first evidence that the suppression of the decay of $Z_b^{'}$ to $B\bar{B^*}$ can be understood in the context of the Born-Oppenheimer Effective Field Theory (BOEFT). BOEFT enables writing both $Z_b$ and $Z_b^{'}$ as superpositions of $Z_1$ and $Z_2$ tetraquark configurations. This decomposition naturally relates the decay patterns of $Z_b$ and $Z_b^{'}$ to the degeneracy of the light degrees of freedom associated with $Z_1$ and $Z_2$ tetraquarks, {\it i.e.,} $1^{--}$and $0^{-+}$ adjoint mesons, respectively. By calculating the adjoint meson correlators within the framework of lattice QCD, we get good indications that these adjoint mesons are degenerate.

### [175] [Towards a formalism for $ππ$ scattering from staggered lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28967)
*A. Dean. M. Valois,M. Dai,A. El-Khadra,E. Gámiz,S. Lahert,R. Merino*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文探讨了从交错夸克（staggered quarks）格点QCD（lattice QCD）数据中提取ππ散射振幅的两种互补方法，以应对因第四根号化（fourth-rooting）和味劈裂（taste splitting）导致的幺正性破坏（unitarity violation）等挑战，并聚焦于同位旋-2通道的ππ散射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 使用交错费米子（staggered fermions）的格点QCD模拟会因第四根号化（fourth-rooting）产生$\mathcal{O}(a^2)$的幺正性破坏（unitarity violation）晶格人工效应。此外，该理论的介子部分包含多个非质量简并的π介子（味劈裂，taste splitting），这些效应限制了Lüscher形式体系（Lüscher formalism）在非零晶格间距下对交错格点数据的适用性。

Method: 本文讨论了两种互补方法：1）首次使用相应的有效理论——根号交错手征微扰理论（Rooted Staggered Chiral Perturbation Theory）计算单圈振幅，以显式检验量子化条件（quantization condition）的有效性。2）将形式体系推广，以纳入味劈裂（taste splitting）和第四根号化（fourth-rooting）效应。

Result: 研究聚焦于同位旋-2通道（isospin-2 channel）的ππ散射这一较简单情况，并讨论了其他通道的应用前景。通过这两种方法，旨在克服从交错夸克格点QCD数据中提取散射振幅时面临的挑战。

Conclusion: 本文提出的两种互补方法为解决从交错夸克格点QCD模拟中提取ππ散射振幅的难题提供了途径，特别是通过扩展Lüscher形式体系以处理味劈裂和第四根号化效应，并利用有效理论进行验证。

Abstract: Scattering processes featuring the strong interactions can be studied using lattice QCD by means of the Lüscher formalism. This approach relies on analyticity and unitarity of the $S$-matrix to relate infinite-volume scattering amplitudes to finite-volume energy levels. However, lattice QCD simulations employing rooted staggered fermions manifest unitarity violation as an $\mathcal{O}(a^2)$ lattice artifact. Moreover, the meson sector of this theory contains multiple non-mass-degenerate pions (due to the so-called taste splitting), which only reduce to the physical pion in the continuum limit. These features restrict the applicability of the Lüscher formalism to staggered lattice data at non-zero lattice spacing. Hence, in this work, we discuss two complementary approaches to deal with the challenges of extracting $ππ$ scattering amplitudes from lattice QCD with staggered quarks: (1) using the corresponding effective theory, Rooted Staggered Chiral Perturbation Theory, to calculate one-loop amplitudes for the first time. These amplitudes can be used to explicitly check the validity of the quantization condition. And (2) generalizing the formalism to incorporate taste-splitting as well as fourth-rooting effects. We focus on the simpler case of $ππ$ scattering in the isospin-2 channel, and discuss prospects for other channels.

</details>


### [176] [The axion-photon coupling from lattice Quantum Chromodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29153)
*Bastian B. Brandt,Gergely Endrődi,José Javier Hernández Hernández,Gergely Markó,Laurin Pannullo*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文首次通过连续外推的格点模拟（continuum extrapolated lattice simulations）非微扰地确定了量子色动力学（QCD）对轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）的贡献，并利用这一第一性原理结果更新了对轴子模型（axion models）的实验约束分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子（axion）作为超越标准模型（Standard Model）的暗物质（dark matter）候选粒子，其实验探测依赖于轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）。该耦合不仅依赖于具体轴子模型，还受到量子色动力学（QCD）的显著贡献，而此前缺乏对这一QCD贡献的非微扰（non-perturbative）精确计算。

Method: 采用两种独立方法，基于连续外推的格点模拟（continuum extrapolated lattice simulations）非微扰地确定QCD真空对时间反演（time reversal）奇异的背景电磁场组合的响应，从而计算QCD对轴子-光子耦合的贡献。

Result: 首次获得QCD贡献的第一性原理结果：$g_{Aγγ}^{\rm QCD} f_A/e^2=-0.0224(10)$（以轴子尺度$f_A$和基本电荷$e$为单位）。这一精确计算为理解轴子-光子耦合提供了关键的模型无关（model-independent）贡献。

Conclusion: 基于这一第一性原理（first-principles）结果，研究提出了对轴子模型（axion models）实验约束的新颖更新，为当前和未来的观测策略提供了理论指导，有助于更精确地探索暗物质候选粒子。

Abstract: Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) is the theory of the strong interactions within the Standard Model of particle physics, which explains more than 99% of the mass of the visible Universe. However, there is evidence that a substantial portion of our Universe is made up of particles beyond the Standard Model, i.e. dark matter. A popular dark matter candidate is the axion -- a hypothetical particle that also solves the so-called strong CP-problem, the unexpected symmetry of QCD under time reversal. The experimental detection of axions hinges on their conversion rate to photons, controlled by the axion-photon coupling. This coupling depends on the specific axion model, but also receives a sizable model-independent contribution from QCD. Here we present the first non-perturbative determination of the QCD contribution using continuum extrapolated lattice simulations. The calculation is based on determining the response of the QCD vacuum to time reversal-odd combinations of background electromagnetic fields. We develop two independent methods exploiting different features of this response and obtain $g_{Aγγ}^{\rm QCD} f_A/e^2=-0.0224(10)$ in units of the axion scale $f_A$ and the elementary charge $e$. Armed with this first-principles result, we present a novel update on how experimental observations can be used to constrain the landscape of axion models, useful for guiding contemporary and future observational strategies.

</details>


### [177] [Lattice Field Theory Analysis of the Chiral Heisenberg Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29461)
*Simon Hands,Johann Ostmeyer*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究通过晶格场论方法构建三维手性海森堡模型，使用畴壁费米子模拟石墨烯和π-通量晶格中哈伯德模型的半金属-莫特绝缘体相变，获得了自发对称性破缺临界指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于对石墨烯和π-通量晶格中哈伯德模型半金属-莫特绝缘体相变普适行为的持续关注，旨在通过构建三维手性海森堡模型来理解这一相变现象。

Method: 采用畴壁费米子构建三维手性海森堡模型的晶格场论，接触相互作用项保持SU(2)全局对称性。使用有理混合蒙特卡洛算法在系统尺寸L³×L_s（L∈{8,...,24}，畴壁分离L_s∈{8,16,24}）上进行数值模拟。

Result: 定位了自发SU(2)→U(1)对称性破缺的相变，获得临界指数估计值ν⁻¹=0.63(3)，η_Φ=1.42(8)。这些值与(2+1)D模拟结果差异显著，但与三维协变场论解析估计更接近。首次展示了费米子关联函数结果，为确定指数η_Ψ奠定基础。

Conclusion: 三维手性海森堡模型的数值模拟结果支持三维协变场论的解析预测，与(2+1)D模拟存在显著差异，强调了处理时空维度对称性的重要性。费米子关联函数的初步结果为完整临界指数确定提供了方向。

Abstract: Motivated by ongoing interest in the universal behaviour of the Hubbard model of spinning electrons on honeycomb and $π$-flux lattices at the semi-metal -- Mott insulator phase transition, we formulate the \threeD~chiral Heisenberg model, a theory of relativistic fermions in three spacetime dimensions, as a lattice field theory using domain wall fermions. The contact interaction term preserves an SU(2) global symmetry. We perform numerical simulations using the Rational Hybrid Monte Carlo algorithm on system sizes $L^3\times L_s$ with $L\in\{8,\ldots,24\}$ and domain wall separation $L_s\in\{8,16,24\}$. We locate the phase transition corresponding to spontaneous SU(2)$\to$U(1) breaking, yielding critical exponent estimates $ν^{-1}=0.63(3)$, $η_Φ=1.42(8)$. These values are considerably removed from estimates obtained from simulations performed in (2+1)D, ie. with the time and spatial directions treated differently, but align more closely with analytic estimates obtained using 3D covariant field theory. We also present first results for the fermion correlator, ultimately needed for the determination of the exponent $η_Ψ$, highlighting the need to rotate the fermion source to a common reference direction in isospace in order to obtain a signal.

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [178] [Quantum Coherence and Giant Enhancement of Positron Channeling Radiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28827)
*Michael Shatnev*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子力学计算，考虑了不同横向能级间跃迁振幅的干涉效应，发现正电子在金刚石(110)面沟道辐射中因相干态形成而产生显著增强效应，强度比非相干模型提高12-31倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究正电子在晶体沟道中的辐射机制，特别是量子相干效应对辐射强度的影响。传统非相干模型（Zhevago-Kumakhov）无法解释实验观测到的辐射峰值位置，需要建立包含量子干涉效应的理论框架。

Method: 采用量子力学方法计算正电子在平面谐波势中的沟道辐射，明确考虑不同横向能级间跃迁振幅的干涉。利用突然近似（sudden approximation）描述正电子进入晶体过程，形成Glauber相干态，并分析相位同步机制对辐射振幅的贡献。

Result: 计算显示相干辐射强度$I_{\rm coh} \propto |A_j|^2$，比非相干结果增强12-31倍（对应正电子能量4-14 GeV）。数值结果与Avakyan等人的实验峰值位置一致，且该增强效应为正电子特有，因为电子的沟道势不呈现类似谐波特性。

Conclusion: 量子相干性驱动辐射强度从$N$标度向$N^2$标度转变，为核物理和材料科学领域的高强度单色伽马射线源开辟了新途径。研究提出了基于预测峰值强度非线性角度依赖性的决定性实验验证方案。

Abstract: We present a quantum-mechanical calculation of positron channeling radiation in a planar harmonic potential, explicitly accounting for the interference between transition amplitudes from different transverse energy levels. Because the planar channel potential for positrons in diamond~(110) is well approximated by a parabola, the transverse spectrum is equidistant, $\varepsilon_n = Ω(n+\tfrac{1}{2})$, and all $n \to n{-}j$ transitions radiate at the same Doppler-shifted frequency. The entry of the positron into the crystal under the sudden approximation creates a Glauber coherent state with population amplitudes $c_n$. Phase synchronization between the $c_n$ and the dipole matrix elements ensures that all occupied levels contribute constructively to the radiation amplitude, giving an intensity $I_{\rm coh} \propto |A_j|^2$ that exceeds the incoherent (Zhevago--Kumakhov) result by a factor $\mathcal{G} = 12\text{--}31$ for positron energies of $4\text{--}14$~GeV in diamond~(110). Numerical results agree with the experimental peak positions of Avakyan \emph{et al.}~\cite{Avakyan1982}. The enhancement is unique to positrons because their nearly harmonic channel potential is not replicated for electrons. We propose a decisive experimental test of the coherent model based on the predicted nonlinear angular dependence of the peak intensity. The transition from $N$- to $N^2$-scaling of the radiated intensity, driven by quantum coherence, opens a route toward high-intensity monochromatic gamma-ray sources for nuclear physics and materials science.

</details>


### [179] [Quantum Approximate Optimization of Integer Graph Problems and Surpassing Semidefinite Programming for Max-k-Cut](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.05956)
*Anuj Apte,Sami Boulebnane,Yuwei Jin,Sivaprasad Omanakuttan,Michael A. Perlin,Ruslan Shaydulin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用量子近似优化算法（QAOA）处理图上的整数优化问题，每个整数变量编码为qudit。推导了深度-p QAOA期望值在高围长d-正则图上的通用迭代公式，该公式计算成本与QAOA深度p呈指数关系但与图规模无关。针对Max-k-Cut问题评估了p≤4时的公式，并引入了基于饱和度（degree-of-saturation）的新启发式算法作为经典基线。

Result: 在k=3且度d≤10以及k=4且d≤40的参数范围内，QAOA表现优于Frieze-Jerrum半定规划（SDP）算法。新提出的基于饱和度的启发式算法在经验上优于Frieze-Jerrum算法和浅层QAOA，但数值证据表明QAOA可能在深度p≤20时超越该启发式算法。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，从二元优化扩展到整数优化问题可以为量子优势开辟新途径。虽然当前提出的经典启发式算法表现优异，但深度QAOA显示出超越经典方法的潜力，特别是在整数优化领域。

Abstract: Quantum algorithms for binary optimization problems have been the subject of extensive study. However, the application of quantum algorithms to integer optimization problems remains comparatively unexplored. In this paper, we study the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) applied to integer problems on graphs, with each integer variable encoded in a qudit. We derive a general iterative formula for depth-$p$ QAOA expectation on high-girth $d$-regular graphs of arbitrary size. The cost of evaluating the formula is exponential in the QAOA depth $p$ but does not depend on the graph size. Evaluating this formula for Max-$k$-Cut problem for $p\leq 4$, we identify parameter regimes ($k=3$ with degree $d \leq 10$ and $k=4$ with $d \leq 40$) in which QAOA outperforms the Frieze-Jerrum semi-definite programming (SDP) algorithm, which provides the best worst-case guarantee on the approximation ratio. To strengthen the classical baseline we introduce a new heuristic algorithm, based on the degree-of-saturation, that empirically outperforms both the Frieze-Jerrum algorithm and shallow-depth QAOA. Nevertheless, we provide numerical evidence that QAOA may overtake this heuristic at depth $p\leq 20$. Our results show that moving beyond binary to integer optimization problems can open up new avenues for quantum advantage.

Abstract: We present exact, closed-form results for the non-stabilizerness of random pure states subject to a U(1) symmetry constraint. We show that the presence of a conserved charge leads to a substantial suppression of non-stabilizerness (magic) compared to the unconstrained case, and identify a qualitative difference between entanglement and magic response. In the thermodynamic limit, stabilizer entropy exhibits a different leading-order scaling close to a vanishing relative charge density, implying that magic is more robust to charge density fluctuations than entanglement entropy. Abstract: We introduce a numerical tensor-network method to compute the statistics of the charge transferred across an interface partitioning an interacting one-dimensional many-body lattice system with $U(1)$ symmetry. Our approach is based on a matrix-product state representation of the process tensor (also known as influence functional or influence matrix) describing the effect of the bulk system on the degrees of freedom at the interface, allowing us to evaluate a multi-time correlation function that yields the moment-generating function of charge transfer. We develop a scheme to truncate non-Markovian correlations which preserves the proper normalization of the process tensor and ensures the correct physical properties of the generating function. In particular, we confirm the breakdown of Kardar-Parisi-Zhang universality in higher-order transport cumulants at the isotropic point. Motivation: 基于超导-半导体混合约瑟夫森结（hybrid superconductor-semiconductor Josephson junctions）的门控量子比特（gatemons）虽然具有栅极可调性（gate tunability），但其弛豫时间（relaxation times）远低于最先进的量子比特，且这种差异的起源尚未完全理解。

Method: 采用共制造（co-fabricate）方法，在同一芯片上制造门控量子比特和SIS结量子比特（SIS-junction transmons），确保除约瑟夫森结（Josephson element）外，电路布局（circuit layouts）、栅极电介质（gate dielectrics）和控制线路（control lines）均完全相同。利用SIS结量子比特作为片上参考（on-chip references），构建包含Purcell衰减（Purcell decay）、控制线自发辐射（spontaneous emission）和内部介电损耗（internal dielectric loss）的损耗预算（loss budget）。

Result: 在多个芯片上，SIS结量子比特的弛豫时间达到数十微秒（tens of microseconds），而门控量子比特仅停留在几微秒范围（few-microsecond range）。损耗预算分析显示，对应T1极限值（T1 limits）超过所有测量到的门控量子比特值一个数量级以上。温度依赖性T1测量遵循共同的准粒子激活模型（quasiparticle-activation model），并显示S-Sm-S和SIS结具有相似超导能隙（superconducting gaps）。

Conclusion: 门控量子比特相干性（coherence）的降低主要受额外的、温度无关的（temperature-independent）、结本征的（junction-intrinsic）耗散机制主导，而非准粒子（quasiparticle）相关效应。

Abstract: Superconducting transmon qubits based on hybrid superconductor-semiconductor Josephson junctions (gatemons) offer gate tunability, but their relaxation times remain well below those of state-of-the-art transmons, and the origin of this discrepancy is not fully understood. Here, we co-fabricate gatemons and SIS-junction transmons with nominally identical circuit layouts, gate dielectrics, and control lines, so that the Josephson element is the only intentional distinction. Across multiple chips, transmons in this architecture reach relaxation times in the tens of microseconds, whereas gatemons saturate in the few-microsecond range. Using the transmons as on-chip references, we construct a loss budget including Purcell decay, spontaneous emission through the control line, and internal dielectric loss, and find that the corresponding T1 limits exceed all measured gatemon values by more than an order of magnitude. Temperature-dependent T1 measurements follow a common quasiparticle-activation model and yield similar superconducting gaps for S-Sm-S and SIS junctions, indicating that the reduced gatemon coherence is dominated by additional temperature-independent, junction-intrinsic dissipation.

</details>


### [187] [Non-Equilibrium Sock Dynamics: Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking in the Agitated Wash](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29650)
*Ahmad Darwish,Matteo Murdaca,Jami J. Kinnunen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种袜子动力学的准粒子理论，将袜子建模为受扰动洗衣凝聚物的玻色子激发，解释了袜子不成对、缩水及降解为线头的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于一个普遍经验观察：袜子在洗涤过程中会变得不成对。该现象缺乏系统的理论解释，需要建立物理模型来理解袜子动力学的基本机制。

Method: 采用准粒子理论（quasiparticle theory）方法，将单个袜子建模为受扰动洗衣凝聚物（agitated laundry condensate）的玻色子激发（bosonic excitations）。通过分析袜子色散关系（dispersion relation）的凸凹区域，分别解释贝利亚耶夫衰变（Beliaev decay）和朗道-哈拉特尼科夫散射（Landau-Khalatnikov scattering）过程。

Result: 研究结果表明：非色散材料保持形状，而色散材料导致袜子缩水现象。在色散谱凸区域，袜子经历贝利亚耶夫衰变自发分裂为两个低动量袜子；在凹区域，朗道-哈拉特尼科夫散射主导袜子降解为线头和松散线头。旋转滚筒通过动态卡西米尔效应（dynamical Casimir effect）从洗衣真空中产生袜子-反袜子对。

Conclusion: 这些产生和破坏通道的共存导致了一个根本性模糊：洗涤周期结束时的不成对袜子，既可能是其配对袜子被破坏的结果，也可能是全新袜子自发产生的结果。该理论为袜子不成对现象提供了系统的物理解释框架。

Abstract: It is a universal empirical observation that socks become unpaired in the laundry. We propose a quasiparticle theory of sock dynamics in which individual socks are modelled as bosonic excitations of the agitated laundry condensate. The sock dispersion relation is material-dependent: nondispersive materials retain their shape, while dispersive materials give rise to the well-documented phenomenon of sock shrinkage. In the convex regions of the dispersive spectrum, socks undergo Beliaev decay and spontaneously split into two lower-momentum socks, while in the concave regions the dominant process is Landau-Khalatnikov scattering, which degrades socks into lint and loose threads. In addition, the rotating drum creates sock-antisock pairs from the laundry vacuum via the dynamical Casimir effect. The coexistence of these creation and destruction channels gives rise to a fundamental ambiguity: an unpaired sock at the end of a wash cycle is equally consistent with the destruction of its partner or the spontaneous creation of an entirely new sock.

</details>

### [188] [AMShortcut: An Inference- and Training-Efficient Inverse Design Model for Amorphous Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29812)
*Yan Lin,Jonas A. Finkler,Tao Du,Jilin Hu,Morten M. Smedskjaer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出AMShortcut，一种用于非晶材料（amorphous materials）逆向设计的推理和训练高效的生成模型，能够在少量采样步骤下准确推断多样的短程和中程结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶材料缺乏长程原子有序性但具有复杂的短程和中程有序结构，其逆向设计需要能够根据期望性质生成原子位置和元素。现有方法存在推理效率低和需要为每种性质组合单独训练模型的问题。

Method: 提出AMShortcut模型，这是一种推理和训练高效的生成模型。该模型只需少量采样步骤即可准确推断非晶材料的多样结构，且能够通过一次训练处理所有相关性质，并基于任意期望性质组合进行条件推理。

Result: 在三个具有不同结构和性质的非晶材料数据集上的实验表明，AMShortcut实现了其设计目标，能够高效地进行条件推理并生成符合期望性质的非晶材料结构。

Conclusion: AMShortcut作为一种高效的生成模型，能够促进非晶材料在能源存储和热管理等领域的应用，通过减少采样步骤和训练需求解决了现有方法的效率瓶颈。

Abstract: Amorphous materials are solids that lack long-range atomic order but possess complex short- and medium-range order. Unlike crystalline materials that can be described by unit cells containing few up to hundreds of atoms, amorphous materials require larger simulation cells with at least hundreds or often thousands of atoms. Inverse design of amorphous materials with probabilistic generative models aims to generate the atomic positions and elements of amorphous materials given a set of desired properties. It has emerged as a promising approach for facilitating the application of amorphous materials in domains such as energy storage and thermal management. In this paper, we introduce AMShortcut, an inference- and training-efficient probabilistic generative model for amorphous materials. AMShortcut enables accurate inference of diverse short- and medium-range structures in amorphous materials with only a few sampling steps, mitigating the need for an excessive number of sampling steps that hinders inference efficiency. AMShortcut can be trained once with all relevant properties and perform inference conditioned on arbitrary combinations of desired properties, mitigating the need for training one model for each combination. Experiments on three amorphous materials datasets with diverse structures and properties demonstrate that AMShortcut achieves its design goals.

</details>

### [189] [Generalizable Foundation Models for Calorimetry via Mixtures-of-Experts and Parameter Efficient Fine Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28804)
*Carlos Cardona-Giraldo,Cristiano Fanelli,James Giroux,Cole Granger,Benjamin Nachman,Gerald Sabin*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于下一代标记（next-token）Transformer架构的通用化量热计基础模型，通过混合专家（Mixture-of-Experts）预训练和参数高效微调策略，实现了跨材料、粒子种类和探测器配置的模块化适应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代粒子物理实验面临高保真探测器模拟的日益增长需求，随着亮度提升和计算需求接近可用资源极限，传统蒙特卡洛模拟方法面临挑战。深度生成模型作为传统模拟的替代方案展现出潜力，特别是借鉴大型语言模型和下一代标记预测范式的最新进展。

Method: 研究采用基于下一代标记Transformer架构的基础模型，结合混合专家预训练和参数高效微调策略。预训练主干网络学习生成跨多种吸收材料的电磁簇射，新材料通过添加和调整轻量级专家模块融入。新粒子类型的扩展通过参数高效微调和模块化词汇表实现，保持基础模型的完整性。

Result: 该方法实现了可控的、可加性模型扩展而不会发生灾难性遗忘，支持高效、增量的知识整合。研究还证明，在已建立的大型语言模型优化程序下，下一代标记量热计模型在计算效率上与标准生成方法具有竞争力。

Conclusion: 下一代标记架构为可扩展的、具有物理感知能力的量热计基础模型和未来高能物理实验提供了可行路径，能够满足现实探测器开发工作流程中对新模拟数据集高效整合的关键需求。

Abstract: Modern particle physics experiments face an increasing demand for high-fidelity detector simulation as luminosities rise and computational requirements approach the limits of available resources. Deep generative models have emerged as promising surrogates for traditional Monte Carlo simulation, with recent advances drawing inspiration from large language models (LLM) and next-token prediction paradigms. In this work, we introduce a generalizable foundation model for calorimetry built on next-token transformer backbones, designed to support modular adaptation across materials, particle species, and detector configurations. Our approach combines Mixture-of-Experts pre-training with parameter-efficient fine-tuning strategies to enable controlled, additive model expansion without catastrophic forgetting. A pre-trained backbone is trained to generate electromagnetic showers across multiple absorber materials, while new materials are incorporated through the addition and tuning of lightweight expert modules. Extensions to new particle types are achieved via parameter-efficient fine-tuning and modular vocabularies, preserving the integrity of the base model. This design enables efficient, incremental knowledge integration as new simulation datasets become available, a critical requirement in realistic detector-development workflows. In addition, we demonstrate that next-token calorimeter models are computationally competitive with standard generative approaches under established LLM optimization procedures. These results establish next-token architectures as a viable path toward extensible, physics-aware foundation models for calorimetry and future high-energy physics experiments.

### [190] [Effects of Cosmic Muons on $μ$eV-to-meV Scale Axion Dark Matter Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28832)
*Dan Zhang,Gray Rybka,Edward J. Daw,Robyn Evren*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙μ子在磁场中的同步辐射可能成为轴子暗物质（axion dark matter）搜索实验的背景噪声，特别是在μeV到meV能量尺度上，需要对此进行定量评估。

Method: 利用GEANT4软件包模拟μ子在8T螺线管磁场圆柱区域内的轨迹，并开发了角频率微分同步辐射功率谱（angular-frequency-differential synchrotron radiation power spectra）的解析估计方法，以覆盖宽范围的洛伦兹因子γ和俯仰角α。

Result: 验证了宇宙μ子不是当前μeV尺度轴子暗物质实验的主要噪声背景，这归因于高Q因子和精细的能量分辨率；但未来宽带轴子暗物质实验若缺乏足够能量分辨率，将易受这些带电粒子同步辐射的影响。

Conclusion: 当前高分辨率轴子搜索实验不受宇宙μ子同步辐射的显著干扰，但未来宽带实验需要改进能量分辨率以避免此类背景噪声。

Abstract: We estimate the synchrotron radiation of cosmic muons in a uniform magnetic field in the $μ$eV-to-meV energy scale. Such events can potentially bring backgrounds to the axion dark matter searches. The GEANT4 software package is utilized to simulate the muon tracks in a cylindrical region of interest with an 8~T solenoid magnetic field applied. We further develop an analytical estimation of the angular-frequency-differential synchrotron radiation power spectra in this work as the cosmic muons span a wide range of Lorentz factor $γ$ and pitch angle $α$. We verify that the cosmic muons are not the dominant noise background for the current axion dark matter experiments on the $μ$eV scale because of the high quality factor $Q$ and fine energy resolution in the readout. However, without sufficient energy resolution in the detector readout, future broadband axion dark matter experiments will be vulnerable to the synchrotron radiation of these charged particles.

### [191] [Machine Learning-Based Cluster Classification to Suppress Background in a Prototype RPC Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28835)
*Souvik Chattopadhay,Zubayer Ahammed*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于机器学习的方法，用于区分低电阻率胶木电阻板室（RPC）中的信号与背景簇射，通过15个簇级描述符训练分类器，有效抑制了二次命中（secondary hits）对探测器性能的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低电阻率胶木电阻板室（low-resistive bakelite RPC）原型常出现二次命中（secondary hits）现象，表现为时间关联谱中的长尾或额外峰。这些背景命中在高计数率环境中难以与真实信号区分，显著降低了径迹重建效率并增加了处理时间。

Method: 研究采用基于机器学习的策略，使用15个簇级描述符（cluster-level descriptors）编码时间和ADC分布的统计特性（直方图均值、宽度、簇大小）和拟合参数（高斯拟合均值、宽度、振幅、chi^2、NDF）。利用三闪烁体主触发（three-scintillator master trigger）的单间隙低电阻RPC实验室数据，在平衡的信号/背景样本上训练和评估了三种分类器：DNN、1D-CNN和XGBoost。

Result: 所有模型均表现出强大的区分能力，其中XGBoost显示出最稳健的泛化性能。特征重要性分析（feature-importance analysis）表明，簇大小（cluster size）和时间形状描述符（temporal-shape descriptors）是主要的区分因素。

Conclusion: 紧凑、可解释的簇级特征与机器学习分类器相结合，为抑制自触发低电阻RPC探测器中的背景提供了一种实用且有效的方法。

Abstract: Resistive Plate Chambers (RPCs) are widely used as tracking detectors in many high-energy physics experiments. It has been observed that low-resistive bakelite RPC prototypes frequently exhibit a secondary hit component, appearing as a long tail or an additional peak in the time-correlation spectra relative to the trigger detector. These secondary hits, which affect both the time and spatial resolution, are difficult to distinguish from genuine signals in high-rate environments without an external trigger. As a result, they can significantly degrade track reconstruction efficiency and increase processing time. We present a machine-learning-based strategy to separate signal and background hit clusters using fifteen cluster-level descriptors that encode both statistical properties (histogram mean, width, cluster size) and fit-based parameters (Gaussian-fit mean, width, amplitude, chi^2, NDF) of the time and ADC distributions. Using laboratory data collected from a single-gap low resistive RPC with a three-scintillator master trigger, we trained and evaluated three classifiers-DNN, 1D-CNN, and XGBoost-on balanced signal/background samples. All models demonstrate strong discrimination capability, with XGBoost showing the most robust generalization performance. Feature-importance analysis indicates that cluster size and temporal-shape descriptors are the dominant discriminants. These results highlight that compact, interpretable cluster-level features combined with machine-learning classifiers offer a practical and effective approach to suppress background in self-triggering low resistive RPC detectors.

Abstract: Liquid scintillators underpin a wide range of radiation detectors, including those used in neutrino physics, but typically rely on organic fluors dissolved in hazardous and costly solvents. This yield is sufficient to detect low-energy protons in water Cherenkov neutrino detectors, expanding their programs in both particle physics and astrophysics. These results establish an accessible, low-cost and environmentally benign route to scintillator development, opening new opportunities for large-scale radiation detection.

### [194] [Hydrogen-helium immiscibility boundary in planets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28927)
*Xiaoyu Wang,Sebastien Hamel,Bingqing Cheng*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 该研究通过机器学习势能驱动的大规模分子动力学模拟，确定了氢-氦（H/He）不混溶边界，发现其温度比先前模拟低约2000K，并表明氦雨在土星中可能发生而在木星中不太可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢-氦（H/He）不混溶边界的位置控制着巨行星中氦雨（helium rain）是否发生及其发生位置，但由于高压实验的挑战性以及从头算（ab initio）模拟在系统尺寸和模拟时间上的限制，该边界仍存在不确定性。

Method: 通过机器学习势能（machine learning potentials）驱动的大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，计算了成分依赖的化学势（chemical potentials），这些势能基于三种密度泛函近似（PBE、vdW-DF和杂化HSE）进行训练。

Result: 三种泛函给出了一致的不混溶边界，在100-1000 GPa压力范围内，相分离温度比先前使用小系统尺寸的从头算模拟低约2000K；将H/He混合自由能拟合到Redlich-Kister规则溶液模型（regular solution model）解释了相分离的热力学驱动力。

Conclusion: 与当前行星内部剖面比较表明，氦雨在土星中可能发生，但在较温暖的木星内部不太可能；该研究缩小了H/He不混溶边界的不确定性，为耦合相分离、热传输和成分梯度的巨行星模型提供了输入参数。

Abstract: The location of the hydrogen-helium (H/He) immiscibility boundary controls whether and where helium rain occurs in giant planets, yet it remains uncertain because high-pressure experiments are challenging and ab initio simulations are limited in system size and simulation time. We map this boundary by computing composition-dependent chemical potentials from large-scale molecular dynamics driven by machine learning potentials trained on three density functional approximations (PBE, vdW-DF, and the hybrid HSE). The three functionals yield consistent immiscibility boundaries, and the demixing temperatures are typically ~2000 K lower than previous ab initio simulations using small system sizes across the pressure range of 100-1000 GPa. Fitting the H/He mixing free energy to a Redlich-Kister regular solution model rationalizes the thermodynamic driving force for phase separation and provides a predictive representation of the boundary. Comparison with current planetary interior profiles indicates that helium rain is plausible in Saturn but unlikely in the warmer interior of Jupiter. Our results narrow the uncertainty in the H/He immiscibility boundary and provide inputs for planetary models that couple demixing, heat transport, and composition gradients in gas giants.

</details>


<div id='math.PR'></div>

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [195] [Uniqueness of the infinite cluster for monotone percolation models without insertion tolerance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29420)
*Christoforos Panagiotis,Alexandre Stauffer*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一类依赖站点渗流模型，证明了当底层粒子配置来自插入容忍测度且雪崩产生连通集时，超临界相几乎必然包含唯一无限簇。结果适用于阿贝尔沙堆、激活随机游走和引导渗流等模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一类通过单调自动机作用于随机初始粒子配置得到的依赖站点渗流模型。这些模型中的诱导渗流测度通常不满足有限能量或插入容忍等标准条件，因此经典的Burton-Keane论证不适用。

Method: 将单调自动机应用于从随机递增测度族中抽取的随机初始粒子配置，构建依赖站点渗流模型。分析底层粒子配置的插入容忍性和雪崩动力学产生的连通集特性。

Result: 证明了当底层粒子配置来自插入容忍测度且雪崩产生连通集时，超临界相几乎必然包含唯一无限簇。该结果适用于阿贝尔沙堆、激活随机游走和引导渗流等多个交互粒子系统。

Conclusion: 研究解决了Fey、Meester和Redig关于阿贝尔沙堆中倾倒顶点渗流的问题，为不满足传统条件的依赖渗流模型提供了统一的唯一无限簇存在性证明框架。

Abstract: We consider a broad class of dependent site-percolation models on $\mathbb{Z}^d$ obtained by applying a monotone automaton to a random initial particle configuration drawn from a stochastically increasing family of measures. We prove that whenever the underlying particle configuration is sampled from an insertion-tolerant measure and the avalanches generated by the dynamics produce connected sets, the supercritical phase almost surely contains a unique infinite cluster. Our result applies to several well-studied interacting particle systems, including the Abelian sandpile, activated random walk, and bootstrap percolation. In these models, the induced percolation measure typically does not satisfy standard conditions such as finite energy or insertion tolerance, so the classical Burton-Keane argument does not apply. As an application, we answer a question of Fey, Meester, and Redig concerning percolation of the toppled vertices in the Abelian sandpile with i.i.d. initial configuration.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.IM'></div>

# astro-ph.IM [[Back]](#toc)

### [196] [Reducing the Virgo site infrastructure noise in preparation of the O4 observing run](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28960)
*Irene Fiori,Federico Paoletti,Roberto Passaquieti,Maria Concetta Tringali,Lorenzo Pierini,Francesca Bucci,Massimo Lenti,Alessandro Longo*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文研究了Virgo引力波干涉仪实验大厅HVAC系统产生的低频噪声（低于100Hz），识别了关键噪声源和传输路径，并实施了针对性缓解措施，为未来引力波天文台的低噪声环境设计提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Virgo引力波干涉仪实验大厅的HVAC系统产生低于100Hz的低频噪声，包括地震、声学和电磁来源的干扰。这些噪声在干涉仪运行历史中多次影响其灵敏度，特别是在第三次观测运行期间影响尤为显著。

Method: 在准备第四次观测运行期间，进行了全面调查以识别基础设施中最关键的噪声源，并追踪它们进入实验区域的传输路径。本文介绍了噪声表征活动的方法论，以及针对性缓解措施的设计、实施和评估。

Result: 研究识别了HVAC系统中最关键的噪声源及其传输路径，并成功实施了针对性的技术解决方案。同时开发了操作最佳实践，有效降低了实验区域的噪声干扰。

Conclusion: 所采用的技术解决方案和开发的操作最佳实践，为未来引力波天文台（gravitational-wave observatories）的低噪声环境设计提供了有价值的指导。

Abstract: The heating, ventilation and air conditioning systems serving the experimental halls of the Virgo gravitational wave interferometer generate low-frequency noise - namely below 100 Hz - of seismic, acoustic, and electromagnetic origin. Such disturbances have repeatedly affected the interferometer sensitivity throughout its operational history, with particularly notable impacts during the third observing run. In preparation for the fourth run, a comprehensive investigation was carried out to identify the most critical noise sources within this infrastructure and to trace their transmission paths into the experimental areas. This manuscript presents the methodology and results of the noise characterization campaign, together with the design, implementation and assessment of targeted mitigation measures. The technical solutions adopted, along with the operational best practices developed, provide valuable guidance for the design of low-noise environments in future gravitational-wave observatories.

</details>
